* 1190: glory
* **Associated Articles:** 1015: God (ID: `1015@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1190: glory (ID: `1190@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 1015: God (id: 1015)

The Creator and Redeemer of the world, who reveals himself in Scripture and in Jesus Christ, and who is loved, worshipped and adored by believers. Scripture stresses the personal nature of God, and also his total reliability and trustworthiness. God is the Father of Jesus Christ and of all believers.

* **Associated Articles:** 1020: God, all-knowing (ID: `1020@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1025: God, anger of (ID: `1025@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1030: God, compassion of (ID: `1030@DictionaryBibleThemes`); ## 1020: God, all-knowing (id: 1020)

The omniscience of God is that attribute by which he knows all things past, present and future. What is hidden from human sight is still known by God. Scripture stresses the wisdom of God in all his actions, and often grounds this in his all\-embracing knowledge.

God's unique self\-knowledge within the Trinity
-----------------------------------------------

**[MAT 11:27](https://ref.ly/Matt11:27)** *See also* [JHN 10:15](https://ref.ly/John10:15); [1CO 2:10–2:11](https://ref.ly/1Cor2:10-1Cor2:11)

The nature of God's knowledge
-----------------------------

### God's knowledge originates within himself

**[ISA 40:13–40:14](https://ref.ly/Isa40:13-Isa40:14)** *See also* [JOB 21:22](https://ref.ly/Job21:22); [ROM 11:33–11:34](https://ref.ly/Rom11:33-Rom11:34); [1CO 2:16](https://ref.ly/1Cor2:16)

### God's knowledge is complete

**[MAT 10:30](https://ref.ly/Matt10:30)** parallel [LUK 12:7](https://ref.ly/Luke12:7) *See also* [PSA 147:4](https://ref.ly/Ps147:4); [ISA 40:26](https://ref.ly/Isa40:26)

### God knows things that are hidden from human understanding

**[DEU 29:29](https://ref.ly/Deut29:29)** *See also* [JOB 37:15–37:16](https://ref.ly/Job37:15-Job37:16); [DAN 2:22](https://ref.ly/Dan2:22); [MAT 24:36](https://ref.ly/Matt24:36) parallel [MRK 13:32](https://ref.ly/Mark13:32); [ACT 1:7](https://ref.ly/Acts1:7); [2CO 12:2–12:4](https://ref.ly/2Cor12:2-2Cor12:4)

God's comprehensive knowledge of people
---------------------------------------

### God's knowledge of people's actions

**[JOB 34:21](https://ref.ly/Job34:21)** *See also* [JOB 24:23](https://ref.ly/Job24:23), [JOB 31:4](https://ref.ly/Job31:4); [PSA 33:13–33:15](https://ref.ly/Ps33:13-Ps33:15), [PSA 139:2–139:3](https://ref.ly/Ps139:2-Ps139:3); [JER 23:24](https://ref.ly/Jer23:24)

### God's knowledge of people's needs

**[MAT 6:8](https://ref.ly/Matt6:8)** *See also* [MAT 6:31–6:32](https://ref.ly/Matt6:31-Matt6:32) parallel [LUK 12:29–12:30](https://ref.ly/Luke12:29-Luke12:30)

### God's knowledge of people's hearts and minds

**[1CH 28:9](https://ref.ly/1Chr28:9)** *Scripture views the heart not primarily as the seat of emotion but more particularly as the seat of the will.* *See also* [PSA 44:20–44:21](https://ref.ly/Ps44:20-Ps44:21), [PSA 139:1–139:2](https://ref.ly/Ps139:1-Ps139:2); [JER 17:10](https://ref.ly/Jer17:10); [EZK 11:5](https://ref.ly/Ezek11:5); [HEB 4:12–4:13](https://ref.ly/Heb4:12-Heb4:13)

### God's knowledge of individuals

[GEN 20:1–20:7](https://ref.ly/Gen20:1-Gen20:7) *God's knowledge of Abimelech's motives and behaviour towards Abraham's wife Sarah*; ; [1SA 16:1–16:12](https://ref.ly/1Sam16:1-1Sam16:12) *the LORD to Samuel regarding David's anointing as king*; ; [ACT 5:1–5:10](https://ref.ly/Acts5:1-Acts5:10) *God's knowledge of the deception of Ananias and Sapphira*

### God's knowledge of people's sin

**[JER 16:17](https://ref.ly/Jer16:17)** *See also* [JOB 10:14](https://ref.ly/Job10:14); [PSA 69:5](https://ref.ly/Ps69:5); [JER 2:22](https://ref.ly/Jer2:22); [HOS 7:2](https://ref.ly/Hos7:2); [AMO 5:12](https://ref.ly/Amos5:12)

God's foreknowledge
-------------------

**[ISA 46:10](https://ref.ly/Isa46:10)** *See also* [ISA 42:9](https://ref.ly/Isa42:9), [ISA 44:7](https://ref.ly/Isa44:7); [DAN 2:28](https://ref.ly/Dan2:28)

### God's foreknowledge of Jesus Christ's passion

**[ACT 2:23](https://ref.ly/Acts2:23)** *See also* [ACT 3:18](https://ref.ly/Acts3:18), [ACT 4:27–4:28](https://ref.ly/Acts4:27-Acts4:28)

### God's foreknowledge of those who would become disciples

**[ROM 8:29](https://ref.ly/Rom8:29)** *See also* [JER 1:5](https://ref.ly/Jer1:5); [ROM 11:2](https://ref.ly/Rom11:2); [1PE 1:2](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:2)

### God's foreknowledge of people's free actions

**[PSA 139:4](https://ref.ly/Ps139:4)** *See also* [EXO 3:19](https://ref.ly/Exod3:19); [DEU 31:21](https://ref.ly/Deut31:21); [1SA 23:10–23:13](https://ref.ly/1Sam23:10-1Sam23:13)

Implications of God's knowledge
-------------------------------

### God's knowledge ensures that all will be judged fairly

**[HEB 4:13](https://ref.ly/Heb4:13)** *See also* [1SA 2:3](https://ref.ly/1Sam2:3); [JOB 34:22–34:23](https://ref.ly/Job34:22-Job34:23); [ECC 12:14](https://ref.ly/Eccl12:14); [ROM 2:16](https://ref.ly/Rom2:16); [1CO 4:5](https://ref.ly/1Cor4:5)

### God's knowledge ensures that he knows those who are his

**[2TI 2:19](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:19)** *See also* [NUM 16:5](https://ref.ly/Num16:5); [EXO 33:12](https://ref.ly/Exod33:12); [JOB 23:10](https://ref.ly/Job23:10)**[JHN 10:14](https://ref.ly/John10:14)** *See also* [1CO 8:3](https://ref.ly/1Cor8:3); [GAL 4:9](https://ref.ly/Gal4:9); [1JN 3:19–3:20](https://ref.ly/1John3:19-1John3:20); [REV 3:8](https://ref.ly/Rev3:8)

## 1025: God, anger of (id: 1025)

The punitive and vindicatory reaction, legitimate and controlled, yet awesomely emphatic, of God the righteous judge to unrighteousness in his human creatures. Up to the present, the expression of God's anger and wrath has had the purpose of drawing sinners to repentance and conversion, but this will not be the case at the final judgment.

The nature of God's anger
-------------------------

### It is fearsome

**[NAM 1:6](https://ref.ly/Nah1:6)** *See also* [JOS 7:26](https://ref.ly/Josh7:26); [EZK 38:18](https://ref.ly/Ezek38:18)

### It is reluctant and short\-lived

**[EXO 34:6](https://ref.ly/Exod34:6)** *See also* [ISA 54:7–54:8](https://ref.ly/Isa54:7-Isa54:8); [NEH 9:16–9:18](https://ref.ly/Neh9:16-Neh9:18)

### It is consistant with his righteous and merciful character

**[PSA 7:11](https://ref.ly/Ps7:11)** *See also* [HAB 3:2](https://ref.ly/Hab3:2)

### It fulfils God's purposes

**[JER 23:20](https://ref.ly/Jer23:20)** *See also* [JER 30:24](https://ref.ly/Jer30:24)

The causes of God's anger
-------------------------

### Idolatry and unbelief

**[NUM 25:3](https://ref.ly/Num25:3)** *See also* [EXO 32:8–32:10](https://ref.ly/Exod32:8-Exod32:10); [DEU 8:19](https://ref.ly/Deut8:19); [JDG 2:10–2:14](https://ref.ly/Judg2:10-Judg2:14); [1KI 14:9](https://ref.ly/1Kgs14:9), [1KI 16:32–16:33](https://ref.ly/1Kgs16:32-1Kgs16:33), [1KI 22:53](https://ref.ly/1Kgs22:53); [2KI 23:19](https://ref.ly/2Kgs23:19) *Josiah removes idolatrous shrines*; [2CH 28:25](https://ref.ly/2Chr28:25), [2CH 34:25](https://ref.ly/2Chr34:25); [JER 8:19](https://ref.ly/Jer8:19), [JER 32:29](https://ref.ly/Jer32:29), [JER 44:3](https://ref.ly/Jer44:3); [JHN 3:36](https://ref.ly/John3:36) *the unbelief of rejecting the Son of God*; [ROM 1:18–1:23](https://ref.ly/Rom1:18-Rom1:23), [ROM 2:8](https://ref.ly/Rom2:8)

### Disobedience and disloyalty

**[JOS 7:1](https://ref.ly/Josh7:1)** *See also* [DEU 9:7](https://ref.ly/Deut9:7); [2KI 22:13](https://ref.ly/2Kgs22:13); [1CH 13:10](https://ref.ly/1Chr13:10); [PSA 106:29](https://ref.ly/Ps106:29); [JER 32:32](https://ref.ly/Jer32:32); [ZEC 7:13](https://ref.ly/Zech7:13); [EPH 5:6](https://ref.ly/Eph5:6)

### Ungodly living

God's judgment against the ungodly is a sign of his anger against actions that contradict his righteous character and purposes: [2TI 3:1–3:9](https://ref.ly/2Tim3:1-2Tim3:9); ; [JUD 1:14–1:16](https://ref.ly/Jude1:14-Jude1:16)

### Pride, arrogance and hypocrisy

**[MAT 23:27–23:28](https://ref.ly/Matt23:27-Matt23:28)** *See also* [2CH 32:25](https://ref.ly/2Chr32:25); [PRO 3:34](https://ref.ly/Prov3:34), [PRO 8:13](https://ref.ly/Prov8:13); [ISA 13:11](https://ref.ly/Isa13:11); [HOS 12:14](https://ref.ly/Hos12:14); [MAL 4:1](https://ref.ly/Mal4:1)

### Complaints against, and opposition to, God's purposes

**[NUM 11:1](https://ref.ly/Num11:1)** *See also* [NUM 14:27](https://ref.ly/Num14:27), [NUM 21:5](https://ref.ly/Num21:5)

### Injustice

**[ZEC 7:9–7:12](https://ref.ly/Zech7:9-Zech7:12)** *See also* [2CH 19:7](https://ref.ly/2Chr19:7); [JER 22:13](https://ref.ly/Jer22:13); [EZK 9:9](https://ref.ly/Ezek9:9); [MAL 3:5](https://ref.ly/Mal3:5); [MAT 23:23](https://ref.ly/Matt23:23)

### The rejection of God's servants

**[HEB 10:29–10:31](https://ref.ly/Heb10:29-Heb10:31)** *See also* [DEU 32:35–32:36](https://ref.ly/Deut32:35-Deut32:36); [PSA 135:14](https://ref.ly/Ps135:14); [NEH 9:26](https://ref.ly/Neh9:26); [ZEC 7:12](https://ref.ly/Zech7:12); [MAT 21:33–21:41](https://ref.ly/Matt21:33-Matt21:41); [ACT 7:35–7:37](https://ref.ly/Acts7:35-Acts7:37)

God reveals his anger
---------------------

### In present times

**[ROM 1:18](https://ref.ly/Rom1:18)** *See also* [JER 10:10](https://ref.ly/Jer10:10)

### On a future \`\`day of wrath'' which is anticipated

**[ROM 2:5](https://ref.ly/Rom2:5)** *See also* [ISA 13:9](https://ref.ly/Isa13:9), [ISA 13:13](https://ref.ly/Isa13:13); [EZK 7:19](https://ref.ly/Ezek7:19); [ZEP 1:15](https://ref.ly/Zeph1:15), [ZEP 1:18](https://ref.ly/Zeph1:18), [ZEP 2:2](https://ref.ly/Zeph2:2)

The consequences of God's anger
-------------------------------

### God allows those who reject righteousness to remain in their sin

**[ROM 1:18–1:32](https://ref.ly/Rom1:18-Rom1:32)** *See also* [1KI 14:16](https://ref.ly/1Kgs14:16); [2CH 12:5](https://ref.ly/2Chr12:5); [NEH 9:28](https://ref.ly/Neh9:28); [ISA 54:7–54:8](https://ref.ly/Isa54:7-Isa54:8); [JER 7:27–7:29](https://ref.ly/Jer7:27-Jer7:29), [JER 12:7–12:8](https://ref.ly/Jer12:7-Jer12:8)

### Punishment will be experienced by rebellious people

**[DEU 8:19](https://ref.ly/Deut8:19)** *See also* [ISA 59:18](https://ref.ly/Isa59:18); [JER 21:14](https://ref.ly/Jer21:14); [MAT 18:34–18:35](https://ref.ly/Matt18:34-Matt18:35), [MAT 25:28–25:30](https://ref.ly/Matt25:28-Matt25:30)EXO [12:12](https://ref.ly/Matt12:12); [NUM 32:13](https://ref.ly/Num32:13); [JOS 7:25–7:26](https://ref.ly/Josh7:25-Josh7:26); [ISA 13:9–13:13](https://ref.ly/Isa13:9-Isa13:13); [DAN 5:30](https://ref.ly/Dan5:30); [ACT 5:5](https://ref.ly/Acts5:5), [ACT 5:101](https://ref.ly/Acts5:101)KI [14:15](https://ref.ly/Acts14:15); [JER 15:13–15:14](https://ref.ly/Jer15:13-Jer15:14), [JER 25:7–25:11](https://ref.ly/Jer25:7-Jer25:11)LAM [2:1–2:9](https://ref.ly/Jer2:1-Jer2:9); [EZK 38:19–38:21](https://ref.ly/Ezek38:19-Ezek38:21)

### God will be feared as his holiness and greatness are revealed

**[ISA 59:18–59:19](https://ref.ly/Isa59:18-Isa59:19)** *See also* [EZK 38:22–38:23](https://ref.ly/Ezek38:22-Ezek38:23)

### Ultimately God will purify and restore his people for service

**[MAL 3:2–3:4](https://ref.ly/Mal3:2-Mal3:4)** *See also* [JER 15:19–15:21](https://ref.ly/Jer15:19-Jer15:21)

* **Associated Passages:** Nahum 1:6; Joshua 7:26; Ezekiel 38:18; Exodus 34:6; Isaiah 54:7-8; Nehemiah 9:16-18; Psalms 7:11; Habakkuk 3:2; Jeremiah 23:20; Jeremiah 30:24; Numbers 25:3; Exodus 32:8-10; Deuteronomy 8:19; Judges 2:10-14; 1 Kings 14:9; 1 Kings 16:32-33; 1 Kings 22:53; 2 Kings 23:19; 2 Chronicles 28:25; 2 Chronicles 34:25; Jeremiah 8:19; Jeremiah 32:29; Jeremiah 44:3; John 3:36; Romans 1:18-23; Romans 2:8; Joshua 7:1; Deuteronomy 9:7; 2 Kings 22:13; 1 Chronicles 13:10; Psalms 106:29; Jeremiah 32:32; Zechariah 7:13; Ephesians 5:6; 2 Timothy 3:1-9; Jude 1:14-16; Matthew 23:27-28; 2 Chronicles 32:25; Proverbs 3:34; Proverbs 8:13; Isaiah 13:11; Hosea 12:14; Malachi 4:1; Numbers 11:1; Numbers 14:27; Numbers 21:5; Zechariah 7:9-12; 2 Chronicles 19:7; Jeremiah 22:13; Ezekiel 9:9; Malachi 3:5; Matthew 23:23; Hebrews 10:29-31; Deuteronomy 32:35-36; Psalms 135:14; Nehemiah 9:26; Zechariah 7:12; Matthew 21:33-41; Acts 7:35-37; Romans 1:18; Jeremiah 10:10; Romans 2:5; Isaiah 13:9; Isaiah 13:13; Ezekiel 7:19; Zephaniah 1:15; Zephaniah 1:18; Zephaniah 2:2; Romans 1:18-32; 1 Kings 14:16; 2 Chronicles 12:5; Nehemiah 9:28; Jeremiah 7:27-29; Jeremiah 12:7-8; Isaiah 59:18; Jeremiah 21:14; Matthew 18:34-35; Matthew 25:28-30; Matthew 12:12; Numbers 32:13; Joshua 7:25-26; Isaiah 13:9-13; Daniel 5:30; Acts 5:5; Acts 5:101; Acts 14:15; Jeremiah 15:13-14; Jeremiah 25:7-11; Jeremiah 2:1-9; Ezekiel 38:19-21; Isaiah 59:18-19; Ezekiel 38:22-23; Malachi 3:2-4; Jeremiah 15:19-21

## 1030: God, compassion of (id: 1030)

An aspect of God's nature which is reflected in his sympathetic understanding of human weakness and his restoration of those in trouble.

God is compassionate by nature
------------------------------

**[2CO 1:3](https://ref.ly/2Cor1:3)** *See also* [EXO 33:19](https://ref.ly/Exod33:19), [EXO 34:6](https://ref.ly/Exod34:6); [PSA 86:15](https://ref.ly/Ps86:15), [PSA 103:8](https://ref.ly/Ps103:8), [PSA 116:5](https://ref.ly/Ps116:5), [PSA 119:156](https://ref.ly/Ps119:156); [HOS 1:7](https://ref.ly/Hos1:7); [JOL 2:13](https://ref.ly/Joel2:13)

God shows compassion as a parent
--------------------------------

**[PSA 103:13–103:14](https://ref.ly/Ps103:13-Ps103:14)** *See also* [ISA 49:15–49:16](https://ref.ly/Isa49:15-Isa49:16), [ISA 63:15–63:16](https://ref.ly/Isa63:15-Isa63:16); [JER 31:20](https://ref.ly/Jer31:20)

God shows compassion to all
---------------------------

**[PSA 145:8–145:9](https://ref.ly/Ps145:8-Ps145:9)**

### God shows compassion to those in deep trouble

**[ISA 49:13](https://ref.ly/Isa49:13)** *See also* [EXO 22:27](https://ref.ly/Exod22:27); [2KI 13:22–13:23](https://ref.ly/2Kgs13:22-2Kgs13:23); [PSA 40:1–40:2](https://ref.ly/Ps40:1-Ps40:2), [PSA 40:11–40:12](https://ref.ly/Ps40:11-Ps40:12), [PSA 69:16–69:17](https://ref.ly/Ps69:16-Ps69:17); [ISA 30:18](https://ref.ly/Isa30:18); [LAM 3:22](https://ref.ly/Lam3:22), [LAM 3:32](https://ref.ly/Lam3:32); [ZEC 10:6](https://ref.ly/Zech10:6); [JAS 5:11](https://ref.ly/Jas5:11)

### God shows compassion towards sinners

**[NEH 9:17](https://ref.ly/Neh9:17)** *See also* [DEU 13:17](https://ref.ly/Deut13:17); [NEH 9:28](https://ref.ly/Neh9:28); [PSA 51:1–51:2](https://ref.ly/Ps51:1-Ps51:2), [PSA 103:3–103:4](https://ref.ly/Ps103:3-Ps103:4); [ISA 54:7–54:8](https://ref.ly/Isa54:7-Isa54:8), [ISA 60:10](https://ref.ly/Isa60:10); [DAN 9:9](https://ref.ly/Dan9:9); [MIC 7:19](https://ref.ly/Mic7:19)

### The return from exile shows God's compassion to sinners

**[EZK 39:25](https://ref.ly/Ezek39:25)** *See also* [DEU 30:2–30:3](https://ref.ly/Deut30:2-Deut30:3); [JER 12:15](https://ref.ly/Jer12:15), [JER 30:18](https://ref.ly/Jer30:18), [JER 33:26](https://ref.ly/Jer33:26)

God's deeds show his compassion
-------------------------------

**[PSA 111:3–111:4](https://ref.ly/Ps111:3-Ps111:4)** *See also* [PSA 102:14](https://ref.ly/Ps102:14); [ISA 14:1](https://ref.ly/Isa14:1), [ISA 63:7](https://ref.ly/Isa63:7)

God's compassion is essential to believers' well\-being
-------------------------------------------------------

**[PSA 119:77](https://ref.ly/Ps119:77)** *See also* [PSA 77:8–77:9](https://ref.ly/Ps77:8-Ps77:9); [ISA 63:15](https://ref.ly/Isa63:15)

God's compassion is reflected in acts of human compassion
---------------------------------------------------------

**[COL 3:12](https://ref.ly/Col3:12)** *See also* [2CH 30:9](https://ref.ly/2Chr30:9); [JER 42:12](https://ref.ly/Jer42:12); [ZEC 7:9](https://ref.ly/Zech7:9); [LUK 6:36](https://ref.ly/Luke6:36); [EPH 4:32](https://ref.ly/Eph4:32)

Jesus Christ reflects God's compassion
--------------------------------------

**[HEB 4:15](https://ref.ly/Heb4:15)** *See also* [LUK 1:72](https://ref.ly/Luke1:72), [LUK 15:20](https://ref.ly/Luke15:20)

## 1035: God, faithfulness of (id: 1035)

God's perfect loyalty and consistency in being true to his name, his character and his word.

God's faithfulness is an integral part of his nature
----------------------------------------------------

**[NUM 23:19](https://ref.ly/Num23:19)** *God's limitless power and steadfast love imply complete faithfulness which contrasts with human nature*; **[LAM 3:22–3:23](https://ref.ly/Lam3:22-Lam3:23)** *See also* [EXO 34:6](https://ref.ly/Exod34:6); [DEU 7:8–7:9](https://ref.ly/Deut7:8-Deut7:9), [DEU 32:4](https://ref.ly/Deut32:4); [ROM 4:21](https://ref.ly/Rom4:21); [2TI 2:13](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:13)

God is faithful to his name and character
-----------------------------------------

**[2TI 2:13](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:13)** *See also* [NEH 9:8](https://ref.ly/Neh9:8); [PSA 106:8](https://ref.ly/Ps106:8); [1TH 5:24](https://ref.ly/1Thess5:24); [HEB 6:13–6:18](https://ref.ly/Heb6:13-Heb6:18)

God's faithfulness is known through fulfilled promises
------------------------------------------------------

**[JOS 23:14](https://ref.ly/Josh23:14)** *See also* [JOS 21:45](https://ref.ly/Josh21:45); [1KI 8:56](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:56); [1CH 16:15](https://ref.ly/1Chr16:15); [PSA 145:13](https://ref.ly/Ps145:13); [2PE 3:9](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:9)

Examples of God's faithfulness in fulfilled promises
----------------------------------------------------

### Abraham's fatherhood

[GEN 12:2–12:3](https://ref.ly/Gen12:2-Gen12:3), [GEN 15:4](https://ref.ly/Gen15:4), [GEN 21:1–21:2](https://ref.ly/Gen21:1-Gen21:2); ; [ROM 9:9](https://ref.ly/Rom9:9); ; [GAL 4:28](https://ref.ly/Gal4:28); ; [HEB 6:13–6:15](https://ref.ly/Heb6:13-Heb6:15), [HEB 11:11](https://ref.ly/Heb11:11)

### The building of the temple

[2SA 7:12–7:13](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:12-2Sam7:13) parallel [1CH 17:11–17:12](https://ref.ly/1Chr17:11-1Chr17:12); ; [1KI 8:17–8:21](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:17-1Kgs8:21) parallel [2CH 6:7–6:11](https://ref.ly/2Chr6:7-2Chr6:11)

### The exile in Babylon

**[JER 25:8–25:11](https://ref.ly/Jer25:8-Jer25:11)** *God's faithfulness will not always mean human prosperity.* *See also* [2KI 25:8–25:12](https://ref.ly/2Kgs25:8-2Kgs25:12) parallels [2CH 36:17–36:21](https://ref.ly/2Chr36:17-2Chr36:21), [JER 52:12–52:16](https://ref.ly/Jer52:12-Jer52:16); [EZR 1:1–1:3](https://ref.ly/Ezra1:1-Ezra1:3); [JER 52:27](https://ref.ly/Jer52:27), [JER 29:10](https://ref.ly/Jer29:10); [DAN 9:2–9:3](https://ref.ly/Dan9:2-Dan9:3), [DAN 9:15–9:19](https://ref.ly/Dan9:15-Dan9:19)

God's faithfulness is revealed to the faithful
----------------------------------------------

**[2SA 22:26](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:26)** *See also* [GAL 3:14](https://ref.ly/Gal3:14); [HEB 10:23](https://ref.ly/Heb10:23)

God's faithfulness is constant
------------------------------

**[ROM 3:3–3:4](https://ref.ly/Rom3:3-Rom3:4)** *God's faithfulness is not negated by human unfaithfulness.* *See also* [EZK 12:25](https://ref.ly/Ezek12:25); [HAB 2:3](https://ref.ly/Hab2:3); [2TI 2:13](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:13)

Jesus Christ is the ultimate evidence of God's faithfulness
-----------------------------------------------------------

**[ACT 13:32–13:33](https://ref.ly/Acts13:32-Acts13:33)** *See also* [JHN 14:9–14:11](https://ref.ly/John14:9-John14:11); [ROM 15:8–15:9](https://ref.ly/Rom15:8-Rom15:9); [2CO 1:20–1:22](https://ref.ly/2Cor1:20-2Cor1:22); [HEB 3:2–3:6](https://ref.ly/Heb3:2-Heb3:6); [REV 1:5](https://ref.ly/Rev1:5), [REV 19:11](https://ref.ly/Rev19:11)

* **Associated Passages:** Numbers 23:19; Lamentations 3:22-23; Exodus 34:6; Deuteronomy 7:8-9; Deuteronomy 32:4; Romans 4:21; 2 Timothy 2:13; Nehemiah 9:8; Psalms 106:8; 1 Thessalonians 5:24; Hebrews 6:13-18; Joshua 23:14; Joshua 21:45; 1 Kings 8:56; 1 Chronicles 16:15; Psalms 145:13; 2 Peter 3:9; Genesis 12:2-3; Genesis 15:4; Genesis 21:1-2; Romans 9:9; Galatians 4:28; Hebrews 6:13-15; Hebrews 11:11; 2 Samuel 7:12-13; 1 Chronicles 17:11-12; 1 Kings 8:17-21; 2 Chronicles 6:7-11; Jeremiah 25:8-11; 2 Kings 25:8-12; 2 Chronicles 36:17-21; Jeremiah 52:12-16; Ezra 1:1-3; Jeremiah 52:27; Jeremiah 29:10; Daniel 9:2-3; Daniel 9:15-19; 2 Samuel 22:26; Galatians 3:14; Hebrews 10:23; Romans 3:3-4; Ezekiel 12:25; Habakkuk 2:3; Acts 13:32-33; John 14:9-11; Romans 15:8-9; 2 Corinthians 1:20-22; Hebrews 3:2-6; Revelation 1:5; Revelation 19:11

## 1040: God, fatherhood of (id: 1040)

Primarily signifying God's paternal relationship to Jesus Christ, the term also refers to God's fatherly relationship to his creation, especially to believers as the “children of God”.

Aspects of the fatherhood of God
--------------------------------

### He is the Creator and provider

**[1CO 8:6](https://ref.ly/1Cor8:6)** *See also* [DEU 32:6](https://ref.ly/Deut32:6), [DEU 32:18](https://ref.ly/Deut32:18); [ISA 64:8](https://ref.ly/Isa64:8); [ACT 17:24–17:28](https://ref.ly/Acts17:24-Acts17:28)

### He shows love and compassion

**[HOS 11:1](https://ref.ly/Hos11:1)** *See also* [PSA 103:13](https://ref.ly/Ps103:13); [JER 3:19](https://ref.ly/Jer3:19); [2CO 1:3](https://ref.ly/2Cor1:3)

### He exercises his providence and care

**[PSA 68:5](https://ref.ly/Ps68:5)** *See also* [MAT 6:26](https://ref.ly/Matt6:26), [MAT 6:31–6:33](https://ref.ly/Matt6:31-Matt6:33) parallel [LUK 12:29–12:31](https://ref.ly/Luke12:29-Luke12:31); [MAT 7:11](https://ref.ly/Matt7:11) parallel [LUK 11:13](https://ref.ly/Luke11:13)

### He disciplines and corrects

**[DEU 8:5](https://ref.ly/Deut8:5)** *See also* [PRO 3:11–3:12](https://ref.ly/Prov3:11-Prov3:12); [HEB 12:5–12:6](https://ref.ly/Heb12:5-Heb12:6)

God as the Father of Jesus Christ
---------------------------------

**[MAT 3:17](https://ref.ly/Matt3:17)** parallels [MRK 1:11](https://ref.ly/Mark1:11), [LUK 3:22](https://ref.ly/Luke3:22) *See also* [MAT 11:27](https://ref.ly/Matt11:27); [LUK 2:49](https://ref.ly/Luke2:49); [JHN 5:17–5:18](https://ref.ly/John5:17-John5:18), [JHN 17:11](https://ref.ly/John17:11), [JHN 20:17](https://ref.ly/John20:17); [ROM 15:6](https://ref.ly/Rom15:6); [EPH 1:3](https://ref.ly/Eph1:3)**[1PE 1:3](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:3)** *See also* [1JN 1:3](https://ref.ly/1John1:3)

God is the father of Israel
---------------------------

### He cares for his covenant people

**[JER 31:9](https://ref.ly/Jer31:9)** *See also* [EXO 4:22](https://ref.ly/Exod4:22); [DEU 14:1](https://ref.ly/Deut14:1), [DEU 32:6](https://ref.ly/Deut32:6), [DEU 32:18](https://ref.ly/Deut32:18); [ISA 63:16](https://ref.ly/Isa63:16); [MAL 2:10](https://ref.ly/Mal2:10)

### He is the father of the kings of Israel

**[2SA 7:13–7:14](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:13-2Sam7:14)** parallel [1CH 17:12–17:13](https://ref.ly/1Chr17:12-1Chr17:13) *This description of God's fatherhood involves the maintenance of a special relationship between God and David's descendants, which ultimately includes Jesus Christ.* *See also* [PSA 2:7](https://ref.ly/Ps2:7), [PSA 89:26–89:27](https://ref.ly/Ps89:26-Ps89:27)

God is the father of Christian believers
----------------------------------------

### He has an intimate relationship with believers

**[MAT 6:9](https://ref.ly/Matt6:9)** parallel [LUK 11:2](https://ref.ly/Luke11:2) *See also* [JHN 20:17](https://ref.ly/John20:17); [2CO 6:18](https://ref.ly/2Cor6:18); [GAL 3:26](https://ref.ly/Gal3:26); [1JN 2:13](https://ref.ly/1John2:13)

### He adopts believers into his family

**[JHN 1:12–1:13](https://ref.ly/John1:12-John1:13)** *See also* [ROM 8:14–8:17](https://ref.ly/Rom8:14-Rom8:17); [GAL 4:5–4:7](https://ref.ly/Gal4:5-Gal4:7); [1JN 3:1](https://ref.ly/1John3:1)

The fatherhood of God has implications for the church
-----------------------------------------------------

### Character: children are to reproduce the Father's likeness

**[MAT 5:48](https://ref.ly/Matt5:48)**

### Unity: one Father means one family

**[EPH 4:3–4:6](https://ref.ly/Eph4:3-Eph4:6)** *See also* [MAL 2:10](https://ref.ly/Mal2:10); [MAT 23:9](https://ref.ly/Matt23:9); [EPH 3:14–3:15](https://ref.ly/Eph3:14-Eph3:15)

### Status: believers are related to Jesus Christ

**[MAT 12:50](https://ref.ly/Matt12:50)** parallels [MRK 3:35](https://ref.ly/Mark3:35), [LUK 8:21](https://ref.ly/Luke8:21) *See also* [ROM 8:29](https://ref.ly/Rom8:29); [HEB 2:11](https://ref.ly/Heb2:11)

### Inheritance: believers are heirs of the Father's kingdom

**[ROM 8:17](https://ref.ly/Rom8:17)** *See also* [LUK 12:32](https://ref.ly/Luke12:32); [GAL 3:29](https://ref.ly/Gal3:29); [COL 1:12](https://ref.ly/Col1:12); [TIT 3:7](https://ref.ly/Titus3:7)

### Submission: believers are to revere the Father

**[1PE 1:17](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:17)** *See also* [MAT 6:9](https://ref.ly/Matt6:9) parallel [LUK 11:2](https://ref.ly/Luke11:2); [EPH 3:14](https://ref.ly/Eph3:14)

## 1045: God, glory of (id: 1045)

The revelation of God's power and characteristics, sometimes accompanied by visible phenomena.

Glory as an attribute of God
----------------------------

**[PSA 24:7–24:8](https://ref.ly/Ps24:7-Ps24:8)** *See also* [PSA 29:3](https://ref.ly/Ps29:3); [JHN 11:40](https://ref.ly/John11:40); [ACT 7:2](https://ref.ly/Acts7:2); [REV 19:1](https://ref.ly/Rev19:1)

Visible phenomena accompanying God's glory
------------------------------------------

### The appearance of God's glory

**[HAB 3:4](https://ref.ly/Hab3:4)** *See also* [DEU 5:24](https://ref.ly/Deut5:24); [2SA 22:8–22:16](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:8-2Sam22:16) parallel [PSA 18:7–18:15](https://ref.ly/Ps18:7-Ps18:15); [PSA 104:1](https://ref.ly/Ps104:1); [EZK 1:26–1:28](https://ref.ly/Ezek1:26-Ezek1:28)

### God's glory as a cloud

**[EXO 24:15–24:16](https://ref.ly/Exod24:15-Exod24:16)** *See also* [EXO 33:9–33:10](https://ref.ly/Exod33:9-Exod33:10); [ISA 4:5](https://ref.ly/Isa4:5); [MAT 17:5](https://ref.ly/Matt17:5) parallels [MRK 9:7](https://ref.ly/Mark9:7), [LUK 9:34](https://ref.ly/Luke9:34); [LUK 21:27](https://ref.ly/Luke21:27) parallels [MAT 24:30](https://ref.ly/Matt24:30), [MRK 13:26](https://ref.ly/Mark13:26)

### God's glory in the tabernacle and the temple

**[2CH 5:13–5:14](https://ref.ly/2Chr5:13-2Chr5:14)** parallel [1KI 8:10–8:11](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:10-1Kgs8:11) *The Jewish term for the outward sign of God's presence in the temple is “Shekinah”.* *See also* [EXO 40:34–40:35](https://ref.ly/Exod40:34-Exod40:35); [2CH 7:1–7:3](https://ref.ly/2Chr7:1-2Chr7:3); [EZK 8:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek8:4), [EZK 9:3](https://ref.ly/Ezek9:3), [EZK 10:19](https://ref.ly/Ezek10:19), [EZK 43:1–43:5](https://ref.ly/Ezek43:1-Ezek43:5); [REV 15:8](https://ref.ly/Rev15:8)

--------------------

--------------------------------

**[1TI 6:15–6:16](https://ref.ly/1Tim6:15-1Tim6:16)** [EXO 33:18–33:20](https://ref.ly/Exod33:18-Exod33:20); ; [JDG 6:22–6:23](https://ref.ly/Judg6:22-Judg6:23), [JDG 13:20–13:22](https://ref.ly/Judg13:20-Judg13:22); ; [ISA 6:5](https://ref.ly/Isa6:5); ; [JHN 1:18](https://ref.ly/John1:18)

-----------------------

**[ACT 7:55](https://ref.ly/Acts7:55)** *See also* [EXO 3:2](https://ref.ly/Exod3:2) *Moses*; [ISA 6:1–6:4](https://ref.ly/Isa6:1-Isa6:4) *Isaiah*; [LUK 2:9](https://ref.ly/Luke2:9) *the shepherds*

The effects of God's glory
--------------------------

### God's glory is acknowledged

**[PSA 72:19](https://ref.ly/Ps72:19)** *See also* [PSA 29:2](https://ref.ly/Ps29:2); [ROM 11:36](https://ref.ly/Rom11:36); [REV 4:11](https://ref.ly/Rev4:11), [REV 5:13](https://ref.ly/Rev5:13), [REV 19:1](https://ref.ly/Rev19:1)

### God's glory brings guilt and fear

**[ROM 3:23](https://ref.ly/Rom3:23)** *See also* [ISA 2:10](https://ref.ly/Isa2:10), [ISA 2:19](https://ref.ly/Isa2:19), [ISA 2:21](https://ref.ly/Isa2:21); [REV 11:13](https://ref.ly/Rev11:13), [REV 15:8](https://ref.ly/Rev15:8)

## 1050: God, goodness of (id: 1050)

All God's perfect qualities are made freely available to all for the benefit of the whole world.

God alone is good
-----------------

**[MRK 10:18](https://ref.ly/Mark10:18)** parallels [MAT 19:17](https://ref.ly/Matt19:17), [LUK 18:19](https://ref.ly/Luke18:19)

God demonstrates his goodness
-----------------------------

### In his actions

**[PSA 119:68](https://ref.ly/Ps119:68)** *See also* [2CH 30:18](https://ref.ly/2Chr30:18); [NEH 9:20](https://ref.ly/Neh9:20); [PSA 73:1](https://ref.ly/Ps73:1), [PSA 143:10](https://ref.ly/Ps143:10); [ACT 10:38](https://ref.ly/Acts10:38); [ROM 2:4](https://ref.ly/Rom2:4)

**[1TI 4:4](https://ref.ly/1Tim4:4)** *See also* [GEN 1:4](https://ref.ly/Gen1:4), [GEN 1:31](https://ref.ly/Gen1:31); [PSA 145:9](https://ref.ly/Ps145:9)

### In his love

**[PSA 86:5](https://ref.ly/Ps86:5)** *See also* [1CH 16:34](https://ref.ly/1Chr16:34) parallel [PSA 106:1](https://ref.ly/Ps106:1); [PSA 25:7–25:8](https://ref.ly/Ps25:7-Ps25:8), [PSA 69:16](https://ref.ly/Ps69:16), [PSA 100:5](https://ref.ly/Ps100:5)

### In his gifts

**[JAS 1:17](https://ref.ly/Jas1:17)** *See also* [NUM 13:27](https://ref.ly/Num13:27); [DEU 8:7](https://ref.ly/Deut8:7), [DEU 26:11](https://ref.ly/Deut26:11); [HEB 9:11](https://ref.ly/Heb9:11)

## 1055: God, grace and mercy of (id: 1055)

The qualities of God's character by which he shows himself compassionate, accepting, and generous to sinful human beings, shielding them from his wrath, forgiving them, and bestowing on them his righteousness so that they can live and grow in faith and obedience. Grace and mercy are particularly expressed through God's covenant with his chosen people and through Jesus Christ's atoning death on the cross.

God's grace and mercy are made known in Jesus Christ
----------------------------------------------------

**[JHN 1:16–1:17](https://ref.ly/John1:16-John1:17)**

The abundance of God's grace and mercy
--------------------------------------

**[EPH 2:4–2:8](https://ref.ly/Eph2:4-Eph2:8)** *See also* [2SA 24:14](https://ref.ly/2Sam24:14) parallel [1CH 21:13](https://ref.ly/1Chr21:13); [PSA 69:13](https://ref.ly/Ps69:13), [PSA 84:11](https://ref.ly/Ps84:11), [PSA 102:13](https://ref.ly/Ps102:13); [ROM 2:4](https://ref.ly/Rom2:4), [ROM 5:17](https://ref.ly/Rom5:17), [ROM 9:23](https://ref.ly/Rom9:23); [1TI 1:14](https://ref.ly/1Tim1:14)

God's grace and mercy are always unearned and unmerited
-------------------------------------------------------

**[DEU 7:7–7:8](https://ref.ly/Deut7:7-Deut7:8)** *See also* [DEU 9:5–9:6](https://ref.ly/Deut9:5-Deut9:6); [EZK 36:22](https://ref.ly/Ezek36:22); [DAN 9:18](https://ref.ly/Dan9:18); [ROM 9:16](https://ref.ly/Rom9:16); [EPH 1:6](https://ref.ly/Eph1:6), [EPH 2:8–2:9](https://ref.ly/Eph2:8-Eph2:9), [EPH 3:8](https://ref.ly/Eph3:8); [TIT 3:5](https://ref.ly/Titus3:5)

God's grace and mercy are a source of blessing
----------------------------------------------

**[GEN 21:1–21:2](https://ref.ly/Gen21:1-Gen21:2)** *See also* [GEN 33:11](https://ref.ly/Gen33:11); [1SA 2:21](https://ref.ly/1Sam2:21)

God's grace and mercy are expressed in the covenant relationship
----------------------------------------------------------------

**[JER 31:3](https://ref.ly/Jer31:3)** *Hebrew “hesed” (translated as “love”, “loving\-kindness”, “unfailing love”) expresses specifically the grace and mercy that underlie the covenant relationship.* *See also* [EXO 34:6](https://ref.ly/Exod34:6); [DEU 7:9](https://ref.ly/Deut7:9), [DEU 7:12](https://ref.ly/Deut7:12); [NEH 9:17](https://ref.ly/Neh9:17); [PSA 6:4](https://ref.ly/Ps6:4); [ISA 55:3](https://ref.ly/Isa55:3); [LAM 3:22](https://ref.ly/Lam3:22), [LAM 3:32](https://ref.ly/Lam3:32)

Salvation comes by grace
------------------------

**[TIT 2:11](https://ref.ly/Titus2:11)** *See also* [MRK 10:25–10:27](https://ref.ly/Mark10:25-Mark10:27) *Jesus Christ's words to his disciples*; [ROM 5:15](https://ref.ly/Rom5:15); [EPH 1:5–1:6](https://ref.ly/Eph1:5-Eph1:6), [EPH 2:8](https://ref.ly/Eph2:8); [2TI 1:9–1:10](https://ref.ly/2Tim1:9-2Tim1:10)

### This is ultimately shown in the cross of Jesus Christ

**[ROM 3:24–3:25](https://ref.ly/Rom3:24-Rom3:25)** *See also* [ROM 5:8](https://ref.ly/Rom5:8); [EPH 1:7](https://ref.ly/Eph1:7); [HEB 2:9](https://ref.ly/Heb2:9); [2PE 1:10–1:11](https://ref.ly/2Pet1:10-2Pet1:11)

--------------------------------------------

### Punishment is withheld

### Sinners' prayers are heard

**[PSA 51:1](https://ref.ly/Ps51:1)**; **[LUK 18:13–18:14](https://ref.ly/Luke18:13-Luke18:14)** *See also* [PSA 6:2–6:3](https://ref.ly/Ps6:2-Ps6:3), [PSA 123:3](https://ref.ly/Ps123:3); [HAB 3:2](https://ref.ly/Hab3:2)

The favour of God
-----------------

### Examples of those who found favour with God

### The OT predicts a future age of God's favour

--------------------------------------------------------

### God's grace and mercy are to influence the character and conduct of believers

**[EPH 3:7–3:8](https://ref.ly/Eph3:7-Eph3:8)** *See also* [1CO 3:10](https://ref.ly/1Cor3:10); [2CO 12:7–12:9](https://ref.ly/2Cor12:7-2Cor12:9); [GAL 1:15–1:16](https://ref.ly/Gal1:15-Gal1:16); [EPH 4:7](https://ref.ly/Eph4:7), [EPH 4:11](https://ref.ly/Eph4:11)

--------------------------------------

## 1060: God, greatness of (id: 1060)

God's nature, deeds and attributes are incomparable, for which he deserves all praise.

God is great
------------

**[JER 10:6](https://ref.ly/Jer10:6)** *See also* [1CH 16:25](https://ref.ly/1Chr16:25) parallel [PSA 96:4](https://ref.ly/Ps96:4); [1CH 29:11](https://ref.ly/1Chr29:11); [NEH 1:5](https://ref.ly/Neh1:5); [ISA 12:6](https://ref.ly/Isa12:6)

God's name is great
-------------------

**[EZK 36:23](https://ref.ly/Ezek36:23)** *See also* [JOS 7:9](https://ref.ly/Josh7:9); [1SA 12:22](https://ref.ly/1Sam12:22); [1KI 8:42](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:42) parallel [2CH 6:32](https://ref.ly/2Chr6:32)

God is a great king
-------------------

**[PSA 47:2](https://ref.ly/Ps47:2)** *See also* [PSA 47:7](https://ref.ly/Ps47:7), [PSA 48:2](https://ref.ly/Ps48:2); [MAL 1:14](https://ref.ly/Mal1:14); [MAT 5:35](https://ref.ly/Matt5:35); [1TI 6:15](https://ref.ly/1Tim6:15)

---------------------

### He does great things

**[PSA 136:4](https://ref.ly/Ps136:4)** *See also* [JDG 2:7](https://ref.ly/Judg2:7); [ISA 55:9](https://ref.ly/Isa55:9); [JER 32:19](https://ref.ly/Jer32:19); [LUK 1:49](https://ref.ly/Luke1:49); [EPH 3:20](https://ref.ly/Eph3:20)

**[DEU 9:29](https://ref.ly/Deut9:29)** *God's powerful acts are often associated with the exodus.* *See also* [EXO 15:7](https://ref.ly/Exod15:7); [DEU 9:261](https://ref.ly/Deut9:261)SA [19:5](https://ref.ly/Deut19:5); [2SA 23:10](https://ref.ly/2Sam23:10)ISA [40:26](https://ref.ly/2Sam40:26); [JER 32:17](https://ref.ly/Jer32:17)[NAM 1:3](https://ref.ly/Nah1:3); [EPH 1:19–1:20](https://ref.ly/Eph1:19-Eph1:20) *His great power at work in the resurrection*

--------------------------

### His great love

**[PSA 108:4](https://ref.ly/Ps108:4)** *See also* [NUM 14:19](https://ref.ly/Num14:19); [2CH 1:8](https://ref.ly/2Chr1:8); [LAM 3:22](https://ref.ly/Lam3:22); [EPH 2:4](https://ref.ly/Eph2:4); [1JN 3:1](https://ref.ly/1John3:1)

The effects of God's greatness
------------------------------

## 1065: God, holiness of (id: 1065)

The moral excellence of God that unifies his attributes and is expressed through his actions, setting him apart from all others. Believers are called to be holy as God is holy.

God's nature is holy
--------------------

### He is perfect

**[DEU 32:4](https://ref.ly/Deut32:4)**; **[ISA 6:3](https://ref.ly/Isa6:3)**; **[REV 4:8](https://ref.ly/Rev4:8)** *See also* [2SA 22:31](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:31); [JOB 6:10](https://ref.ly/Job6:10); [PSA 18:30](https://ref.ly/Ps18:30), [PSA 22:3](https://ref.ly/Ps22:3), [PSA 71:22](https://ref.ly/Ps71:22), [PSA 78:41](https://ref.ly/Ps78:41); [ISA 41:14](https://ref.ly/Isa41:14), [ISA 43:15](https://ref.ly/Isa43:15); [HAB 1:13](https://ref.ly/Hab1:13); [JHN 17:11](https://ref.ly/John17:11); [REV 6:10](https://ref.ly/Rev6:10)

### He is uniquely holy

**[1SA 2:2](https://ref.ly/1Sam2:2)** *See also* [EXO 15:11](https://ref.ly/Exod15:11); [PSA 77:13](https://ref.ly/Ps77:13); [ISA 40:25](https://ref.ly/Isa40:25); [REV 15:4](https://ref.ly/Rev15:4)

God's name is holy
------------------

**[EZK 36:21–36:23](https://ref.ly/Ezek36:21-Ezek36:23)** *See also* [LEV 22:32](https://ref.ly/Lev22:32); [1CH 16:35](https://ref.ly/1Chr16:35), [1CH 29:16](https://ref.ly/1Chr29:16); [PSA 33:21](https://ref.ly/Ps33:21), [PSA 97:12](https://ref.ly/Ps97:12); [ISA 57:15](https://ref.ly/Isa57:15); [EZK 39:25](https://ref.ly/Ezek39:25); [LUK 1:49](https://ref.ly/Luke1:49)

## 1070: God, joy of (id: 1070)

God rejoices in the well\-being and faithfulness of his covenant people, and in the repentance and conversion of sinners. He brings joy to his people, who rejoice in his presence and faithfulness.

God is the source of joy
------------------------

**[PSA 37:4](https://ref.ly/Ps37:4)** *See also* [1SA 2:1](https://ref.ly/1Sam2:1); [NEH 1:11](https://ref.ly/Neh1:11), [NEH 12:43](https://ref.ly/Neh12:43); [ISA 61:10](https://ref.ly/Isa61:10); [JHN 15:11](https://ref.ly/John15:11); [PHP 4:4](https://ref.ly/Phil4:4)

---------------------------------------------

------------------------------------------------

## 1075: God, justice of (id: 1075)

The moral righteousness of God is revealed in his laws and expressed in his judicial acts. God's commands and judgments meet perfect standards of justice, and his apportioning of punishments and rewards is also perfectly just. God's justice is impartial. Special praise is his for vindicating the penitent and the needy who have no human champions. Ultimately, all God's ways will be seen as just and equitable.

God's justice displays his righteousness
----------------------------------------

### It conforms to his moral law

**[JOB 34:12](https://ref.ly/Job34:12)** *See also* [DEU 32:4](https://ref.ly/Deut32:4); [PSA 9:16](https://ref.ly/Ps9:16), [PSA 11:7](https://ref.ly/Ps11:7); [ZEP 3:5](https://ref.ly/Zeph3:5); [ROM 2:2](https://ref.ly/Rom2:2); [2TI 2:13](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:13); [REV 15:3](https://ref.ly/Rev15:3)

### It is seen in his perfect will

**[PSA 99:4](https://ref.ly/Ps99:4)** *See also* [PSA 40:8](https://ref.ly/Ps40:8); [ISA 53:10](https://ref.ly/Isa53:10); [MAT 6:10](https://ref.ly/Matt6:10), [MAT 26:39](https://ref.ly/Matt26:39) parallels [MRK 14:36](https://ref.ly/Mark14:36), [LUK 22:42](https://ref.ly/Luke22:42); [HEB 10:9–10:10](https://ref.ly/Heb10:9-Heb10:10)

God acts with justice
---------------------

**[PSA 33:5–33:15](https://ref.ly/Ps33:5-Ps33:15)** *See also* [NEH 9:33](https://ref.ly/Neh9:33)

### God's justice is exercised fairly and equitably

**[PSA 9:7–9:8](https://ref.ly/Ps9:7-Ps9:8)** *See also* [PSA 96:13](https://ref.ly/Ps96:13), [PSA 98:9](https://ref.ly/Ps98:9), [PSA 99:4](https://ref.ly/Ps99:4)

**[REV 20:12–20:13](https://ref.ly/Rev20:12-Rev20:13)** *See also* [EXO 34:6–34:7](https://ref.ly/Exod34:6-Exod34:7); [PSA 62:12](https://ref.ly/Ps62:12); [JER 17:10](https://ref.ly/Jer17:10); [EZK 18:20](https://ref.ly/Ezek18:20); [MAT 16:27](https://ref.ly/Matt16:27); [REV 22:12](https://ref.ly/Rev22:12)

### He punishes wickedness

**[EZK 18:20](https://ref.ly/Ezek18:20)** *See also* [EXO 34:7](https://ref.ly/Exod34:7); [DEU 32:35](https://ref.ly/Deut32:35); [ISA 59:18](https://ref.ly/Isa59:18), [ISA 66:24](https://ref.ly/Isa66:24); [MAT 25:41–25:46](https://ref.ly/Matt25:41-Matt25:46); [COL 3:25](https://ref.ly/Col3:25); [2TH 1:8–1:9](https://ref.ly/2Thess1:8-2Thess1:9)

**[PSA 58:11](https://ref.ly/Ps58:11)** *See also* [ISA 62:11](https://ref.ly/Isa62:11); [MAT 5:12](https://ref.ly/Matt5:12) parallel [LUK 6:23](https://ref.ly/Luke6:23); [MAT 25:34–25:40](https://ref.ly/Matt25:34-Matt25:40), [MAT 25:46](https://ref.ly/Matt25:46); [ROM 2:7](https://ref.ly/Rom2:7), [ROM 8:1–8:2](https://ref.ly/Rom8:1-Rom8:2); [2TI 4:8](https://ref.ly/2Tim4:8)

God establishes justice
-----------------------

### He upholds the cause of the oppressed

God's ways in exercising justice
--------------------------------

### God's justice is not always immediately apparent

**[JER 12:1](https://ref.ly/Jer12:1)** *See also* [JOB 21:7](https://ref.ly/Job21:7); [PSA 73:3–73:14](https://ref.ly/Ps73:3-Ps73:14); [ECC 7:15](https://ref.ly/Eccl7:15); [HAB 1:2–1:4](https://ref.ly/Hab1:2-Hab1:4); [MAL 2:17](https://ref.ly/Mal2:17), [MAL 3:14–3:15](https://ref.ly/Mal3:14-Mal3:15); [MAT 20:10–20:12](https://ref.ly/Matt20:10-Matt20:12)

**[2CH 36:15](https://ref.ly/2Chr36:15)** *See also* [2KI 17:23](https://ref.ly/2Kgs17:23); [NEH 9:29–9:30](https://ref.ly/Neh9:29-Neh9:30); [JER 7:13](https://ref.ly/Jer7:13); [JON 3:4](https://ref.ly/Jonah3:4); [HEB 12:25](https://ref.ly/Heb12:25)

--------------------------------

**[GAL 6:7–6:8](https://ref.ly/Gal6:7-Gal6:8)** *See also* [GEN 18:25](https://ref.ly/Gen18:25); [NUM 32:23](https://ref.ly/Num32:23); [PSA 73:17](https://ref.ly/Ps73:17); [LUK 16:25](https://ref.ly/Luke16:25), [LUK 18:7–18:8](https://ref.ly/Luke18:7-Luke18:8); [COL 3:24–3:25](https://ref.ly/Col3:24-Col3:25)

------------------------------------------------------

**[ROM 3:25–3:26](https://ref.ly/Rom3:25-Rom3:26)** *See also* [ISA 53:10–53:11](https://ref.ly/Isa53:10-Isa53:11); [HEB 9:22](https://ref.ly/Heb9:22); [1JN 1:9](https://ref.ly/1John1:9), [1JN 2:1–2:2](https://ref.ly/1John2:1-1John2:2)

--------------------------------------------------------------

**[MAT 25:31–25:33](https://ref.ly/Matt25:31-Matt25:33)** *See also* [ISA 9:6–9:7](https://ref.ly/Isa9:6-Isa9:7); [ACT 17:31](https://ref.ly/Acts17:31); [REV 19:11–19:16](https://ref.ly/Rev19:11-Rev19:16)

## 1080: God, living and self-sustaining (id: 1080)

God is alive and active. In contrast to idols, he is uncreated and the source of all continuing life.

God is alive
------------

**[JER 10:10](https://ref.ly/Jer10:10)** *See also* [GEN 1:1](https://ref.ly/Gen1:1); [DEU 5:26](https://ref.ly/Deut5:26); [JOS 3:10](https://ref.ly/Josh3:10); [JER 23:36](https://ref.ly/Jer23:36); [MAT 26:63](https://ref.ly/Matt26:63); [1TI 3:15](https://ref.ly/1Tim3:15); [HEB 3:12](https://ref.ly/Heb3:12), [HEB 12:22](https://ref.ly/Heb12:22)

God lives for ever
------------------

---------------------

**[JHN 5:26](https://ref.ly/John5:26)** *See also* [EXO 3:14](https://ref.ly/Exod3:14); [JHN 8:58](https://ref.ly/John8:58); [ACT 17:25](https://ref.ly/Acts17:25)

## 1085: God, love of (id: 1085)

The deepest possible expression of God's character. Though God loves all people, he is especially committed to sacrificial, loyal relationships with his people.

God's nature is love
--------------------

**[1JN 4:8](https://ref.ly/1John4:8)** *See also* [1JN 4:16](https://ref.ly/1John4:16)

### His love is perfectly expressed within the Trinity

**[MRK 1:10–1:11](https://ref.ly/Mark1:10-Mark1:11)** parallels [MAT 3:16–3:17](https://ref.ly/Matt3:16-Matt3:17), [LUK 3:21–3:22](https://ref.ly/Luke3:21-Luke3:22) *See also* [JHN 5:20](https://ref.ly/John5:20), [JHN 10:17](https://ref.ly/John10:17), [JHN 14:23](https://ref.ly/John14:23); [EPH 1:6](https://ref.ly/Eph1:6); [COL 1:13](https://ref.ly/Col1:13)

Characteristics of God's love
-----------------------------

### It is eternal

**[JER 31:3](https://ref.ly/Jer31:3)** *See also* [PSA 103:17](https://ref.ly/Ps103:17), [PSA 136:1–136:26](https://ref.ly/Ps136:1-Ps136:26); [ISA 49:15–49:16](https://ref.ly/Isa49:15-Isa49:16), [ISA 54:8](https://ref.ly/Isa54:8), [ISA 54:10](https://ref.ly/Isa54:10)

### It is a covenant love

**[DEU 7:9](https://ref.ly/Deut7:9)** *See also* [EXO 20:6](https://ref.ly/Exod20:6) parallel [DEU 5:10](https://ref.ly/Deut5:10); [DEU 7:12](https://ref.ly/Deut7:12); [1KI 8:23](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:23) parallel [2CH 6:14](https://ref.ly/2Chr6:14); [PSA 106:45](https://ref.ly/Ps106:45); [DAN 9:4](https://ref.ly/Dan9:4)

### It is lavish

**[EXO 34:6–34:7](https://ref.ly/Exod34:6-Exod34:7)** *See also* [NEH 9:17](https://ref.ly/Neh9:17); [PSA 103:8](https://ref.ly/Ps103:8); [JOL 2:13](https://ref.ly/Joel2:13); [JON 4:2](https://ref.ly/Jonah4:2); [1JN 3:1](https://ref.ly/1John3:1)

### It is holy and just

**[PSA 33:5](https://ref.ly/Ps33:5)** *See also* [PSA 37:28](https://ref.ly/Ps37:28), [PSA 99:4](https://ref.ly/Ps99:4); [ISA 61:8](https://ref.ly/Isa61:8)

## 1090: God, majesty of (id: 1090)

The greatness and splendour of God, revealed in his creation and mighty works of deliverance. On account of his majesty, God is worthy of praise and adoration from all people.

God is majestic
---------------

**[HEB 8:1](https://ref.ly/Heb8:1)** *See also* [1SA 15:29](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:29); [PSA 24:10](https://ref.ly/Ps24:10) *The word translated “glory” also means “majesty”*; [HEB 1:3–1:4](https://ref.ly/Heb1:3-Heb1:4)

Majesty belongs to God
----------------------

**[1CH 29:11](https://ref.ly/1Chr29:11)** *See also* [PSA 145:12](https://ref.ly/Ps145:12); [JUD 1:25](https://ref.ly/Jude1:25)

God's majesty is awesome
------------------------

**[JOB 37:22](https://ref.ly/Job37:22)** *See also* [ISA 2:10](https://ref.ly/Isa2:10), [ISA 2:19](https://ref.ly/Isa2:19), [ISA 2:21](https://ref.ly/Isa2:21)

God's character is majestic
---------------------------

**[PSA 93:1](https://ref.ly/Ps93:1)** *A figurative expression indicating that God is fully majestic.* *See also* [EXO 15:11](https://ref.ly/Exod15:11); [PSA 104:1](https://ref.ly/Ps104:1), [PSA 145:5](https://ref.ly/Ps145:5); [ISA 24:14](https://ref.ly/Isa24:14), [ISA 26:10](https://ref.ly/Isa26:10)

God's activity is majestic
--------------------------

**[EXO 15:6–15:7](https://ref.ly/Exod15:6-Exod15:7)** *“hand” is a symbol of God's power which accomplishes his purposes.* *See also* [DEU 9:26](https://ref.ly/Deut9:26), [DEU 11:2–11:3](https://ref.ly/Deut11:2-Deut11:3); [2CH 20:6](https://ref.ly/2Chr20:6); [PSA 111:3](https://ref.ly/Ps111:3); [LUK 9:43](https://ref.ly/Luke9:43)

----------------------

**[PSA 8:1](https://ref.ly/Ps8:1)** *See also* [PSA 8:9](https://ref.ly/Ps8:9)

God's voice is majestic
-----------------------

**[PSA 29:4](https://ref.ly/Ps29:4)** *See also* [JOB 37:4](https://ref.ly/Job37:4); [ISA 30:30](https://ref.ly/Isa30:30)

God's presence is majestic
--------------------------

**[1CH 16:27](https://ref.ly/1Chr16:27)** *See also* [PSA 96:6](https://ref.ly/Ps96:6); [2TH 1:9](https://ref.ly/2Thess1:9); [2PE 1:17](https://ref.ly/2Pet1:17)

----------------------------------------

**[2PE 1:16–1:17](https://ref.ly/2Pet1:16-2Pet1:17)** *See also* [HEB 1:3–1:4](https://ref.ly/Heb1:3-Heb1:4), [HEB 8:1](https://ref.ly/Heb8:1)

-----------------------

### To the Messiah

------------------------------------------

## 1095: God, patience of (id: 1095)

God shows forbearance in his character, decisions and actions. Above all, he waits patiently for people to turn to him for salvation.

God's patient character
-----------------------

### God is slow to anger

**[NUM 14:18](https://ref.ly/Num14:18)** *“slow to anger” is the main OT expression for God's patient character.* *See also* [EXO 34:6](https://ref.ly/Exod34:6); [NEH 9:16–9:17](https://ref.ly/Neh9:16-Neh9:17); [PSA 86:15](https://ref.ly/Ps86:15), [PSA 103:8](https://ref.ly/Ps103:8), [PSA 145:8](https://ref.ly/Ps145:8); [JOL 2:13](https://ref.ly/Joel2:13); [JON 4:2](https://ref.ly/Jonah4:2); [NAM 1:3](https://ref.ly/Nah1:3)

### God imparts patience

**[ROM 15:5](https://ref.ly/Rom15:5)** *The Greek can be translated “God of endurance/patience”. The phrase suggests that God is patient and imparts patience.* *See also* [JER 15:15](https://ref.ly/Jer15:15); [2TH 3:5](https://ref.ly/2Thess3:5); [1PE 3:20](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:20)

God's patience with sinful people
---------------------------------

### God's patience lasts a long time

**[ACT 13:18](https://ref.ly/Acts13:18)** *See also* [DEU 8:2](https://ref.ly/Deut8:2); [NEH 9:30](https://ref.ly/Neh9:30); [PSA 78:38](https://ref.ly/Ps78:38)

### God is patient in delaying punishment

**[ISA 42:14](https://ref.ly/Isa42:14)** *See also* [NEH 9:30–9:31](https://ref.ly/Neh9:30-Neh9:31); [PSA 50:20–50:21](https://ref.ly/Ps50:20-Ps50:21), [PSA 78:38](https://ref.ly/Ps78:38); [ISA 48:9](https://ref.ly/Isa48:9); [HAB 2:3](https://ref.ly/Hab2:3)

### Sinful people try God's patience

**[MAL 2:17](https://ref.ly/Mal2:17)** *See also* [GEN 18:16–18:33](https://ref.ly/Gen18:16-Gen18:33); [NUM 14:27](https://ref.ly/Num14:27); [PSA 78:41](https://ref.ly/Ps78:41), [PSA 78:56](https://ref.ly/Ps78:56); [ISA 1:14](https://ref.ly/Isa1:14), [ISA 7:13](https://ref.ly/Isa7:13), [ISA 43:24](https://ref.ly/Isa43:24)

Examples of God's patience
--------------------------

[GEN 8:22](https://ref.ly/Gen8:22) *with creation*; ; [GEN 18:32](https://ref.ly/Gen18:32) *with the city of Sodom*; ; [1SA 3:10](https://ref.ly/1Sam3:10) *with Samuel*; [EZK 20:17](https://ref.ly/Ezek20:17); ; [MIC 7:19](https://ref.ly/Mic7:19); [JON 3:1](https://ref.ly/Jonah3:1) *with Jonah*

The purpose of God's patience
-----------------------------

### Repentance

**[ROM 2:4](https://ref.ly/Rom2:4)** *See also* [2PE 3:9](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:9)

### Salvation

**[2PE 3:15](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:15)** *See also* [ROM 9:22–9:24](https://ref.ly/Rom9:22-Rom9:24)

* **Associated Passages:** Numbers 14:18; Exodus 34:6; Nehemiah 9:16-17; Psalms 86:15; Psalms 103:8; Psalms 145:8; Joel 2:13; Jonah 4:2; Nahum 1:3; Romans 15:5; Jeremiah 15:15; 2 Thessalonians 3:5; 1 Peter 3:20; Acts 13:18; Deuteronomy 8:2; Nehemiah 9:30; Psalms 78:38; Isaiah 42:14; Nehemiah 9:30-31; Psalms 50:20-21; Isaiah 48:9; Habakkuk 2:3; Malachi 2:17; Genesis 18:16-33; Numbers 14:27; Psalms 78:41; Psalms 78:56; Isaiah 1:14; Isaiah 7:13; Isaiah 43:24; Genesis 8:22; Genesis 18:32; 1 Samuel 3:10; Ezekiel 20:17; Micah 7:19; Jonah 3:1; Romans 2:4; 2 Peter 3:9; 2 Peter 3:15; Romans 9:22-24
* **Associated Articles:** 1030: God, compassion of (ID: `1030@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1055: God, grace and mercy of (ID: `1055@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1085: God, love of (ID: `1085@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2060: Jesus Christ, patience of (ID: `2060@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5482: punishment (ID: `5482@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5883: impatience (ID: `5883@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5977: waiting (ID: `5977@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6020: sin (ID: `6020@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6510: salvation (ID: `6510@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6686: mercy (ID: `6686@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6732: repentance (ID: `6732@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 8318: patience (ID: `8318@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 1100: God, perfection of (id: 1100)

God is complete, faultless and totally sufficient in every aspect of his being and ways. That perfection is made known in Jesus Christ, and is the ultimate goal of the Christian life.

God's moral perfection
----------------------

**[PSA 25:8](https://ref.ly/Ps25:8)** *See also* [EXO 33:19](https://ref.ly/Exod33:19); [PSA 18:25–18:26](https://ref.ly/Ps18:25-Ps18:26), [PSA 92:15](https://ref.ly/Ps92:15); [ISA 26:7](https://ref.ly/Isa26:7); [MRK 10:18](https://ref.ly/Mark10:18) parallel [LUK 18:19](https://ref.ly/Luke18:19)

### Humanity should emulate God's moral perfection

**[MAT 5:48](https://ref.ly/Matt5:48)** *See also* [LEV 19:2](https://ref.ly/Lev19:2), [LEV 11:44–11:45](https://ref.ly/Lev11:44-Lev11:45); [1PE 1:16](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:16); [2CO 7:1](https://ref.ly/2Cor7:1), [2CO 13:11](https://ref.ly/2Cor13:11)

God's work is perfect
---------------------

**[DEU 32:4](https://ref.ly/Deut32:4)** *See also* [2SA 22:31](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:31) parallel [PSA 18:30](https://ref.ly/Ps18:30); [PSA 19:1](https://ref.ly/Ps19:1), [PSA 40:5](https://ref.ly/Ps40:5), [PSA 96:3](https://ref.ly/Ps96:3), [PSA 139:14](https://ref.ly/Ps139:14), [PSA 145:4–145:6](https://ref.ly/Ps145:4-Ps145:6); [JER 32:19–32:20](https://ref.ly/Jer32:19-Jer32:20)

God's will is perfect
---------------------

**[ROM 12:2](https://ref.ly/Rom12:2)** *See also* [PSA 19:7–19:11](https://ref.ly/Ps19:7-Ps19:11)

God's words are perfect
-----------------------

**[PSA 12:6](https://ref.ly/Ps12:6)** *See also* [PSA 18:30](https://ref.ly/Ps18:30); [PRO 30:5](https://ref.ly/Prov30:5)

Humanity cannot always grasp the perfection of God's ways
---------------------------------------------------------

**[JOB 42:3](https://ref.ly/Job42:3)** *See also* [ECC 3:11](https://ref.ly/Eccl3:11); [EZK 18:25](https://ref.ly/Ezek18:25), [EZK 18:29](https://ref.ly/Ezek18:29), [EZK 33:17–33:20](https://ref.ly/Ezek33:17-Ezek33:20)

----------------------------------------

## 1105: God, power of (id: 1105)

God is all\-powerful (that is omnipotent), and is able to do whatever he wills. His power is limited only by his character.

God is all\-powerful
--------------------

**[MRK 10:27](https://ref.ly/Mark10:27)** parallel [MAT 19:26](https://ref.ly/Matt19:26) *See also* [GEN 18:14](https://ref.ly/Gen18:14); [PSA 93:1](https://ref.ly/Ps93:1); [MRK 14:36](https://ref.ly/Mark14:36); [LUK 1:37](https://ref.ly/Luke1:37); [2CO 4:7](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:7)

God cannot be thwarted
----------------------

**[JOB 42:2](https://ref.ly/Job42:2)** *See also* [JOB 9:12](https://ref.ly/Job9:12); [ISA 14:27](https://ref.ly/Isa14:27)

God's names denote his power
----------------------------

### The uniqueness of God's power

**[JER 10:6](https://ref.ly/Jer10:6)**

### He is the Almighty

`the Almighty'' is Hebrew`El Shaddai'': [GEN 28:3](https://ref.ly/Gen28:3), [GEN 35:11](https://ref.ly/Gen35:11), [GEN 43:14](https://ref.ly/Gen43:14); ; [EXO 6:3](https://ref.ly/Exod6:3); ; [JOB 11:7](https://ref.ly/Job11:7), [JOB 31:2](https://ref.ly/Job31:2)

### He is the LORD Almighty and God Almighty

`Almighty'' in these verses is usually Hebrew`Sabaoth'': [PSA 24:10](https://ref.ly/Ps24:10), [PSA 89:8](https://ref.ly/Ps89:8); ; [JER 10:16](https://ref.ly/Jer10:16); ; [2CO 6:18](https://ref.ly/2Cor6:18); ; [REV 11:17](https://ref.ly/Rev11:17), [REV 19:6](https://ref.ly/Rev19:6)

### He is the Mighty One

[GEN 49:24](https://ref.ly/Gen49:24); ; [JOS 22:22](https://ref.ly/Josh22:22); ; [PSA 50:1](https://ref.ly/Ps50:1); ; [ISA 1:24](https://ref.ly/Isa1:24), [ISA 10:21](https://ref.ly/Isa10:21), [ISA 60:16](https://ref.ly/Isa60:16); ; [MRK 14:62](https://ref.ly/Mark14:62); ; [LUK 1:49](https://ref.ly/Luke1:49)

God's power is seen above all in his acts of redemption
-------------------------------------------------------

### God is powerful to save

**[ZEP 3:17](https://ref.ly/Zeph3:17)**

**[ACT 2:24](https://ref.ly/Acts2:24)** *See also* [ROM 1:4](https://ref.ly/Rom1:4); [EPH 1:19–1:21](https://ref.ly/Eph1:19-Eph1:21); [COL 2:13–2:15](https://ref.ly/Col2:13-Col2:15); [REV 12:10](https://ref.ly/Rev12:10)

**[ROM 1:16](https://ref.ly/Rom1:16)** *See also* [1CO 1:18](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:18), [1CO 1:24–1:25](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:24-1Cor1:25); [2CO 10:4](https://ref.ly/2Cor10:4); [COL 2:12](https://ref.ly/Col2:12)

-------------------------------------------

### God's power in Jesus Christ's earthly ministry

### God's power in Jesus Christ's heavenly ministry

**[HEB 7:16](https://ref.ly/Heb7:16)** *In contrast to all other priests, Jesus Christ exercises his ministry now in heaven because death could not hold him.* *See also* [ACT 4:10](https://ref.ly/Acts4:10); [2CO 13:4](https://ref.ly/2Cor13:4)

God's power in the lives of believers
-------------------------------------

### God gives his own power to his people

**[1CH 29:11–29:12](https://ref.ly/1Chr29:11-1Chr29:12)** *See also* [1SA 2:10](https://ref.ly/1Sam2:10); [DAN 2:27–2:28](https://ref.ly/Dan2:27-Dan2:28); [2CO 13:3–13:4](https://ref.ly/2Cor13:3-2Cor13:4); [PHP 4:13](https://ref.ly/Phil4:13); [2TI 1:7](https://ref.ly/2Tim1:7); [1PE 4:11](https://ref.ly/1Pet4:11)

**[2TH 1:11](https://ref.ly/2Thess1:11)** *See also* [MIC 5:4](https://ref.ly/Mic5:4); [ACT 4:28](https://ref.ly/Acts4:28); [1CO 5:4](https://ref.ly/1Cor5:4); [EPH 1:20–1:21](https://ref.ly/Eph1:20-Eph1:21)

### God's power completes his work of salvation in believers' lives

**[1PE 1:5](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:5)** *See also* [2TI 1:12](https://ref.ly/2Tim1:12); [HEB 7:25](https://ref.ly/Heb7:25); [JUD 1:24](https://ref.ly/Jude1:24)

### God's power gives believers inner strength

**[EPH 3:16–3:17](https://ref.ly/Eph3:16-Eph3:17)** *See also* [EPH 1:18–1:19](https://ref.ly/Eph1:18-Eph1:19), [EPH 6:10](https://ref.ly/Eph6:10); [PHP 3:10](https://ref.ly/Phil3:10); [COL 1:11](https://ref.ly/Col1:11)

### God's power is made plain through human weakness

**[2CO 12:9–12:10](https://ref.ly/2Cor12:9-2Cor12:10)** *See also* [ISA 53:1–53:3](https://ref.ly/Isa53:1-Isa53:3); [2CO 4:7](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:7), [2CO 13:4](https://ref.ly/2Cor13:4)

**[2TI 4:16–4:17](https://ref.ly/2Tim4:16-2Tim4:17)** *See also* [2CH 25:8](https://ref.ly/2Chr25:8); [PSA 46:1](https://ref.ly/Ps46:1); [DAN 3:17](https://ref.ly/Dan3:17); [2CO 6:7](https://ref.ly/2Cor6:7); [2TI 1:8](https://ref.ly/2Tim1:8)

--------------------------------------------

### God cannot deny himself

### God cannot tolerate evil

**[HAB 1:13](https://ref.ly/Hab1:13)**

### God cannot be tempted

**[JAS 1:13](https://ref.ly/Jas1:13)**

**[NUM 23:19](https://ref.ly/Num23:19)** *See also* [1SA 15:29](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:29); [HEB 6:18](https://ref.ly/Heb6:18)

God's power is to be praised

## 1110: God, present everywhere (id: 1110)

God is omnipresent in that he transcends all limitations of space and is present in the fulness of his being in every place but in varying ways.

God transcends all spatial limitations
--------------------------------------

**[1KI 8:27](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:27)** parallel [2CH 6:18](https://ref.ly/2Chr6:18) *See also* [2CH 2:6](https://ref.ly/2Chr2:6); [PSA 113:4–113:6](https://ref.ly/Ps113:4-Ps113:6)

God is present throughout heaven and earth
------------------------------------------

**[PSA 139:7–139:12](https://ref.ly/Ps139:7-Ps139:12)**; **[JER 23:23–23:24](https://ref.ly/Jer23:23-Jer23:24)** *See also* [NUM 14:21](https://ref.ly/Num14:21); [DEU 4:39](https://ref.ly/Deut4:39); [ISA 6:3](https://ref.ly/Isa6:3), [ISA 66:1](https://ref.ly/Isa66:1); [AMO 9:2–9:3](https://ref.ly/Amos9:2-Amos9:3)

God sees and knows everything
-----------------------------

**[PRO 15:3](https://ref.ly/Prov15:3)** *See also* [2CH 16:9](https://ref.ly/2Chr16:9); [ZEC 4:10](https://ref.ly/Zech4:10)

God is near to all human beings
-------------------------------

**[ACT 17:27–17:28](https://ref.ly/Acts17:27-Acts17:28)**

God is present with special groups of people
--------------------------------------------

### God is especially close to the poor and needy

**[PSA 34:18](https://ref.ly/Ps34:18)** *See also* [ISA 57:15](https://ref.ly/Isa57:15)

### God is especially close to those who call on him

**[PSA 145:18](https://ref.ly/Ps145:18)** *See also* [PSA 16:8](https://ref.ly/Ps16:8); [ISA 50:8](https://ref.ly/Isa50:8)

------------------------------

## 1115: God, purpose of (id: 1115)

God has a plan for his creation which he will certainly accomplish. It is carried out through the control of circumstances and his choice and use of people, and above all in the life, death, resurrection and second coming of Jesus Christ.

God's purpose will be accomplished
----------------------------------

**[ISA 46:10–46:11](https://ref.ly/Isa46:10-Isa46:11)** *See also* [PSA 135:6](https://ref.ly/Ps135:6); [PRO 16:4](https://ref.ly/Prov16:4); [ECC 3:14](https://ref.ly/Eccl3:14); [ISA 14:24](https://ref.ly/Isa14:24), [ISA 14:26–14:27](https://ref.ly/Isa14:26-Isa14:27), [ISA 25:1](https://ref.ly/Isa25:1), [ISA 55:11](https://ref.ly/Isa55:11); [EPH 1:11](https://ref.ly/Eph1:11)

God's purpose prevails
----------------------

### It stands for ever

**[PSA 33:11](https://ref.ly/Ps33:11)** *See also* [JOB 42:2](https://ref.ly/Job42:2); [JER 23:20](https://ref.ly/Jer23:20)

### It cannot be thwarted by human beings

**[PRO 19:21](https://ref.ly/Prov19:21)** *See also* [JOB 9:12](https://ref.ly/Job9:12), [JOB 23:13](https://ref.ly/Job23:13); [ISA 8:10](https://ref.ly/Isa8:10); [DAN 4:35](https://ref.ly/Dan4:35)

### It cannot be thwarted by evil powers

**[REV 17:17](https://ref.ly/Rev17:17)** *See also* [1SA 16:14](https://ref.ly/1Sam16:14) *The implication is that evil is subject to God's control and operates within the determined limits of his sovereign purpose*; [JOB 1:12](https://ref.ly/Job1:12), [JOB 2:6](https://ref.ly/Job2:6); [2CO 12:7](https://ref.ly/2Cor12:7)

### It prevails in people's lives and circumstances

**[PRO 16:9](https://ref.ly/Prov16:9)** *See also* [PRO 20:24](https://ref.ly/Prov20:24), [PRO 21:1](https://ref.ly/Prov21:1)

### It is fulfilled through his choice of individuals

**[EPH 1:11](https://ref.ly/Eph1:11)** *God's choice of individuals does not invalidate their free will to do or not to do anything, nor remove their answerability to God for their actions.* *See also* [GEN 18:19](https://ref.ly/Gen18:19); [ROM 11:5](https://ref.ly/Rom11:5); [1CO 1:1](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:1); [EPH 1:4–1:5](https://ref.ly/Eph1:4-Eph1:5); [2TH 2:13](https://ref.ly/2Thess2:13)

### Examples of the actions of evil people serving God's purpose

**[ACT 2:23](https://ref.ly/Acts2:23)** *See also* [GEN 50:20](https://ref.ly/Gen50:20); [ISA 10:5–10:7](https://ref.ly/Isa10:5-Isa10:7)

God's purpose is founded on divine wisdom
-----------------------------------------

**[EPH 3:10–3:11](https://ref.ly/Eph3:10-Eph3:11)** *See also* [PSA 104:24](https://ref.ly/Ps104:24); [ROM 11:33](https://ref.ly/Rom11:33)

God's purpose is determined from eternity
-----------------------------------------

**[2TI 1:9](https://ref.ly/2Tim1:9)** *See also* [2KI 19:25](https://ref.ly/2Kgs19:25); [ISA 25:1](https://ref.ly/Isa25:1), [ISA 46:10](https://ref.ly/Isa46:10); [MAT 25:34](https://ref.ly/Matt25:34); [EPH 1:4](https://ref.ly/Eph1:4); [TIT 1:2](https://ref.ly/Titus1:2); [1PE 1:20](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:20)

God's purpose is for his own glory
----------------------------------

**[EXO 9:16](https://ref.ly/Exod9:16)** *See also* [ROM 9:17](https://ref.ly/Rom9:17); [EZK 36:22–36:23](https://ref.ly/Ezek36:22-Ezek36:23); [EPH 1:5–1:6](https://ref.ly/Eph1:5-Eph1:6), [EPH 1:11–1:12](https://ref.ly/Eph1:11-Eph1:12)

God's purpose for his people
----------------------------

### God reveals his purpose to his people

**[AMO 3:7](https://ref.ly/Amos3:7)** *See also* [GEN 18:17](https://ref.ly/Gen18:17); [2SA 7:20–7:21](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:20-2Sam7:21); [1CO 2:9–2:10](https://ref.ly/1Cor2:9-1Cor2:10); [EPH 1:9](https://ref.ly/Eph1:9)

### Its fulness is beyond human understanding

**[ROM 11:33](https://ref.ly/Rom11:33)** *See also* [DEU 29:29](https://ref.ly/Deut29:29); [1CO 2:9–2:10](https://ref.ly/1Cor2:9-1Cor2:10); [EPH 1:9](https://ref.ly/Eph1:9), [EPH 3:4–3:5](https://ref.ly/Eph3:4-Eph3:5)

**[ROM 8:28](https://ref.ly/Rom8:28)** *See also* [JER 29:11](https://ref.ly/Jer29:11); [ROM 12:2](https://ref.ly/Rom12:2); [EPH 1:4–1:5](https://ref.ly/Eph1:4-Eph1:5); [2TI 1:9](https://ref.ly/2Tim1:9)

God's purpose is revealed through Jesus Christ
----------------------------------------------

### In the church

**[EPH 3:10–3:11](https://ref.ly/Eph3:10-Eph3:11)**

### It centres on the cross

**[ISA 53:10](https://ref.ly/Isa53:10)** *See also* [ACT 4:27–4:28](https://ref.ly/Acts4:27-Acts4:28); [1PE 1:19–1:20](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:19-1Pet1:20); [1JN 4:10](https://ref.ly/1John4:10)

### It is God's purpose to redeem the world through the cross

[MAT 26:18](https://ref.ly/Matt26:18), [MAT 26:45](https://ref.ly/Matt26:45) parallel [MRK 14:41](https://ref.ly/Mark14:41) *Jesus Christ often speaks of his appointed “hour”. In John's Gospel in particular his “hour” refers to the cross. Jesus Christ refuses to allow anything except the cross to be the climax of his ministry ([Jn 12:27](https://ref.ly/John12:27)).*; ; [JHN 7:6–7:8](https://ref.ly/John7:6-John7:8), [JHN 12:23](https://ref.ly/John12:23), [JHN 13:1](https://ref.ly/John13:1), [JHN 17:1](https://ref.ly/John17:1)

### It is God's purpose to exalt and establish Jesus Christ as Lord

**[EPH 1:9–1:10](https://ref.ly/Eph1:9-Eph1:10)** *See also* [ACT 2:36](https://ref.ly/Acts2:36); [PHP 2:8–2:11](https://ref.ly/Phil2:8-Phil2:11); [COL 1:18](https://ref.ly/Col1:18); [HEB 1:2–1:4](https://ref.ly/Heb1:2-Heb1:4)

### Jesus Christ submits to God's purpose

**[JHN 6:38](https://ref.ly/John6:38)** *See also* [MAT 26:39–26:42](https://ref.ly/Matt26:39-Matt26:42) parallels [MRK 14:35–14:36](https://ref.ly/Mark14:35-Mark14:36), [LUK 22:42](https://ref.ly/Luke22:42); [JHN 4:34](https://ref.ly/John4:34), [JHN 5:30](https://ref.ly/John5:30); [HEB 5:7–5:8](https://ref.ly/Heb5:7-Heb5:8), [HEB 10:7](https://ref.ly/Heb10:7)

God's ultimate purpose is to save
---------------------------------

### The salvation of people through Jesus Christ

**[JHN 6:40](https://ref.ly/John6:40)** *See also* [JHN 3:16–3:17](https://ref.ly/John3:16-John3:17); [GAL 1:3–1:4](https://ref.ly/Gal1:3-Gal1:4); [1TI 2:3–2:4](https://ref.ly/1Tim2:3-1Tim2:4); [1PE 1:2](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:2); [2PE 3:9](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:9)

### Specific aspects of God's purpose in salvation

[2CO 5:5](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:5) *knowing heavenly life*; ; [ROM 8:29](https://ref.ly/Rom8:29) *being conformed to Jesus Christ*; ; [EPH 1:4](https://ref.ly/Eph1:4) *being holy and blameless*; ; [EPH 2:15](https://ref.ly/Eph2:15) *becoming unified*; ; [EPH 3:10–3:11](https://ref.ly/Eph3:10-Eph3:11) *that the wisdom of God be revealed*

God wills that people submit to his purposes
--------------------------------------------

**[JAS 4:15](https://ref.ly/Jas4:15)** *See also* [PSA 40:8](https://ref.ly/Ps40:8), [PSA 143:10](https://ref.ly/Ps143:10); [MAT 6:10](https://ref.ly/Matt6:10)

God's people should pray for the fulfilment of his purposes
-----------------------------------------------------------

**[MAT 6:9–6:10](https://ref.ly/Matt6:9-Matt6:10)** parallel [LUK 11:2](https://ref.ly/Luke11:2)

People can reject God's purposes in their lives
-----------------------------------------------

## 1120: God, repentance of (id: 1120)

A change in God's plan or intention, often in response to human repentance, but without implying any fault or moral imperfection on God's part.

God's repentance may show his pain and sorrow
---------------------------------------------

**[GEN 6:6–6:7](https://ref.ly/Gen6:6-Gen6:7)** *God's change of purpose here involves his intention to punish.* *See also* [1SA 15:11](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:11), [1SA 15:35](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:35)

God's repentance may show his compassion
----------------------------------------

**[JON 4:2](https://ref.ly/Jonah4:2)** *God's change of purpose here involves his compassion for sinners: “relent” in this and other passages may also be translated “repent”.* *See also* [DEU 32:36](https://ref.ly/Deut32:36); [2SA 24:15–24:16](https://ref.ly/2Sam24:15-2Sam24:16) parallel [1CH 21:14–21:15](https://ref.ly/1Chr21:14-1Chr21:15); [PSA 106:45](https://ref.ly/Ps106:45); [ISA 38:1–38:5](https://ref.ly/Isa38:1-Isa38:5); [HOS 11:8](https://ref.ly/Hos11:8); [AMO 7:1–7:6](https://ref.ly/Amos7:1-Amos7:6)

### God may repent in response to human repentance

**[JER 18:8](https://ref.ly/Jer18:8)** *See also* [EXO 32:14](https://ref.ly/Exod32:14); [2CH 12:1–12:8](https://ref.ly/2Chr12:1-2Chr12:8); [JER 26:13](https://ref.ly/Jer26:13), [JER 26:19](https://ref.ly/Jer26:19); [JOL 2:13](https://ref.ly/Joel2:13); [JON 3:6–3:10](https://ref.ly/Jonah3:6-Jonah3:10)

God never repents of his oath or changes his character
------------------------------------------------------

## 1125: God, righteousness of (id: 1125)

An aspect of God's nature which expresses his unique moral perfection and his readiness to save sinners. It is made known especially through the gospel of Jesus Christ.

God's nature is righteous
-------------------------

**[PSA 119:137](https://ref.ly/Ps119:137)** *See also* [DEU 32:4](https://ref.ly/Deut32:4); [PSA 48:10](https://ref.ly/Ps48:10), [PSA 97:2](https://ref.ly/Ps97:2), [PSA 119:142](https://ref.ly/Ps119:142), [PSA 145:17](https://ref.ly/Ps145:17); [ISA 45:21](https://ref.ly/Isa45:21); [JER 12:1](https://ref.ly/Jer12:1); [JHN 17:25](https://ref.ly/John17:25)

## 1130: God, sovereignty of (id: 1130)

The fact that God is free and able to do all that he wills; that he reigns over all creation and that his will is the final cause of all things. This is often expressed in the language of kingship.

God is free to do all he wills
------------------------------

**[PSA 135:6](https://ref.ly/Ps135:6)** *See also* [PSA 115:3](https://ref.ly/Ps115:3); [ISA 46:10](https://ref.ly/Isa46:10); [DAN 4:35](https://ref.ly/Dan4:35); [ROM 9:19–9:21](https://ref.ly/Rom9:19-Rom9:21)

God is able to do whatever he wills
-----------------------------------

**[LUK 1:37](https://ref.ly/Luke1:37)** *Gabriel speaking to Mary.* *See also* [JOB 42:2](https://ref.ly/Job42:2); [MAT 19:26](https://ref.ly/Matt19:26); [EPH 3:20](https://ref.ly/Eph3:20)

God cannot be successfully opposed
----------------------------------

**[JOB 42:2](https://ref.ly/Job42:2)** *From Job's prayer of submission and repentance.* *See also* [1SA 2:10](https://ref.ly/1Sam2:10); [2CH 20:6](https://ref.ly/2Chr20:6); [JOB 9:12](https://ref.ly/Job9:12); [ECC 7:13](https://ref.ly/Eccl7:13); [ISA 43:13](https://ref.ly/Isa43:13), [ISA 45:9–45:10](https://ref.ly/Isa45:9-Isa45:10); [ACT 5:39](https://ref.ly/Acts5:39)

--------------------

### He is King

## 1135: God, suffering of (id: 1135)

God suffers on account of the failures and pain of his people, and especially through his Son, Jesus Christ. Scripture often likens God to a parent who suffers pain and grief on account of children.

God feels real suffering
------------------------

### He suffers pain because people sin

**[GEN 6:6](https://ref.ly/Gen6:6)** *See also* [1SA 15:10–15:11](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:10-1Sam15:11), [1SA 15:35](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:35)

### He is angered because people sin

**[PSA 78:58](https://ref.ly/Ps78:58)** *See also* [DEU 32:15–32:16](https://ref.ly/Deut32:15-Deut32:16); [JDG 2:12–2:13](https://ref.ly/Judg2:12-Judg2:13); [1KI 21:22](https://ref.ly/1Kgs21:22); [EZK 8:17](https://ref.ly/Ezek8:17); [HOS 12:14](https://ref.ly/Hos12:14)

God identifies with suffering
-----------------------------

### He suffers with his chosen people

**[ISA 63:9](https://ref.ly/Isa63:9)** *See also* [EXO 3:7](https://ref.ly/Exod3:7); [JDG 10:16](https://ref.ly/Judg10:16); [2CH 36:15](https://ref.ly/2Chr36:15)

### He suffers with all humanity

**[ISA 16:11](https://ref.ly/Isa16:11)** parallel [JER 48:31](https://ref.ly/Jer48:31) *See also* [2SA 24:15–24:17](https://ref.ly/2Sam24:15-2Sam24:17) parallel [1CH 21:14–21:17](https://ref.ly/1Chr21:14-1Chr21:17) *God suffers even with those who endure punishment from his own hand*; [ISA 16:9](https://ref.ly/Isa16:9); [JER 48:32–48:36](https://ref.ly/Jer48:32-Jer48:36); [HOS 11:8–11:9](https://ref.ly/Hos11:8-Hos11:9)

### He suffers as a parent

**[JER 31:20](https://ref.ly/Jer31:20)** *An indication that God suffers in both disciplining and loving.* *See also* [ISA 42:14](https://ref.ly/Isa42:14), [ISA 49:15](https://ref.ly/Isa49:15); [HOS 11:1–11:4](https://ref.ly/Hos11:1-Hos11:4)

God's plan of salvation causes him suffering
--------------------------------------------

### He suffered in giving his Son

## 1150: God, truth of (id: 1150)

God's unique integrity is displayed in his perfection of character and attributes. It is further emphasised by the consistent truth of his words and works, supremely shown in Jesus Christ.

God is the one and only true God
--------------------------------

### He alone is God

## 1155: God, truthfulness of (id: 1155)

To call the LORD “the true God” means that he alone has in his being the fulness of deity and is worthy to be worshipped as God. He and his word are a trustworthy foundation for life because he speaks the truth and is utterly reliable and consistent in his character, his revelation of himself, his promises and his pronouncements.

Titles reflecting God's truthfulness
------------------------------------

### The true God

[2CH 15:3](https://ref.ly/2Chr15:3); ; [JER 10:10](https://ref.ly/Jer10:10); ; [1TH 1:9](https://ref.ly/1Thess1:9)

### The God of truth

[PSA 31:5](https://ref.ly/Ps31:5); ; [ISA 65:16](https://ref.ly/Isa65:16)

### Jesus Christ is \`\`the truth''

**[JHN 14:6](https://ref.ly/John14:6)** *See also* [JHN 1:14](https://ref.ly/John1:14), [JHN 1:17](https://ref.ly/John1:17), [JHN 6:32](https://ref.ly/John6:32) *Jesus Christ calls himself “the true bread” meaning that he is real, substantial, reliable and life\-giving*; [1JN 5:20](https://ref.ly/1John5:20); [REV 3:7](https://ref.ly/Rev3:7), [REV 3:14](https://ref.ly/Rev3:14)

### The Spirit of truth

[JHN 14:17](https://ref.ly/John14:17), [JHN 15:26](https://ref.ly/John15:26), [JHN 16:13](https://ref.ly/John16:13); ; [1JN 4:6](https://ref.ly/1John4:6), [1JN 5:6](https://ref.ly/1John5:6)

God is true to his character and his word
-----------------------------------------

### He speaks the truth

**[ISA 45:19](https://ref.ly/Isa45:19)** *See also* [2SA 7:28](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:28); [PSA 33:4](https://ref.ly/Ps33:4), [PSA 119:160](https://ref.ly/Ps119:160); [JHN 17:17](https://ref.ly/John17:17); [REV 21:5](https://ref.ly/Rev21:5), [REV 22:6](https://ref.ly/Rev22:6)

### He does not lie

**[NUM 23:19](https://ref.ly/Num23:19)** *See also* [ROM 3:4](https://ref.ly/Rom3:4); [2TI 2:13](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:13); [TIT 1:2](https://ref.ly/Titus1:2); [HEB 6:18](https://ref.ly/Heb6:18)

### He is true to himself and his promises

[DEU 32:4](https://ref.ly/Deut32:4); ; [PSA 25:10](https://ref.ly/Ps25:10), [PSA 33:4](https://ref.ly/Ps33:4), [PSA 145:13](https://ref.ly/Ps145:13), [PSA 146:6](https://ref.ly/Ps146:6); ; [LAM 3:23](https://ref.ly/Lam3:23); ; [2TI 2:13](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:13)

The truthfulness of God undergirds the law
------------------------------------------

**[PSA 119:142](https://ref.ly/Ps119:142)** *See also* [PSA 19:7](https://ref.ly/Ps19:7), [PSA 119:151](https://ref.ly/Ps119:151), [PSA 119:160](https://ref.ly/Ps119:160); [MAL 2:6–2:7](https://ref.ly/Mal2:6-Mal2:7)

The truthfulness of God undergirds the covenant
-----------------------------------------------

The word is particularly associated with God steadfastly upholding his covenant promises.* *See also* [PSA 145:13](https://ref.ly/Ps145:13); [HOS 2:19–2:20](https://ref.ly/Hos2:19-Hos2:20); [2TI 2:13](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:13)

-----------------------------------------------------

-----------------------------------------------

## 1160: God, unchangeableness of (id: 1160)

God's nature, plans and actions do not change even though he is active and his relationships do not remain static. His moral consistency guarantees his commitment to unchanging principles.

God's being is unchangeable
---------------------------

**[PSA 102:27](https://ref.ly/Ps102:27)** *See also* [HEB 1:12](https://ref.ly/Heb1:12); [MAL 3:6](https://ref.ly/Mal3:6); [HEB 13:8](https://ref.ly/Heb13:8); [JAS 1:17](https://ref.ly/Jas1:17)

God's characteristics do not change
-----------------------------------

### God's love is constant

**[PSA 89:2](https://ref.ly/Ps89:2)** *See also* [PSA 136:1–136:26](https://ref.ly/Ps136:1-Ps136:26); [2TI 2:13](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:13)

God's purposes and plans do not change
--------------------------------------

**[HEB 6:17](https://ref.ly/Heb6:17)** *See also* [NUM 23:19](https://ref.ly/Num23:19); [1SA 15:29](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:29); [PRO 19:21](https://ref.ly/Prov19:21); [JER 44:29](https://ref.ly/Jer44:29); [HEB 7:21](https://ref.ly/Heb7:21); [PSA 110:4](https://ref.ly/Ps110:4)

God does not revoke his promises
--------------------------------

**[PSA 132:11](https://ref.ly/Ps132:11)** *See also* [PSA 145:13](https://ref.ly/Ps145:13); [HEB 4:1](https://ref.ly/Heb4:1)

God's word does not change
--------------------------

**[ISA 40:8](https://ref.ly/Isa40:8)** *See also* [PSA 119:89](https://ref.ly/Ps119:89); [MAT 5:18](https://ref.ly/Matt5:18); [1PE 1:23–1:25](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:23-1Pet1:25)

God's failure to inflict promised judgment is a sign of his unchanging grace
----------------------------------------------------------------------------

**[HOS 11:8](https://ref.ly/Hos11:8)** *See also* [EXO 32:10–32:14](https://ref.ly/Exod32:10-Exod32:14); [JON 3:10](https://ref.ly/Jonah3:10), [JON 4:2](https://ref.ly/Jonah4:2)

* **Associated Passages:** Psalms 102:27; Hebrews 1:12; Malachi 3:6; Hebrews 13:8; James 1:17; Psalms 89:2; Psalms 136:1-26; 2 Timothy 2:13; Hebrews 6:17; Numbers 23:19; 1 Samuel 15:29; Proverbs 19:21; Jeremiah 44:29; Hebrews 7:21; Psalms 110:4; Psalms 132:11; Psalms 145:13; Hebrews 4:1; Isaiah 40:8; Psalms 119:89; Matthew 5:18; 1 Peter 1:23-25; Hosea 11:8; Exodus 32:10-14; Jonah 3:10; Jonah 4:2

## 1165: God, uniqueness of (id: 1165)

No\-one and nothing is comparable to the triune God in his nature or comparable to him in his character and activity.

There is no God except the LORD
-------------------------------

**[ISA 45:5–45:6](https://ref.ly/Isa45:5-Isa45:6)** *God alone stands outside nature as its Creator. All other beings are created by him.* *See also* [DEU 4:35](https://ref.ly/Deut4:35), [DEU 6:4](https://ref.ly/Deut6:4), [DEU 32:3](https://ref.ly/Deut32:3); [1KI 8:60](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:60); [PSA 83:18](https://ref.ly/Ps83:18), [PSA 86:10](https://ref.ly/Ps86:10); [ISA 43:10–43:11](https://ref.ly/Isa43:10-Isa43:11), [ISA 44:6–44:8](https://ref.ly/Isa44:6-Isa44:8), [ISA 45:18](https://ref.ly/Isa45:18); [1CO 8:4–8:6](https://ref.ly/1Cor8:4-1Cor8:6); [EPH 4:6](https://ref.ly/Eph4:6); [1TI 2:5](https://ref.ly/1Tim2:5)

There is no\-one like God
