## 1170: God, unity of (id: 1170)

God acts as a unity in all his deeds. The three persons of the Trinity are united in one Godhead. They are interrelated with one another, share the same attributes and co\-operate in the same work. God's characteristics are consistent, expressing his integral divine nature.

God is one
----------

**[DEU 6:4](https://ref.ly/Deut6:4)** *See also* [MRK 12:29](https://ref.ly/Mark12:29), [MRK 12:32](https://ref.ly/Mark12:32); [1CO 8:4](https://ref.ly/1Cor8:4); [GAL 3:20](https://ref.ly/Gal3:20); [EPH 4:5–4:6](https://ref.ly/Eph4:5-Eph4:6); [1TI 2:5](https://ref.ly/1Tim2:5); [JAS 2:19](https://ref.ly/Jas2:19)

The three persons of the Trinity are united in one Godhead
----------------------------------------------------------

### All three are interrelated

**[ROM 8:9–8:11](https://ref.ly/Rom8:9-Rom8:11)** *The interchange between the persons of the Trinity reflects their unity in terms of activity.* *See also* [JHN 14:23](https://ref.ly/John14:23); [2CO 13:14](https://ref.ly/2Cor13:14); [EPH 2:18](https://ref.ly/Eph2:18); [1PE 1:2](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:2)

### The Son is one with the Father

**[JHN 10:30](https://ref.ly/John10:30)** *See also* [MAT 10:40](https://ref.ly/Matt10:40); [MRK 9:37](https://ref.ly/Mark9:37) parallel [LUK 9:48](https://ref.ly/Luke9:48); [LUK 10:16](https://ref.ly/Luke10:16); [JHN 8:16](https://ref.ly/John8:16), [JHN 14:9](https://ref.ly/John14:9)

### The Spirit is one with God

**[2SA 23:2–23:3](https://ref.ly/2Sam23:2-2Sam23:3)** *See also* [PSA 51:11](https://ref.ly/Ps51:11); [1CO 3:16](https://ref.ly/1Cor3:16)

The three persons are one in character
--------------------------------------

### All three are eternal

[ROM 16:26](https://ref.ly/Rom16:26) *the Father*; ; [ISA 9:6](https://ref.ly/Isa9:6) *the Son*; ; [HEB 9:14](https://ref.ly/Heb9:14) *the Spirit*

### All three are all\-knowing

[ISA 40:13–40:14](https://ref.ly/Isa40:13-Isa40:14) *the Father*; [JHN 2:24–2:25](https://ref.ly/John2:24-John2:25), [JHN 21:17](https://ref.ly/John21:17); [1CO 2:10–2:11](https://ref.ly/1Cor2:10-1Cor2:11) *the Spirit*

### All three are holy

[JHN 17:11](https://ref.ly/John17:11) *the Father*; [MRK 1:24](https://ref.ly/Mark1:24); ; [ACT 3:14](https://ref.ly/Acts3:14); [JHN 14:26](https://ref.ly/John14:26); ; [ROM 1:4](https://ref.ly/Rom1:4)

### All three are called Lord and God

The Father: [MAT 11:25](https://ref.ly/Matt11:25); ; [ACT 3:22](https://ref.ly/Acts3:22); ; [1CO 8:6](https://ref.ly/1Cor8:6); [JHN 1:1](https://ref.ly/John1:1), [JHN 20:28](https://ref.ly/John20:28); ; [ACT 10:36](https://ref.ly/Acts10:36); ; [2PE 1:1](https://ref.ly/2Pet1:1); [ACT 5:3–5:4](https://ref.ly/Acts5:3-Acts5:4); ; [2CO 3:17–3:18](https://ref.ly/2Cor3:17-2Cor3:18)

### All three are glorious

The Father: [ACT 7:2](https://ref.ly/Acts7:2); ; [EPH 1:17](https://ref.ly/Eph1:17); [JHN 1:14](https://ref.ly/John1:14), [JHN 12:41](https://ref.ly/John12:41); [2CO 3:8](https://ref.ly/2Cor3:8), [2CO 3:18](https://ref.ly/2Cor3:18); ; [1PE 4:14](https://ref.ly/1Pet4:14)

The three persons share in the same work
----------------------------------------

### In creation

**[GEN 1:1–1:3](https://ref.ly/Gen1:1-Gen1:3)** *See also* [PSA 33:6](https://ref.ly/Ps33:6), [PSA 104:30](https://ref.ly/Ps104:30); [JHN 1:3–1:4](https://ref.ly/John1:3-John1:4); [COL 1:16](https://ref.ly/Col1:16)

### In Jesus Christ's ministry

**[JHN 3:34](https://ref.ly/John3:34)** *See also* [ACT 10:38](https://ref.ly/Acts10:38)

### In salvation

**[1PE 1:2](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:2)** *See also* [2CO 1:21–1:22](https://ref.ly/2Cor1:21-2Cor1:22); [TIT 3:4–3:6](https://ref.ly/Titus3:4-Titus3:6)

### In indwelling the church

**[EPH 2:22](https://ref.ly/Eph2:22)** [1CO 3:16](https://ref.ly/1Cor3:16), [1CO 6:19](https://ref.ly/1Cor6:19); [GAL 2:20](https://ref.ly/Gal2:20); ; [EPH 3:17](https://ref.ly/Eph3:17)

God's characteristics are consistent
------------------------------------

### His love and justice are in unity

**[EXO 34:6–34:7](https://ref.ly/Exod34:6-Exod34:7)** *See also* [2SA 7:14–7:15](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:14-2Sam7:15); [PSA 103:6–103:8](https://ref.ly/Ps103:6-Ps103:8); [ROM 3:25–3:26](https://ref.ly/Rom3:25-Rom3:26)

## 1175: God, will of (id: 1175)

The intent and purpose of God, as revealed in Scripture. God's will for his creation and his people is set out in the Law and the Prophets, which find their fulfilment in Jesus Christ. A central aspect of the will of God is that his people be faithful and obedient.

The revelation of God's will
----------------------------

### In his word

**[2TI 3:16](https://ref.ly/2Tim3:16)** *See also* [2SA 7:21](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:21) parallel [1CH 17:19](https://ref.ly/1Chr17:19); [PSA 103:20–103:21](https://ref.ly/Ps103:20-Ps103:21); [COL 1:25–1:26](https://ref.ly/Col1:25-Col1:26); [1JN 2:4–2:5](https://ref.ly/1John2:4-1John2:5)

### Through the law

[EXO 18:15–18:16](https://ref.ly/Exod18:15-Exod18:16), [EXO 24:12](https://ref.ly/Exod24:12); ; [DEU 30:16](https://ref.ly/Deut30:16); ; [PSA 119:43](https://ref.ly/Ps119:43); ; [ROM 7:12](https://ref.ly/Rom7:12); ; [1TI 1:8](https://ref.ly/1Tim1:8)

### Through the prophets

[1KI 22:6–22:7](https://ref.ly/1Kgs22:6-1Kgs22:7) parallel [2CH 18:5–18:6](https://ref.ly/2Chr18:5-2Chr18:6); ; [2KI 3:11](https://ref.ly/2Kgs3:11); ; [JER 42:3–42:4](https://ref.ly/Jer42:3-Jer42:4); ; [EZK 12:25](https://ref.ly/Ezek12:25); ; [AMO 3:7](https://ref.ly/Amos3:7)

### In the apostolic gospel

[ACT 20:27](https://ref.ly/Acts20:27); ; [GAL 1:11–1:12](https://ref.ly/Gal1:11-Gal1:12)

The fulfilment of God's will
----------------------------

### God's will is fulfilled in Jesus Christ

**[EPH 1:9–1:10](https://ref.ly/Eph1:9-Eph1:10)** *See also* [EPH 3:4–3:11](https://ref.ly/Eph3:4-Eph3:11); [COL 1:27](https://ref.ly/Col1:27)

### Jesus Christ obeyed his Father's will

**[JHN 6:38](https://ref.ly/John6:38)** *See also* [MAT 26:39](https://ref.ly/Matt26:39) parallels [MRK 14:36](https://ref.ly/Mark14:36), [LUK 22:42](https://ref.ly/Luke22:42); [JHN 4:34](https://ref.ly/John4:34), [JHN 5:30](https://ref.ly/John5:30); [HEB 10:7](https://ref.ly/Heb10:7); [PSA 40:8](https://ref.ly/Ps40:8)

### Jesus Christ's death fulfilled God's will

**[GAL 1:3–1:4](https://ref.ly/Gal1:3-Gal1:4)** *See also* [ISA 53:10](https://ref.ly/Isa53:10); [ACT 2:23](https://ref.ly/Acts2:23)

God's will for the world
------------------------

## 1180: God, wisdom of (id: 1180)

Scripture declares that God alone is wise and discerning, and that human wisdom is often unable or unwilling to understand his ways. God's wisdom is expressed in both creation and redemption.

God's wisdom described
----------------------

**[ISA 28:29](https://ref.ly/Isa28:29)** *See also* [1SA 2:3](https://ref.ly/1Sam2:3); [ROM 16:27](https://ref.ly/Rom16:27)

### God's wisdom is beyond measure

**[PSA 147:5](https://ref.ly/Ps147:5)** *See also* [ISA 44:7](https://ref.ly/Isa44:7); [JER 10:7](https://ref.ly/Jer10:7); [ROM 11:33](https://ref.ly/Rom11:33)

**[ISA 40:28](https://ref.ly/Isa40:28)** *See also* [JOB 9:4](https://ref.ly/Job9:4), [JOB 28:12–28:24](https://ref.ly/Job28:12-Job28:24); [PSA 92:5](https://ref.ly/Ps92:5); [ECC 8:17](https://ref.ly/Eccl8:17)

### God's wisdom is superior to human wisdom

**[ISA 55:9](https://ref.ly/Isa55:9)** *See also* [JOB 21:22](https://ref.ly/Job21:22)

----------------------

**[JER 10:12](https://ref.ly/Jer10:12)** *See also* [JOB 28:25–28:27](https://ref.ly/Job28:25-Job28:27), [JOB 37:14–37:16](https://ref.ly/Job37:14-Job37:16); [PSA 104:24](https://ref.ly/Ps104:24), [PSA 136:5](https://ref.ly/Ps136:5); [PRO 3:19–3:20](https://ref.ly/Prov3:19-Prov3:20); [ISA 40:12–40:14](https://ref.ly/Isa40:12-Isa40:14)

## 1185: God, zeal of (id: 1185)

The intense and protective commitment of God to his people and to his purposes which seeks a passionate and obedient response. The zeal of God is often linked with the idea of the “jealousy of God”, in which God refuses to contemplate his people giving their allegiance or affection to another.

God in his zeal demands exclusive loyalty from his people
---------------------------------------------------------

**[EXO 20:5](https://ref.ly/Exod20:5)** *The jealousy of God implies that he seeks for and insists on exclusive loyalty which is due to him and which will benefit those who give it.* *See also* [EXO 34:14](https://ref.ly/Exod34:14); [DEU 4:24](https://ref.ly/Deut4:24), [DEU 5:9](https://ref.ly/Deut5:9); [JOS 24:19](https://ref.ly/Josh24:19); [NAM 1:2](https://ref.ly/Nah1:2)

God's zeal for the honour of his name
-------------------------------------

**[ISA 42:8](https://ref.ly/Isa42:8)** *See also* [EXO 20:7](https://ref.ly/Exod20:7); [DEU 32:51](https://ref.ly/Deut32:51); [ISA 48:9–48:11](https://ref.ly/Isa48:9-Isa48:11); [EZK 20:9](https://ref.ly/Ezek20:9), [EZK 20:14](https://ref.ly/Ezek20:14), [EZK 20:22](https://ref.ly/Ezek20:22), [EZK 36:20–36:23](https://ref.ly/Ezek36:20-Ezek36:23), [EZK 39:7](https://ref.ly/Ezek39:7), [EZK 39:25](https://ref.ly/Ezek39:25)

----------------------------------

## 1190: glory (id: 1190)

The distinctive feature of the presence of God, often compared to power, weight or brightness. Scripture affirms that God's glory is made known through his work of creation, his acts of intervention in history and supremely in the life and resurrection of Jesus Christ.

* **Associated Articles:** 1191: glory, of God (ID: `1191@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1192: glory, of Jesus Christ (ID: `1192@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1193: glory, revelation of (ID: `1193@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1194: glory, divine and human (ID: `1194@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 1191: glory, of God (id: 1191)

See [1045: God, glory of](1045.md)



## 1192: glory, of Jesus Christ (id: 1192)

See [2024: Jesus Christ, glory of](2024.md)



## 1193: glory, revelation of (id: 1193)

God's majestic brilliance shown to the world through Israel and the church, and supremely in and through Jesus Christ.

God's glory revealed in nature
------------------------------

**[PSA 19:1](https://ref.ly/Ps19:1)** *See also* [GEN 1:31](https://ref.ly/Gen1:31); [PSA 29:3–29:9](https://ref.ly/Ps29:3-Ps29:9), [PSA 104:1–104:4](https://ref.ly/Ps104:1-Ps104:4); [ROM 1:20](https://ref.ly/Rom1:20)

## 1194: glory, divine and human (id: 1194)

Through the death and resurrection of Jesus Christ, believers will finally be glorified. All human glory derives from God.

Human glory in the creation
---------------------------

### Human glory as God's intention

**[HEB 2:6–2:7](https://ref.ly/Heb2:6-Heb2:7)** *See also* [PSA 8:4–8:5](https://ref.ly/Ps8:4-Ps8:5)

### People are created in God's image

**[GEN 5:1](https://ref.ly/Gen5:1)** *See also* [GEN 1:26–1:27](https://ref.ly/Gen1:26-Gen1:27), [GEN 9:6](https://ref.ly/Gen9:6); [1CO 11:7](https://ref.ly/1Cor11:7); [JAS 3:9](https://ref.ly/Jas3:9)

### Human beings have precedence over the rest of creation

**[MAT 6:26](https://ref.ly/Matt6:26)** parallel [LUK 12:24](https://ref.ly/Luke12:24) *See also* [MAT 10:29–10:31](https://ref.ly/Matt10:29-Matt10:31) parallel [LUK 12:6–12:7](https://ref.ly/Luke12:6-Luke12:7); [MAT 12:12](https://ref.ly/Matt12:12)

### Human responsibility for creation

**[GEN 2:19–2:20](https://ref.ly/Gen2:19-Gen2:20)** *See also* [GEN 1:28](https://ref.ly/Gen1:28); [PSA 8:6–8:8](https://ref.ly/Ps8:6-Ps8:8); [HEB 2:8](https://ref.ly/Heb2:8); [JAS 3:7](https://ref.ly/Jas3:7)

-------------------------------------

**[ROM 3:23](https://ref.ly/Rom3:23)** *See also* [GEN 5:3](https://ref.ly/Gen5:3); [ECC 7:29](https://ref.ly/Eccl7:29); [ROM 5:12](https://ref.ly/Rom5:12)

-----------------------------------

**[1PE 1:24–1:25](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:24-1Pet1:25)** *See also* [ISA 40:6–40:8](https://ref.ly/Isa40:6-Isa40:8); [PSA 49:10–49:11](https://ref.ly/Ps49:10-Ps49:11), [PSA 49:16–49:17](https://ref.ly/Ps49:16-Ps49:17), [PSA 103:15](https://ref.ly/Ps103:15); [2CO 3:7–3:8](https://ref.ly/2Cor3:7-2Cor3:8), [2CO 3:10](https://ref.ly/2Cor3:10), [2CO 3:13](https://ref.ly/2Cor3:13)

-----------------------------

**[JOB 40:9–40:10](https://ref.ly/Job40:9-Job40:10)** *God shows Job the impossibility of human beings attaining the perfection of God's glory.* *See also* [EXO 15:11](https://ref.ly/Exod15:11); [1CH 16:24–16:28](https://ref.ly/1Chr16:24-1Chr16:28) parallel [PSA 96:3–96:7](https://ref.ly/Ps96:3-Ps96:7); [ISA 42:8](https://ref.ly/Isa42:8), [ISA 48:11](https://ref.ly/Isa48:11)

## 1205: God, titles and names of (id: 1205)

These reflect the great and varied aspects of God's being and character. They are particularly used by the psalmists to speak of God as a source of strength, security, blessing and hope.

Titles which denote God's greatness
-----------------------------------

### God Almighty

**[GEN 17:1](https://ref.ly/Gen17:1)** *This was the special name by which God revealed himself to the patriarchs. The Hebrew is “El\-Shaddai” possibly meaning “God the mountain”, emphasising God's might.* *See also* [GEN 28:3](https://ref.ly/Gen28:3), [GEN 48:3](https://ref.ly/Gen48:3); [EXO 6:3](https://ref.ly/Exod6:3); [RUT 1:20–1:21](https://ref.ly/Ruth1:20-Ruth1:21); [JOB 5:17](https://ref.ly/Job5:17)JOB [6:4](https://ref.ly/Job6:4), [JOB 37:23](https://ref.ly/Job37:23)[PSA 91:1](https://ref.ly/Ps91:1); [REV 16:14](https://ref.ly/Rev16:14), [REV 19:15](https://ref.ly/Rev19:15)

### God Most High

**[GEN 14:18–14:20](https://ref.ly/Gen14:18-Gen14:20)** *The Hebrew “El\-Elyon” denotes the supremacy and sovereignty of God.* *See also* [GEN 14:22](https://ref.ly/Gen14:22); [DEU 32:8](https://ref.ly/Deut32:8); [2SA 22:14](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:14) parallel [PSA 18:13](https://ref.ly/Ps18:13); [PSA 9:2](https://ref.ly/Ps9:2), [PSA 21:7](https://ref.ly/Ps21:7), [PSA 46:4](https://ref.ly/Ps46:4), [PSA 47:2](https://ref.ly/Ps47:2), [PSA 78:35](https://ref.ly/Ps78:35), [PSA 97:9](https://ref.ly/Ps97:9); [ISA 14:14](https://ref.ly/Isa14:14); [DAN 3:26](https://ref.ly/Dan3:26)MRK [5:7](https://ref.ly/Dan5:7) parallel [LUK 8:28](https://ref.ly/Luke8:28); [LUK 1:32](https://ref.ly/Luke1:32), [LUK 1:35](https://ref.ly/Luke1:35)[LUK 6:35](https://ref.ly/Luke6:35); [ACT 16:17](https://ref.ly/Acts16:17)

### The Eternal God

**[GEN 21:33](https://ref.ly/Gen21:33)** *The Hebrew “El\-Olam” only occurs in this verse.* *See also* [DEU 33:27](https://ref.ly/Deut33:27); [ROM 16:26](https://ref.ly/Rom16:26)

### The Ancient of Days

[DAN 7:9](https://ref.ly/Dan7:9), [DAN 7:13](https://ref.ly/Dan7:13), [DAN 7:22](https://ref.ly/Dan7:22)

### The Mighty One

**[LUK 1:49](https://ref.ly/Luke1:49)** *See also* [JOS 22:22](https://ref.ly/Josh22:22); [PSA 50:1](https://ref.ly/Ps50:1), [PSA 132:2](https://ref.ly/Ps132:2), [PSA 132:5](https://ref.ly/Ps132:5); [ISA 1:24](https://ref.ly/Isa1:24), [ISA 49:26](https://ref.ly/Isa49:26), [ISA 60:16](https://ref.ly/Isa60:16); [MRK 14:62](https://ref.ly/Mark14:62)

### The living God

**[PSA 84:2](https://ref.ly/Ps84:2)**; **[DAN 6:26–6:27](https://ref.ly/Dan6:26-Dan6:27)** *See also* [DEU 5:26](https://ref.ly/Deut5:26); [JOS 3:10](https://ref.ly/Josh3:10); [1SA 17:26](https://ref.ly/1Sam17:26), [1SA 17:36](https://ref.ly/1Sam17:36); [2KI 19:16](https://ref.ly/2Kgs19:16) parallel [ISA 37:17](https://ref.ly/Isa37:17); [PSA 42:2](https://ref.ly/Ps42:2); [JER 10:10](https://ref.ly/Jer10:10); [MAT 16:16](https://ref.ly/Matt16:16); [ACT 14:15](https://ref.ly/Acts14:15); [HEB 10:31](https://ref.ly/Heb10:31)

### The Holy One of Israel

**[ISA 12:6](https://ref.ly/Isa12:6)** *“the Holy One of Israel” is a favourite divine title in the book of Isaiah.* *See also* [2KI 19:22](https://ref.ly/2Kgs19:22) parallel [ISA 37:23](https://ref.ly/Isa37:23); [PSA 71:22](https://ref.ly/Ps71:22), [PSA 78:41](https://ref.ly/Ps78:41), [PSA 89:18](https://ref.ly/Ps89:18); [ISA 30:12](https://ref.ly/Isa30:12), [ISA 30:15](https://ref.ly/Isa30:15), [ISA 41:14](https://ref.ly/Isa41:14), [ISA 45:11](https://ref.ly/Isa45:11), [ISA 55:5](https://ref.ly/Isa55:5), [ISA 60:9](https://ref.ly/Isa60:9)

### The LORD

**[GEN 4:26](https://ref.ly/Gen4:26)**; **[EXO 6:2](https://ref.ly/Exod6:2)** *See also* [EXO 3:15](https://ref.ly/Exod3:15), [EXO 34:5–34:7](https://ref.ly/Exod34:5-Exod34:7)

Titles which refer to God as LORD
---------------------------------

### The Lord God

## 1210: God, human descriptions of (id: 1210)

Figures of speech which describe God in human terms, sometimes referred to as anthropomorphisms. Since God is Spirit, these expressions help the human mind to understand God, and enable God to reveal himself to human beings.

Bodily form ascribed to God
---------------------------

**[EXO 33:23](https://ref.ly/Exod33:23)** *See also* [GEN 18:2–18:14](https://ref.ly/Gen18:2-Gen18:14); [JOS 5:13–5:15](https://ref.ly/Josh5:13-Josh5:15); [EZK 1:26–1:28](https://ref.ly/Ezek1:26-Ezek1:28)

### His face

**[NUM 6:25–6:26](https://ref.ly/Num6:25-Num6:26)** *See also* [PSA 27:8](https://ref.ly/Ps27:8), [PSA 51:9](https://ref.ly/Ps51:9); [MAT 18:10](https://ref.ly/Matt18:10); [REV 22:4](https://ref.ly/Rev22:4)

### His heart

**[2CH 7:16](https://ref.ly/2Chr7:16)** *See also* [GEN 6:6](https://ref.ly/Gen6:6), [GEN 8:21](https://ref.ly/Gen8:21); [1SA 13:14](https://ref.ly/1Sam13:14); [ACT 13:22](https://ref.ly/Acts13:22)

### His hands

**[ISA 14:27](https://ref.ly/Isa14:27)** *See also* [1CH 28:19](https://ref.ly/1Chr28:19), [1CH 29:14](https://ref.ly/1Chr29:14), [1CH 29:16](https://ref.ly/1Chr29:16); [PSA 45:4](https://ref.ly/Ps45:4); [ACT 2:33–2:34](https://ref.ly/Acts2:33-Acts2:34); [1PE 3:22](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:22), [1PE 5:6](https://ref.ly/1Pet5:6)

### His eyes

**[2CH 16:9](https://ref.ly/2Chr16:9)** *See also* [DEU 11:12](https://ref.ly/Deut11:12); [PRO 15:3](https://ref.ly/Prov15:3); [AMO 9:8](https://ref.ly/Amos9:8); [ZEC 4:10](https://ref.ly/Zech4:10); [1PE 3:12](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:12); [PSA 34:15](https://ref.ly/Ps34:15)

### His feet

**[EZK 43:7](https://ref.ly/Ezek43:7)** *See also* [DEU 33:3](https://ref.ly/Deut33:3); [2SA 22:10](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:10) parallel [PSA 18:9](https://ref.ly/Ps18:9); [PSA 45:5](https://ref.ly/Ps45:5); [ISA 60:13](https://ref.ly/Isa60:13)

### His arm

**[ISA 59:1](https://ref.ly/Isa59:1)**; **[JER 32:21](https://ref.ly/Jer32:21)** *God's arm is particularly used as a symbol of his power at the exodus.* *See also* [EXO 6:6](https://ref.ly/Exod6:6); [DEU 5:15](https://ref.ly/Deut5:15); [JOB 40:9](https://ref.ly/Job40:9); [ISA 51:9](https://ref.ly/Isa51:9), [ISA 52:10](https://ref.ly/Isa52:10), [ISA 63:5](https://ref.ly/Isa63:5); [LUK 1:51](https://ref.ly/Luke1:51); [JHN 12:38](https://ref.ly/John12:38); [ISA 53:1](https://ref.ly/Isa53:1)

### His mind

**[ROM 11:34](https://ref.ly/Rom11:34)** *See also* [ISA 40:13](https://ref.ly/Isa40:13); [1SA 15:29](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:29); [JER 7:31](https://ref.ly/Jer7:31); [HEB 7:21](https://ref.ly/Heb7:21); [PSA 110:4](https://ref.ly/Ps110:4)

## 1225: God, as Spirit (id: 1225)

God has no material body and he is not subject to human limitations. While his spiritual nature is clearly inferred in Scripture, it is seldom directly stated; the emphasis is on his dynamic, living personhood.

God as spirit
-------------

**[JHN 4:24](https://ref.ly/John4:24)** *See also* [ISA 28:5–28:6](https://ref.ly/Isa28:5-Isa28:6), [ISA 31:3](https://ref.ly/Isa31:3)

### God is not subject to physical limitations

[1SA 16:7](https://ref.ly/1Sam16:7); ; [1KI 18:27](https://ref.ly/1Kgs18:27) *Elijah's mockery of Baal implies a contrast with the true God who is not subject to the limitations suggested*; ; [JOB 10:4–10:8](https://ref.ly/Job10:4-Job10:8); ; [PSA 121:3–121:4](https://ref.ly/Ps121:3-Ps121:4)

### God as the Spirit

**[PSA 139:7](https://ref.ly/Ps139:7)** *See also* [PSA 51:11](https://ref.ly/Ps51:11) *The Spirit and the presence of God are equated*; [PSA 143:10](https://ref.ly/Ps143:10) *God's guidance and the Spirit's leading are equated*; [ISA 34:16](https://ref.ly/Isa34:16) *God's Spirit participates in God's plans*; [2CO 3:17–3:18](https://ref.ly/2Cor3:17-2Cor3:18)

God cannot be represented physically
------------------------------------

## 1230: God, the Lord (id: 1230)

God is the almighty ruler to whom everything and everyone is subject. His lordship is seen in his power and his victory over his enemies and also in his deliverance of his people and his loving care for them. He is the recipient of their obedience and their prayers. (“Lord” is the translation of the Hebrew word “Adonai” meaning “Ruler” or “Master” and is distinct from “LORD” which is the translation of the divine name “Yahweh”.).

God is the almighty ruler
-------------------------

### He is Lord of lords

**[1TI 6:15](https://ref.ly/1Tim6:15)** *God exercises his lordship over all creation, but especially over all humanity.* *See also* [DEU 10:17](https://ref.ly/Deut10:17); [PSA 136:3](https://ref.ly/Ps136:3); [DAN 2:47](https://ref.ly/Dan2:47)

### He is Lord of all the earth

**[PSA 97:5](https://ref.ly/Ps97:5)** *See also* [JOS 3:11](https://ref.ly/Josh3:11), [JOS 3:13](https://ref.ly/Josh3:13); [MIC 4:13](https://ref.ly/Mic4:13); [ZEC 4:14](https://ref.ly/Zech4:14); [ACT 17:24](https://ref.ly/Acts17:24)

Characteristics of God as Lord
------------------------------

### He is great and powerful

**[PSA 147:5](https://ref.ly/Ps147:5)** *See also* [NEH 4:14](https://ref.ly/Neh4:14); [PSA 86:8](https://ref.ly/Ps86:8), [PSA 114:7–114:8](https://ref.ly/Ps114:7-Ps114:8), [PSA 135:5](https://ref.ly/Ps135:5); [ISA 28:2](https://ref.ly/Isa28:2); [DAN 9:4](https://ref.ly/Dan9:4); [ACT 4:24](https://ref.ly/Acts4:24)

### He is majestic and exalted

**[ISA 6:1](https://ref.ly/Isa6:1)** *See also* [PSA 8:1](https://ref.ly/Ps8:1), [PSA 8:9](https://ref.ly/Ps8:9); [2TH 1:9](https://ref.ly/2Thess1:9)

### He is righteous

**[DAN 9:16](https://ref.ly/Dan9:16)** *See also* [PSA 97:5–97:6](https://ref.ly/Ps97:5-Ps97:6); [DAN 9:7](https://ref.ly/Dan9:7)

### He is loving and caring

**[PSA 86:15](https://ref.ly/Ps86:15)** *See also* [PSA 62:12](https://ref.ly/Ps62:12), [PSA 86:5](https://ref.ly/Ps86:5)

## 1235: God, the LORD (id: 1235)

The translation of the Hebrew name “Yahweh” which is the personal name of God whose meaning was revealed to Moses. It emphasises that God is the one who is eternal, unique, unchangeable and always actively present with his people. It expresses God's role as Israel's Redeemer and covenant Lord.

The name of God, the LORD
-------------------------

### The LORD is the personal name of God

**[ISA 42:8](https://ref.ly/Isa42:8)** *“The LORD” is the NIV rendering of the Hebrew “Yahweh”.*

### The name's meaning

**[EXO 3:14–3:15](https://ref.ly/Exod3:14-Exod3:15)** *This forms part of God's explanation of who he is. “I AM” (in Hebrew closely resembling “Yahweh”) expresses the ever\-present, unchanging, totally dependable character of God.*

### The name is revealed to Moses

**[EXO 6:2–6:3](https://ref.ly/Exod6:2-Exod6:3)** *The name had been used previously (e.g., [Ge 4:26](https://ref.ly/Gen4:26)) but its meaning was not fully understood until God revealed it to Moses in the context of the exodus from Egypt.*

### The name is glorious and awesome

**[DEU 28:58–28:59](https://ref.ly/Deut28:58-Deut28:59)** *See also* [JOS 7:9](https://ref.ly/Josh7:9); [1SA 12:22](https://ref.ly/1Sam12:22)

### The name is not to be misused

**[EXO 20:7](https://ref.ly/Exod20:7)** parallel [DEU 5:11](https://ref.ly/Deut5:11) *The misuse referred to here is swearing falsely by God's name.* *See also* [LEV 19:12](https://ref.ly/Lev19:12), [LEV 24:11](https://ref.ly/Lev24:11), [LEV 24:15–24:16](https://ref.ly/Lev24:15-Lev24:16) *The Jews came to believe that just uttering the name “Yahweh” was an offence and as a result its exact pronunciation has been lost. What merited the death penalty here was using God's name as a curse.*

God's character is revealed by his name the LORD
------------------------------------------------

### He is unique

[EXO 8:10](https://ref.ly/Exod8:10); ; [DEU 4:35](https://ref.ly/Deut4:35), [DEU 4:39](https://ref.ly/Deut4:39); ; [1KI 8:60](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:60); ; [ISA 45:5](https://ref.ly/Isa45:5), [ISA 45:18](https://ref.ly/Isa45:18); ; [JOL 2:27](https://ref.ly/Joel2:27)

### He is eternal

[GEN 21:33](https://ref.ly/Gen21:33); ; [PSA 9:7](https://ref.ly/Ps9:7), [PSA 29:10](https://ref.ly/Ps29:10), [PSA 102:12](https://ref.ly/Ps102:12), [PSA 135:13](https://ref.ly/Ps135:13); ; [ISA 26:4](https://ref.ly/Isa26:4)

### He is holy

[DEU 31:6](https://ref.ly/Deut31:6); ; [JOS 1:9](https://ref.ly/Josh1:9); ; [1KI 8:57](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:57); ; [HAG 1:13](https://ref.ly/Hag1:13)

God reveals the relevance of his name the LORD by his actions
-------------------------------------------------------------

### In creation

**[JER 33:2](https://ref.ly/Jer33:2)** *See also* [ISA 42:5](https://ref.ly/Isa42:5), [ISA 43:15](https://ref.ly/Isa43:15) *“The LORD” is Creator of the universe but also the Creator of the people Israel*; [ISA 45:18](https://ref.ly/Isa45:18) *Human beings are the purpose of God's creation; they know God as “the LORD”.*

### In the deliverance of his people from Egypt

**[EXO 6:6](https://ref.ly/Exod6:6)** *Deliverance is a central concept in the revelation of the divine name.* *See also* [EXO 12:51](https://ref.ly/Exod12:51), [EXO 14:30](https://ref.ly/Exod14:30), [EXO 16:6](https://ref.ly/Exod16:6), [EXO 20:2](https://ref.ly/Exod20:2); [LEV 26:13](https://ref.ly/Lev26:13); [PSA 81:10](https://ref.ly/Ps81:10)

### In establishing a covenant with his people

**[EXO 6:7](https://ref.ly/Exod6:7)** *See also* [EXO 29:46](https://ref.ly/Exod29:46); [2SA 7:24](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:24) parallel [1CH 17:22](https://ref.ly/1Chr17:22); [JER 14:9](https://ref.ly/Jer14:9)

### In the judgment of his enemies

**[EXO 12:12](https://ref.ly/Exod12:12)** *See also* [EXO 7:5](https://ref.ly/Exod7:5), [EXO 8:22–8:23](https://ref.ly/Exod8:22-Exod8:23); [1SA 17:45–17:47](https://ref.ly/1Sam17:45-1Sam17:47); [2CH 14:11–14:13](https://ref.ly/2Chr14:11-2Chr14:13)

### In the restoration of his people

**[EZK 36:36](https://ref.ly/Ezek36:36)** *See also* [PSA 102:15–102:22](https://ref.ly/Ps102:15-Ps102:22); [ISA 60:15–60:22](https://ref.ly/Isa60:15-Isa60:22); [EZK 37:6](https://ref.ly/Ezek37:6), [EZK 37:13–37:14](https://ref.ly/Ezek37:13-Ezek37:14) *The theme “then you, my people, will know that I am the LORD” (with slight variations) runs throughout the book of Ezekiel and is connected to divine acts of judgment and restoration.*

God, the LORD denotes God's lordship
------------------------------------

### He is the Sovereign LORD

**[EZK 2:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek2:4)** *“Sovereign LORD” is the NIV rendering of “Adonai Yahweh”, the favourite divine title in Ezekiel.* *See also* [GEN 15:2](https://ref.ly/Gen15:2), [GEN 15:8](https://ref.ly/Gen15:8); [DEU 3:24](https://ref.ly/Deut3:24); [JOS 7:7](https://ref.ly/Josh7:7); [JDG 6:22](https://ref.ly/Judg6:22); [2SA 7:18–7:29](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:18-2Sam7:29); [PSA 73:28](https://ref.ly/Ps73:28); [ISA 61:1](https://ref.ly/Isa61:1); [JER 1:6](https://ref.ly/Jer1:6); [AMO 1:8](https://ref.ly/Amos1:8)

### He is the LORD Almighty

**[1SA 1:3](https://ref.ly/1Sam1:3)** *“The LORD Almighty” is the NIV rendering of “Yahweh Sabaoth” (“the LORD of hosts”) which emphasises the sovereignty of “the LORD”.* *See also* [1CH 11:9](https://ref.ly/1Chr11:9); [PSA 24:10](https://ref.ly/Ps24:10), [PSA 46:7](https://ref.ly/Ps46:7), [PSA 46:11](https://ref.ly/Ps46:11); [ISA 2:12](https://ref.ly/Isa2:12); [JER 39:16](https://ref.ly/Jer39:16); [HAG 2:6–2:9](https://ref.ly/Hag2:6-Hag2:9); [ZEC 1:3–1:4](https://ref.ly/Zech1:3-Zech1:4), [ZEC 1:6](https://ref.ly/Zech1:6); [MAL 1:14](https://ref.ly/Mal1:14)

### He is the Lord, the LORD Almighty

**[ISA 1:24](https://ref.ly/Isa1:24)** *“The Lord, the LORD Almighty” is the NIV rendering of “Adonai Yahweh Sabaoth” which is often associated with the LORD's authority to rule and to judge.* *See also* [PSA 69:6](https://ref.ly/Ps69:6); [ISA 3:15](https://ref.ly/Isa3:15), [ISA 19:4](https://ref.ly/Isa19:4); [JER 2:19](https://ref.ly/Jer2:19), [JER 46:10](https://ref.ly/Jer46:10), [JER 49:5](https://ref.ly/Jer49:5); [AMO 9:5](https://ref.ly/Amos9:5)

As the LORD, God interacts with his people
------------------------------------------

### He enforces the moral code

**[LEV 18:1–18:5](https://ref.ly/Lev18:1-Lev18:5)** *The phrase “I am the LORD” occurs over 40 times in Leviticus chapters 18–26 and is the authority behind the moral law given to God's people.* *See also* [LEV 11:44–11:45](https://ref.ly/Lev11:44-Lev11:45), [LEV 19:2](https://ref.ly/Lev19:2)

### He makes his people holy

**[LEV 22:32](https://ref.ly/Lev22:32)** *See also* [EXO 31:13](https://ref.ly/Exod31:13); [LEV 20:8](https://ref.ly/Lev20:8), [LEV 21:8](https://ref.ly/Lev21:8); [EZK 20:12](https://ref.ly/Ezek20:12), [EZK 37:28](https://ref.ly/Ezek37:28)

### He is the object of his people's worship

**[EXO 4:22–4:23](https://ref.ly/Exod4:22-Exod4:23)** *The purpose of Israel's redemption from Egypt was that they would be free to worship the LORD.* *See also* [EXO 12:31](https://ref.ly/Exod12:31), [EXO 23:25](https://ref.ly/Exod23:25); [1CH 16:29](https://ref.ly/1Chr16:29) parallel [PSA 96:9](https://ref.ly/Ps96:9); [PSA 29:2](https://ref.ly/Ps29:2), [PSA 99:5](https://ref.ly/Ps99:5), [PSA 100:2](https://ref.ly/Ps100:2); [JON 1:9](https://ref.ly/Jonah1:9)

Jesus Christ takes God's name to himself
----------------------------------------

**[JHN 8:58–8:59](https://ref.ly/John8:58-John8:59)** *The form of expression used by Jesus Christ meant that he was clearly identifying himself with the divine name “I AM”. The response of the crowd confirms this.*

## 1240: God, the Rock (id: 1240)

An OT title for God and a Messianic title signifying that God's people can rely on him for absolute protection and salvation.

Rock as a title for Israel's God
--------------------------------

**[PSA 78:35](https://ref.ly/Ps78:35)** *See also* [GEN 49:24](https://ref.ly/Gen49:24); [DEU 32:15](https://ref.ly/Deut32:15), [DEU 32:18](https://ref.ly/Deut32:18), [DEU 32:30](https://ref.ly/Deut32:30); [2SA 23:3](https://ref.ly/2Sam23:3); [PSA 42:9](https://ref.ly/Ps42:9); [ISA 30:29](https://ref.ly/Isa30:29); [HAB 1:12](https://ref.ly/Hab1:12)

God the Rock is unique
----------------------

**[2SA 22:32](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:32)** parallel [PSA 18:31](https://ref.ly/Ps18:31) *See also* [1SA 2:2](https://ref.ly/1Sam2:2); [ISA 44:8](https://ref.ly/Isa44:8)

The Rock is superior to other gods
----------------------------------

**[DEU 32:31](https://ref.ly/Deut32:31)** *See also* [DEU 32:37](https://ref.ly/Deut32:37)

The Rock is worthy to be praised
--------------------------------

**[PSA 144:1](https://ref.ly/Ps144:1)** *See also* [DEU 32:4](https://ref.ly/Deut32:4); [PSA 92:15](https://ref.ly/Ps92:15)

---------------------------

## 1245: God of the fathers (id: 1245)

God's particular association with Abraham, Isaac and Jacob, the fathers of the nations of Israel, highlights his faithfulness in fulfilling the promises made to them. He is the God who establishes a covenant with his people for their everlasting blessing.

God's relationship with the fathers
-----------------------------------

### The God of Abraham, Isaac and Jacob

**[ACT 7:32](https://ref.ly/Acts7:32)** *See also* [EXO 3:6](https://ref.ly/Exod3:6), [EXO 3:15](https://ref.ly/Exod3:15), [EXO 4:5](https://ref.ly/Exod4:5)

### The God of Jacob

**[PSA 20:1](https://ref.ly/Ps20:1)** *“Jacob” is used here as a synonym for the nation of Israel. This usage is common in the Psalms as a reminder to God's people of his faithfulness to Jacob and the emergent nation of Israel.* *See also* [GEN 32:27–32:28](https://ref.ly/Gen32:27-Gen32:28); [PSA 14:7](https://ref.ly/Ps14:7), [PSA 46:7](https://ref.ly/Ps46:7), [PSA 46:11](https://ref.ly/Ps46:11), [PSA 75:9](https://ref.ly/Ps75:9), [PSA 76:6](https://ref.ly/Ps76:6), [PSA 114:7](https://ref.ly/Ps114:7)

### Such a relationship served as an encouragement to others

Abraham's servant was encouraged to trust God in his mission by the example of Abraham's faith: [GEN 24:12](https://ref.ly/Gen24:12), [GEN 24:27](https://ref.ly/Gen24:27), [GEN 24:42](https://ref.ly/Gen24:42), [GEN 24:48](https://ref.ly/Gen24:48); [GEN 26:24](https://ref.ly/Gen26:24), [GEN 31:42](https://ref.ly/Gen31:42), [GEN 31:53](https://ref.ly/Gen31:53); [GEN 46:1–46:3](https://ref.ly/Gen46:1-Gen46:3) *Jacob learned to fear and trust God through his father Isaac.*

God's covenant with the fathers
-------------------------------

### God's promises that they will be the fathers of a great nation

**[GEN 28:13–28:15](https://ref.ly/Gen28:13-Gen28:15)** *See also* [GEN 26:2–26:4](https://ref.ly/Gen26:2-Gen26:4); [EXO 3:16–3:17](https://ref.ly/Exod3:16-Exod3:17)

### God remembers and fulfils his promises

**[EXO 2:24](https://ref.ly/Exod2:24)** *See also* [EXO 6:3–6:5](https://ref.ly/Exod6:3-Exod6:5), [EXO 32:13](https://ref.ly/Exod32:13); [LEV 26:42](https://ref.ly/Lev26:42); [DEU 1:8](https://ref.ly/Deut1:8); [ACT 7:17](https://ref.ly/Acts7:17)

### God makes a covenant with his people to be their God

**[DEU 29:12–29:13](https://ref.ly/Deut29:12-Deut29:13)** *See also* [GEN 17:7](https://ref.ly/Gen17:7); [EXO 6:7–6:8](https://ref.ly/Exod6:7-Exod6:8); [PSA 105:8–105:11](https://ref.ly/Ps105:8-Ps105:11)

-----------------------------------------

People sometimes fail to respond to the God of their fathers
------------------------------------------------------------

## 1250: Abba (id: 1250)

The Aramaic word “Abba” is thought to be a very intimate term for “Father” suggesting that those who use it to refer to God enjoy a close relationship with him. Jesus Christ uses the term as a consequence of his natural sonship of God; believers may use it as a consequence of their adopted sonship of God through faith.

\`\`Abba'' used in addressing God
---------------------------------

### By Jesus Christ

[MRK 14:36](https://ref.ly/Mark14:36)

### By believers

[ROM 8:15](https://ref.ly/Rom8:15); ; [GAL 4:6](https://ref.ly/Gal4:6)

* **Associated Passages:** Mark 14:36; Romans 8:15; Galatians 4:6
* **Associated Articles:** 1040: God, fatherhood of (ID: `1040@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1205: God, titles and names of (ID: `1205@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1510: Trinity, the (ID: `1510@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2078: Jesus Christ, sonship of (ID: `2078@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2218: Jesus Christ, Son of God (ID: `2218@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 3221: Holy Spirit, and prayer (ID: `3221@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5895: intimacy (ID: `5895@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7922: fellowship, with God (ID: `7922@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 8104: assurance (ID: `8104@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 8134: knowing God (ID: `8134@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 1255: face of God (id: 1255)

A term used to refer to the character of God, especially his favour towards his people. For God to turn his face to his people is to offer them his grace and help; for God to turn his face against his people is to withhold his favour and blessing. To seek the face of God is to seek his favour.

The face of God as a sign of blessing
-------------------------------------

**[NUM 6:25–6:26](https://ref.ly/Num6:25-Num6:26)** *See also* [2SA 21:1](https://ref.ly/2Sam21:1); [1CH 16:11](https://ref.ly/1Chr16:11); [PSA 4:6](https://ref.ly/Ps4:6), [PSA 31:16](https://ref.ly/Ps31:16), [PSA 67:1](https://ref.ly/Ps67:1), [PSA 80:19](https://ref.ly/Ps80:19), [PSA 105:4](https://ref.ly/Ps105:4), [PSA 119:135](https://ref.ly/Ps119:135); [EZK 39:29](https://ref.ly/Ezek39:29)

Parts of God's face
-------------------

### His ears

[2SA 22:7](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:7); ; [2KI 19:28](https://ref.ly/2Kgs19:28); ; [PSA 34:15](https://ref.ly/Ps34:15), [PSA 102:2](https://ref.ly/Ps102:2); ; [ISA 59:1](https://ref.ly/Isa59:1)

### His eyes

**[PSA 34:15](https://ref.ly/Ps34:15)** *See also* [DEU 11:12](https://ref.ly/Deut11:12); [2CH 16:9](https://ref.ly/2Chr16:9); [PSA 139:16](https://ref.ly/Ps139:16); [PRO 15:3](https://ref.ly/Prov15:3)

### His hair

[DAN 7:9](https://ref.ly/Dan7:9)

### His lips

[PSA 89:34](https://ref.ly/Ps89:34); ; [ISA 11:4](https://ref.ly/Isa11:4), [ISA 30:27](https://ref.ly/Isa30:27)

### His mouth

[2SA 22:9](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:9); ; [JOB 15:30](https://ref.ly/Job15:30); ; [ISA 45:23](https://ref.ly/Isa45:23)

### His nostrils

[2SA 22:9](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:9), [2SA 22:16](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:16)

The visibility of God's face
----------------------------

### His face cannot be seen

**[EXO 33:20–33:23](https://ref.ly/Exod33:20-Exod33:23)** *“The face of God” may mean here God's real and true self, the inference being that no\-one can look on God as he is in his total purity and majesty.*

### Apparent exceptions where God is seen face to face

**[GEN 32:30](https://ref.ly/Gen32:30)** *After Jacob's wrestling with a figure whose exact identity is not explicit in the preceding verses. Jacob did experience a real encounter with God but God was in a real and approachable form, not in his transcendent and visible glory.* *See also* [EXO 33:11](https://ref.ly/Exod33:11); [NUM 12:8](https://ref.ly/Num12:8); [DEU 5:4](https://ref.ly/Deut5:4), [DEU 34:10](https://ref.ly/Deut34:10); [EZK 20:35](https://ref.ly/Ezek20:35)

### The angels in heaven look upon the face of God

[MAT 18:10](https://ref.ly/Matt18:10)

### God must reveal himself if people are to see his face

[JOB 34:29](https://ref.ly/Job34:29) *The Greek word for “revelation” literally means “removing a veil from one's face”.*

### The righteous will see God's face in the life to come

[1CO 13:12](https://ref.ly/1Cor13:12); ; [REV 22:4](https://ref.ly/Rev22:4)

When God hides his face blessing is withheld
--------------------------------------------

### Complaints at God hiding his face

**[PSA 44:24](https://ref.ly/Ps44:24)** *See also* [PSA 13:1](https://ref.ly/Ps13:1), [PSA 88:14](https://ref.ly/Ps88:14)

**[PSA 27:9](https://ref.ly/Ps27:9)** *See also* [PSA 69:17](https://ref.ly/Ps69:17), [PSA 102:2](https://ref.ly/Ps102:2), [PSA 143:7](https://ref.ly/Ps143:7)

### Statements concerning God's anger and judgment

**[ISA 54:8](https://ref.ly/Isa54:8)** *See also* [DEU 31:17–31:18](https://ref.ly/Deut31:17-Deut31:18); [PSA 22:24](https://ref.ly/Ps22:24), [PSA 30:7](https://ref.ly/Ps30:7), [PSA 51:9](https://ref.ly/Ps51:9), [PSA 104:29](https://ref.ly/Ps104:29); [ISA 8:17](https://ref.ly/Isa8:17), [ISA 64:7](https://ref.ly/Isa64:7); [JER 33:5](https://ref.ly/Jer33:5); [EZK 39:23–39:24](https://ref.ly/Ezek39:23-Ezek39:24); [MIC 3:4](https://ref.ly/Mic3:4); [REV 6:16](https://ref.ly/Rev6:16)

### Other phrases synonymous with God hiding his face

God's face as a symbol of his favour
------------------------------------

### Seeking the face of God in prayer

**[2CH 7:14](https://ref.ly/2Chr7:14)** *See also* [2SA 21:1](https://ref.ly/2Sam21:1); [1CH 16:11](https://ref.ly/1Chr16:11); [PSA 24:6](https://ref.ly/Ps24:6), [PSA 105:4](https://ref.ly/Ps105:4), [PSA 119:58](https://ref.ly/Ps119:58); [HOS 5:15](https://ref.ly/Hos5:15)

**[EXO 32:11](https://ref.ly/Exod32:11)** *See also* [1SA 13:12](https://ref.ly/1Sam13:12); [2KI 13:4](https://ref.ly/2Kgs13:4); [2CH 33:12](https://ref.ly/2Chr33:12); [JER 26:19](https://ref.ly/Jer26:19); [DAN 9:13](https://ref.ly/Dan9:13); [ZEC 7:2](https://ref.ly/Zech7:2), [ZEC 8:21](https://ref.ly/Zech8:21); [MAL 1:9](https://ref.ly/Mal1:9)

### Appearing before God in worship

**[EXO 23:15](https://ref.ly/Exod23:15)** *The phrase seems to recall the fact that in ancient religions worshippers came before carved faces of their idols. In Israel such physical representations of God were forbidden but the phrase was still used underlining the belief that Israel's God was present in his sanctuary.* *See also* [EXO 23:17](https://ref.ly/Exod23:17), [EXO 34:20](https://ref.ly/Exod34:20); [DEU 16:16](https://ref.ly/Deut16:16), [DEU 31:11](https://ref.ly/Deut31:11); [PSA 42:2](https://ref.ly/Ps42:2); [ISA 1:12](https://ref.ly/Isa1:12)

### The shining of God's face upon his people indicates his blessing

**[NUM 6:25–6:26](https://ref.ly/Num6:25-Num6:26)** *See also* [PSA 4:6](https://ref.ly/Ps4:6), [PSA 31:16](https://ref.ly/Ps31:16), [PSA 44:3](https://ref.ly/Ps44:3), [PSA 67:1](https://ref.ly/Ps67:1), [PSA 80:3](https://ref.ly/Ps80:3), [PSA 80:19](https://ref.ly/Ps80:19), [PSA 119:135](https://ref.ly/Ps119:135)

God's face accompanies Israel as a symbol of his presence
---------------------------------------------------------

**[EXO 33:14](https://ref.ly/Exod33:14)** *Literally “my face will go ...” Here this phrase may allude not only to God's presence but also to the manifestations of his presence (e.g., the cloud in verse 9\).* *See also* [DEU 4:37](https://ref.ly/Deut4:37); [ISA 63:9](https://ref.ly/Isa63:9)

## 1260: finger of God (id: 1260)

## 1265: hand of God (id: 1265)

A figure of speech which points to God's sovereign power in creation and in his actions on his people's behalf, especially in redemption. Also used as a symbol of authority and in taking oaths.

God creates by his hand
-----------------------

**[ACT 7:50](https://ref.ly/Acts7:50)** *See also* [ISA 66:2](https://ref.ly/Isa66:2); [JOB 10:3](https://ref.ly/Job10:3), [JOB 10:8](https://ref.ly/Job10:8); [PSA 8:3](https://ref.ly/Ps8:3), [PSA 19:1](https://ref.ly/Ps19:1), [PSA 95:5](https://ref.ly/Ps95:5), [PSA 138:8](https://ref.ly/Ps138:8); [ISA 48:13](https://ref.ly/Isa48:13), [ISA 64:8](https://ref.ly/Isa64:8)

God holds the world in his hand
-------------------------------

**[PSA 95:4](https://ref.ly/Ps95:4)** *See also* [JOB 12:10](https://ref.ly/Job12:10), [JOB 26:13](https://ref.ly/Job26:13), [JOB 36:32](https://ref.ly/Job36:32); [PSA 31:15](https://ref.ly/Ps31:15); [ISA 40:12](https://ref.ly/Isa40:12), [ISA 41:19–41:20](https://ref.ly/Isa41:19-Isa41:20); [DAN 5:23](https://ref.ly/Dan5:23)

God's creatures are fed from his hand
-------------------------------------

**[PSA 145:16](https://ref.ly/Ps145:16)** *See also* [PSA 104:28](https://ref.ly/Ps104:28); [ISA 34:17](https://ref.ly/Isa34:17)

God's hand symbolises his power
-------------------------------

### God's hand is mighty

**[HAB 3:4](https://ref.ly/Hab3:4)** *See also* [1CH 29:12](https://ref.ly/1Chr29:12); [PSA 118:15–118:16](https://ref.ly/Ps118:15-Ps118:16); [JER 18:6](https://ref.ly/Jer18:6); [DAN 4:35](https://ref.ly/Dan4:35); [AMO 9:2](https://ref.ly/Amos9:2)

### God executes judgment by the power of his hand

**[AMO 1:6–1:8](https://ref.ly/Amos1:6-Amos1:8)** *Judgment on the Philistine cities.* *See also* [DEU 32:41](https://ref.ly/Deut32:41); [1SA 5:6–5:9](https://ref.ly/1Sam5:6-1Sam5:9); [ISA 40:2](https://ref.ly/Isa40:2); [JER 15:6](https://ref.ly/Jer15:6); [LAM 2:3](https://ref.ly/Lam2:3); [EZK 6:14](https://ref.ly/Ezek6:14); [ZEP 1:4](https://ref.ly/Zeph1:4); [ACT 13:11](https://ref.ly/Acts13:11)

## 1270: right hand of God (id: 1270)

A figure of speech that represents God's ultimate power and authority, and where the exalted Jesus Christ now sits.

The right hand of God as a symbol
---------------------------------

### A symbol of power

**[PSA 89:13](https://ref.ly/Ps89:13)**

### A symbol of protection

**[PSA 16:8](https://ref.ly/Ps16:8)** *See also* [PSA 63:8](https://ref.ly/Ps63:8), [PSA 139:10](https://ref.ly/Ps139:10); [ISA 41:13](https://ref.ly/Isa41:13); [LAM 2:3](https://ref.ly/Lam2:3)

### A symbol of God's presence

**[PSA 16:11](https://ref.ly/Ps16:11)** *See also* [PSA 48:10](https://ref.ly/Ps48:10), [PSA 73:23](https://ref.ly/Ps73:23); [ISA 62:8](https://ref.ly/Isa62:8)

### A symbol of God's saving power

**[PSA 60:5](https://ref.ly/Ps60:5)** parallel [PSA 108:6](https://ref.ly/Ps108:6) *See also* [PSA 17:7](https://ref.ly/Ps17:7), [PSA 20:6](https://ref.ly/Ps20:6), [PSA 80:15](https://ref.ly/Ps80:15), [PSA 98:1](https://ref.ly/Ps98:1), [PSA 138:7](https://ref.ly/Ps138:7)

### A symbol of victory

[PSA 18:35](https://ref.ly/Ps18:35), [PSA 44:3](https://ref.ly/Ps44:3), [PSA 78:54](https://ref.ly/Ps78:54); ; [ISA 41:10](https://ref.ly/Isa41:10)

### A symbol of the defeat of God's enemies

**[EXO 15:6](https://ref.ly/Exod15:6)** *See also* [EXO 15:12](https://ref.ly/Exod15:12); [PSA 21:8](https://ref.ly/Ps21:8), [PSA 74:11](https://ref.ly/Ps74:11)

### A symbol of God's mighty works

**[PSA 45:4](https://ref.ly/Ps45:4)** *See also* [PSA 77:10](https://ref.ly/Ps77:10), [PSA 118:15–118:16](https://ref.ly/Ps118:15-Ps118:16); [ISA 48:13](https://ref.ly/Isa48:13)

### A symbol of judgment

[LAM 2:4](https://ref.ly/Lam2:4); ; [HAB 2:16](https://ref.ly/Hab2:16)

Jesus Christ at God's right hand
--------------------------------

### Jesus Christ is exalted to God's right hand

**[HEB 1:13](https://ref.ly/Heb1:13)** *Comparison between Jesus Christ and the angels confirms Christ's absolute supremacy.* *See also* [PSA 110:1](https://ref.ly/Ps110:1); [MAT 22:44](https://ref.ly/Matt22:44) parallels [MRK 12:36](https://ref.ly/Mark12:36), [LUK 20:42](https://ref.ly/Luke20:42); [LUK 22:69](https://ref.ly/Luke22:69); [ACT 2:34](https://ref.ly/Acts2:34), [ACT 7:55–7:56](https://ref.ly/Acts7:55-Acts7:56); [COL 3:1](https://ref.ly/Col3:1); [HEB 1:3](https://ref.ly/Heb1:3), [HEB 12:2](https://ref.ly/Heb12:2)

### Jesus Christ rules every authority at God's right hand

**[1PE 3:22](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:22)** *See also* [EPH 1:20–1:21](https://ref.ly/Eph1:20-Eph1:21)

### Jesus Christ continues his work at God's right hand

**[ROM 8:34](https://ref.ly/Rom8:34)** *See also* [ACT 2:33](https://ref.ly/Acts2:33), [ACT 5:31](https://ref.ly/Acts5:31); [HEB 4:14–4:16](https://ref.ly/Heb4:14-Heb4:16), [HEB 8:1](https://ref.ly/Heb8:1)

### Jesus Christ will return at God's right hand

**[MAT 26:64](https://ref.ly/Matt26:64)** parallel [MRK 14:62](https://ref.ly/Mark14:62)

### Jesus Christ takes a scroll from God's right hand

**[REV 5:1–5:7](https://ref.ly/Rev5:1-Rev5:7)** *The scroll probably refers to God's decrees for the destiny of the world.*

------------------------------

## 1305: God, activity of (id: 1305)

God is not passive or remote from his creation but dynamically involved in all that he has made. In the past, this activity was seen in the history of Israel and in the ministry of Jesus Christ. In the present, God's activity can be seen in the life of believers and of the church.

God is active by nature
-----------------------

### He actively works out his purposes

**[JHN 5:17](https://ref.ly/John5:17)** *See also* [NUM 23:19](https://ref.ly/Num23:19); [PSA 115:3](https://ref.ly/Ps115:3); [PRO 16:4](https://ref.ly/Prov16:4); [ISA 43:13](https://ref.ly/Isa43:13)

### His names reflect his activity and involvement in his people's lives

[GEN 22:14](https://ref.ly/Gen22:14) *“The LORD Will Provide”*; ; [EXO 15:26](https://ref.ly/Exod15:26) *“The LORD, who heals you”*; ; [EXO 17:15](https://ref.ly/Exod17:15) *“The LORD is my Banner”: this title emphasises that God is like a warrior who champions his people's cause*; ; [PSA 95:6](https://ref.ly/Ps95:6) *“The LORD our Maker”: the Hebrew word used does not refer to original creation but to the way in which God is fashioning a people for himself.*

### His word is active

**[ISA 55:10–55:11](https://ref.ly/Isa55:10-Isa55:11)** *The Hebrew for “word” can also be translated “deed” or “action”. God's word is not merely a communication of abstract truth but a powerful force active in the world.* *See also* [GEN 1:3](https://ref.ly/Gen1:3); [EZK 37:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek37:4), [EZK 37:7](https://ref.ly/Ezek37:7)

God is active in the creation
-----------------------------

### In making the universe

**[NEH 9:6](https://ref.ly/Neh9:6)** *See also* [GEN 1:1](https://ref.ly/Gen1:1), [GEN 1:31](https://ref.ly/Gen1:31), [GEN 2:2](https://ref.ly/Gen2:2), [GEN 5:1–5:2](https://ref.ly/Gen5:1-Gen5:2); [PSA 102:25](https://ref.ly/Ps102:25); [AMO 4:13](https://ref.ly/Amos4:13); [ACT 17:24](https://ref.ly/Acts17:24); [REV 4:11](https://ref.ly/Rev4:11)

### In sustaining the created order

**[PSA 103:19](https://ref.ly/Ps103:19)** *See also* [PSA 104:10–104:17](https://ref.ly/Ps104:10-Ps104:17), [PSA 107:33–107:35](https://ref.ly/Ps107:33-Ps107:35); [MAT 6:28–6:30](https://ref.ly/Matt6:28-Matt6:30); [ACT 14:17](https://ref.ly/Acts14:17); [EPH 1:11](https://ref.ly/Eph1:11); [COL 1:16–1:17](https://ref.ly/Col1:16-Col1:17)

### In bringing about changes in the weather

[JOB 37:10](https://ref.ly/Job37:10), [JOB 38:22–38:30](https://ref.ly/Job38:22-Job38:30), [JOB 38:34–38:35](https://ref.ly/Job38:34-Job38:35); ; [PSA 107:25](https://ref.ly/Ps107:25), [PSA 147:8](https://ref.ly/Ps147:8); ; [MAT 5:45](https://ref.ly/Matt5:45); ; [ACT 14:17](https://ref.ly/Acts14:17)

### In the stars and other heavenly bodies

[JOB 38:31–38:33](https://ref.ly/Job38:31-Job38:33); ; [PSA 104:19](https://ref.ly/Ps104:19), [PSA 147:4](https://ref.ly/Ps147:4); ; [ISA 40:26](https://ref.ly/Isa40:26); ; [JAS 1:17](https://ref.ly/Jas1:17)

### In the animal creation

[JOB 39:1–39:30](https://ref.ly/Job39:1-Job39:30), [JOB 40:15–40:24](https://ref.ly/Job40:15-Job40:24), [JOB 41:1–41:11](https://ref.ly/Job41:1-Job41:11); ; [PSA 104:20–104:27](https://ref.ly/Ps104:20-Ps104:27), [PSA 147:9](https://ref.ly/Ps147:9); ; [MAT 10:29](https://ref.ly/Matt10:29) parallel [LUK 12:6](https://ref.ly/Luke12:6)

God is active in Israel's history
---------------------------------

### In the calling and creation of Israel as a people

**[EXO 6:6–6:8](https://ref.ly/Exod6:6-Exod6:8)** *See also* [GEN 12:1–12:3](https://ref.ly/Gen12:1-Gen12:3); [EXO 19:3–19:6](https://ref.ly/Exod19:3-Exod19:6); [DEU 4:32–4:34](https://ref.ly/Deut4:32-Deut4:34); [ISA 51:2](https://ref.ly/Isa51:2); [EZK 16:6–16:7](https://ref.ly/Ezek16:6-Ezek16:7); [HOS 11:1–11:4](https://ref.ly/Hos11:1-Hos11:4); [MAL 2:10](https://ref.ly/Mal2:10)

### In saving and delivering his people

**[PSA 106:2](https://ref.ly/Ps106:2)** *This verse introduces a psalm which recounts the history of God's dealings with his people.* *See also* [EXO 33:16–33:17](https://ref.ly/Exod33:16-Exod33:17); [2SA 7:7–7:11](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:7-2Sam7:11); [1KI 18:36–18:38](https://ref.ly/1Kgs18:36-1Kgs18:38); [PSA 28:8–28:9](https://ref.ly/Ps28:8-Ps28:9), [PSA 107:2–107:3](https://ref.ly/Ps107:2-Ps107:3)

### In judgment

[NUM 25:3–25:4](https://ref.ly/Num25:3-Num25:4); ; [1SA 2:25](https://ref.ly/1Sam2:25), [1SA 12:16–12:18](https://ref.ly/1Sam12:16-1Sam12:18); ; [2SA 21:1](https://ref.ly/2Sam21:1)

### In bringing victory in battle

[EXO 14:27–14:28](https://ref.ly/Exod14:27-Exod14:28), [EXO 17:8–17:16](https://ref.ly/Exod17:8-Exod17:16); ; [NUM 21:1–21:3](https://ref.ly/Num21:1-Num21:3); ; [JOS 6:2](https://ref.ly/Josh6:2), [JOS 10:30](https://ref.ly/Josh10:30); ; [JDG 7:9](https://ref.ly/Judg7:9), [JDG 7:22](https://ref.ly/Judg7:22); ; [1SA 17:47](https://ref.ly/1Sam17:47); ; [2CH 20:22–20:23](https://ref.ly/2Chr20:22-2Chr20:23)

### In raising up and sending leaders to the people

[2SA 7:8–7:9](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:8-2Sam7:9); ; [2CH 24:19](https://ref.ly/2Chr24:19); ; [EST 4:14](https://ref.ly/Esth4:14); ; [JER 7:25](https://ref.ly/Jer7:25); ; [ZEC 7:7](https://ref.ly/Zech7:7)

## 1310: God, as judge (id: 1310)

As a part of his sovereignty and authority, God is executor of his righteousness within the created order. Jesus Christ shares in this ongoing work.

God has authority to judge
--------------------------

### God's status as judge

**[PSA 75:7](https://ref.ly/Ps75:7)** *See also* [PSA 50:6](https://ref.ly/Ps50:6), [PSA 76:8–76:9](https://ref.ly/Ps76:8-Ps76:9); [ECC 11:9](https://ref.ly/Eccl11:9); [ISA 33:22](https://ref.ly/Isa33:22), [ISA 66:16](https://ref.ly/Isa66:16); [2TI 4:8](https://ref.ly/2Tim4:8); [HEB 12:23](https://ref.ly/Heb12:23); [JAS 4:12](https://ref.ly/Jas4:12)

### He decides disputes

**[JDG 11:27](https://ref.ly/Judg11:27)** *See also* [GEN 16:5](https://ref.ly/Gen16:5), [GEN 31:53](https://ref.ly/Gen31:53); [1SA 24:15](https://ref.ly/1Sam24:15); [ISA 2:4](https://ref.ly/Isa2:4) parallel [MIC 4:3](https://ref.ly/Mic4:3); [JAS 5:9](https://ref.ly/Jas5:9)

### He presides in the heavenly court

**[ISA 3:13](https://ref.ly/Isa3:13)** *See also* [PSA 50:4](https://ref.ly/Ps50:4), [PSA 82:1](https://ref.ly/Ps82:1); [DAN 7:9–7:10](https://ref.ly/Dan7:9-Dan7:10); [JOL 3:12](https://ref.ly/Joel3:12); [REV 20:11–20:15](https://ref.ly/Rev20:11-Rev20:15)

---------------------------------------

### He judges the earth

### He judges every individual

## 1315: God, as redeemer (id: 1315)

God alone has the ability to save his people from slavery and captivity. God's redemptive will and power is demonstrated in his deliverance of Israel from bondage in Egypt, and supremely through the death and resurrection of Jesus Christ.

God as the sole redeemer of Israel
----------------------------------

**[ISA 47:4](https://ref.ly/Isa47:4)** *See also* [DEU 13:5](https://ref.ly/Deut13:5); [PSA 19:14](https://ref.ly/Ps19:14)

### He redeems because of his love

[DEU 7:8](https://ref.ly/Deut7:8); ; [PSA 44:26](https://ref.ly/Ps44:26)

### He is able to redeem because of his power

[DEU 9:26](https://ref.ly/Deut9:26); ; [2SA 7:23](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:23) parallel [1CH 17:21](https://ref.ly/1Chr17:21); ; [NEH 1:10](https://ref.ly/Neh1:10)

God acts as Israel's redeemer
-----------------------------

## 1320: God, as Saviour (id: 1320)

God is the only Saviour and deliverer of his people. His work of salvation is inaugurated in the OT, and reaches its climax in the work of Jesus Christ.

God is the only Saviour
-----------------------

**[ISA 45:21–45:22](https://ref.ly/Isa45:21-Isa45:22)** *See also* [JDG 10:13–10:14](https://ref.ly/Judg10:13-Judg10:14); [ISA 43:11](https://ref.ly/Isa43:11); [JER 2:28](https://ref.ly/Jer2:28), [JER 3:23](https://ref.ly/Jer3:23), [JER 11:12](https://ref.ly/Jer11:12)

God's deliverance can be worked through a human agent
-----------------------------------------------------

**[JDG 2:16](https://ref.ly/Judg2:16)** *See also* [GEN 45:5–45:7](https://ref.ly/Gen45:5-Gen45:7); [EXO 3:10](https://ref.ly/Exod3:10); [JOS 10:6–10:10](https://ref.ly/Josh10:6-Josh10:10); [JDG 2:18](https://ref.ly/Judg2:18), [JDG 6:14–6:16](https://ref.ly/Judg6:14-Judg6:16); [2KI 13:5](https://ref.ly/2Kgs13:5); [ISA 45:1](https://ref.ly/Isa45:1), [ISA 45:13](https://ref.ly/Isa45:13)

Examples of God's saving deeds
------------------------------

God delivers his people from Egypt: [EXO 6:6–6:7](https://ref.ly/Exod6:6-Exod6:7), [EXO 14:13–14:14](https://ref.ly/Exod14:13-Exod14:14), [EXO 14:21–14:23](https://ref.ly/Exod14:21-Exod14:23), [EXO 14:27–14:28](https://ref.ly/Exod14:27-Exod14:28); ; [PSA 77:19–77:20](https://ref.ly/Ps77:19-Ps77:20); ; [HOS 13:4](https://ref.ly/Hos13:4); [1SA 17:37](https://ref.ly/1Sam17:37); ; [2SA 22:1–22:3](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:1-2Sam22:3) parallel [PSA 18:2](https://ref.ly/Ps18:2); ; [2SA 22:18](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:18) parallel [PSA 18:17](https://ref.ly/Ps18:17); ; [PSA 3:8](https://ref.ly/Ps3:8); [DAN 6:16–6:22](https://ref.ly/Dan6:16-Dan6:22) *God delivers Daniel from the lions' den.*; [ACT 5:18–5:19](https://ref.ly/Acts5:18-Acts5:19), [ACT 12:6–12:11](https://ref.ly/Acts12:6-Acts12:11), [ACT 16:25–16:26](https://ref.ly/Acts16:25-Acts16:26)

God's acts of deliverance reveal his nature and character
---------------------------------------------------------

**[ISA 52:10](https://ref.ly/Isa52:10)** *See also* [PSA 98:2](https://ref.ly/Ps98:2); [ISA 49:6](https://ref.ly/Isa49:6); [LUK 3:4–3:6](https://ref.ly/Luke3:4-Luke3:6); [ISA 40:3–40:5](https://ref.ly/Isa40:3-Isa40:5); [ROM 1:16](https://ref.ly/Rom1:16)

### His strength is seen

**[PSA 18:2](https://ref.ly/Ps18:2)** *“rock” and “horn” symbolise God's strength; they are fequently used to emphasise his ability to save.* *See also* [EXO 15:2](https://ref.ly/Exod15:2) parallel [PSA 118:14](https://ref.ly/Ps118:14); [1SA 2:1](https://ref.ly/1Sam2:1); [2SA 22:2–22:3](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:2-2Sam22:3), [2SA 22:47](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:47) parallel [PSA 18:46](https://ref.ly/Ps18:46); [PSA 28:8](https://ref.ly/Ps28:8)

### His glory is seen

**[EXO 14:4](https://ref.ly/Exod14:4)** *See also* [EXO 14:17–14:18](https://ref.ly/Exod14:17-Exod14:18); [NUM 14:22](https://ref.ly/Num14:22); [PSA 85:9](https://ref.ly/Ps85:9); [ISA 66:19](https://ref.ly/Isa66:19); [EZK 39:21](https://ref.ly/Ezek39:21)

God's deliverance is anticipated
--------------------------------

**[PSA 31:2](https://ref.ly/Ps31:2)** *See also* [GEN 49:18](https://ref.ly/Gen49:18); [PSA 35:4](https://ref.ly/Ps35:4), [PSA 69:13–69:15](https://ref.ly/Ps69:13-Ps69:15); [ISA 33:22](https://ref.ly/Isa33:22), [ISA 35:4](https://ref.ly/Isa35:4)

God's deliverance is promised
-----------------------------

**[EXO 6:6](https://ref.ly/Exod6:6)** *See also* [PSA 50:15](https://ref.ly/Ps50:15), [PSA 91:14](https://ref.ly/Ps91:14); [ISA 38:6](https://ref.ly/Isa38:6), [ISA 46:4](https://ref.ly/Isa46:4); [EZK 34:12](https://ref.ly/Ezek34:12)

Implications of God's deliverance for believers
-----------------------------------------------

### God is able to deliver believers from trials and testing

### God is able to deliver believers from sin and death

**[ROM 7:24–7:25](https://ref.ly/Rom7:24-Rom7:25)** *God delivers both from death owing to adversity and from death that comes about as a result of sin.* *See also* [2SA 12:13](https://ref.ly/2Sam12:13); [PSA 33:19](https://ref.ly/Ps33:19); [EZK 37:23](https://ref.ly/Ezek37:23); [1CO 15:56–15:57](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:56-1Cor15:57); [2CO 1:9–1:10](https://ref.ly/2Cor1:9-2Cor1:10)

-----------------------------------------

## 1325: God, the Creator (id: 1325)

God's power is revealed in the initial creation and the continuing sustenance of the universe. Humanity represents the climax of the Creator's purposes.

God is the Creator
------------------

**[NEH 9:6](https://ref.ly/Neh9:6)** *See also* [GEN 1:1](https://ref.ly/Gen1:1); [ISA 45:7](https://ref.ly/Isa45:7), [ISA 66:2](https://ref.ly/Isa66:2); [EPH 3:9](https://ref.ly/Eph3:9); [REV 4:11](https://ref.ly/Rev4:11)

### God's creative activity demonstrates his uniqueness

**[PSA 96:5](https://ref.ly/Ps96:5)** *See also* [ISA 37:16](https://ref.ly/Isa37:16); [JER 10:11](https://ref.ly/Jer10:11)

### God's creative activity implies that he is good

**[1TI 4:4](https://ref.ly/1Tim4:4)** *See also* [GEN 1:4](https://ref.ly/Gen1:4), [GEN 1:31](https://ref.ly/Gen1:31)

God creates all things
----------------------

### He creates the physical world

**[ISA 45:18](https://ref.ly/Isa45:18)** *See also* [GEN 1:1–1:25](https://ref.ly/Gen1:1-Gen1:25)

### He creates the spiritual world

**[PSA 148:2–148:5](https://ref.ly/Ps148:2-Ps148:5)** *See also* [ROM 8:38–8:39](https://ref.ly/Rom8:38-Rom8:39); [COL 1:16](https://ref.ly/Col1:16)

### The human race is the apex of God's creation

**[PSA 8:3–8:8](https://ref.ly/Ps8:3-Ps8:8)** *See also* [GEN 1:26–1:28](https://ref.ly/Gen1:26-Gen1:28), [GEN 5:1](https://ref.ly/Gen5:1), [GEN 9:6](https://ref.ly/Gen9:6); [PSA 100:3](https://ref.ly/Ps100:3), [PSA 139:13](https://ref.ly/Ps139:13); [ISA 42:5](https://ref.ly/Isa42:5); [ACT 17:26–17:28](https://ref.ly/Acts17:26-Acts17:28)

The Creator's agents
--------------------

### He creates through Jesus Christ

**[1CO 8:6](https://ref.ly/1Cor8:6)** *See also* [JHN 1:3](https://ref.ly/John1:3); [COL 1:16](https://ref.ly/Col1:16); [HEB 1:2](https://ref.ly/Heb1:2)

### He creates by the Spirit

**[JOB 33:4](https://ref.ly/Job33:4)** *See also* [GEN 1:2](https://ref.ly/Gen1:2); [PSA 104:30](https://ref.ly/Ps104:30)

### He creates by his word

**[PSA 33:6](https://ref.ly/Ps33:6)** *See also* [JOB 38:8–38:11](https://ref.ly/Job38:8-Job38:11); [PSA 33:9](https://ref.ly/Ps33:9)

### He creates by wisdom

**[PRO 3:19](https://ref.ly/Prov3:19)** *Wisdom is personified and is active with the Creator.* *See also* [PRO 8:30](https://ref.ly/Prov8:30); [JER 10:12–10:13](https://ref.ly/Jer10:12-Jer10:13)

He creates from nothing
-----------------------

**[HEB 11:3](https://ref.ly/Heb11:3)** *God creates out of non\-existent material, which emphasises the absolute dependence of all creation upon him.* *See also* [JOB 26:7](https://ref.ly/Job26:7); [ROM 4:17](https://ref.ly/Rom4:17)

The Creator sustains the created order
--------------------------------------

**[ISA 44:24](https://ref.ly/Isa44:24)** *The Hebrew indicates continuous activity.* *See also* [DEU 30:20](https://ref.ly/Deut30:20); [JOB 9:8–9:9](https://ref.ly/Job9:8-Job9:9); [PSA 104:2–104:4](https://ref.ly/Ps104:2-Ps104:4); [ISA 42:5](https://ref.ly/Isa42:5)

### Examples of God sustaining creation

**[MAT 5:45](https://ref.ly/Matt5:45)** *See also* [JOB 5:10](https://ref.ly/Job5:10), [JOB 38:31–38:33](https://ref.ly/Job38:31-Job38:33); [MAT 6:28–6:30](https://ref.ly/Matt6:28-Matt6:30)

The Creator watches over his creation
-------------------------------------

**[PSA 33:14](https://ref.ly/Ps33:14)** *See also* [PSA 121:2–121:8](https://ref.ly/Ps121:2-Ps121:8)

The creation is a vehicle for God's self\-revelation
----------------------------------------------------

**[ROM 1:20](https://ref.ly/Rom1:20)** *See also* [PSA 19:1](https://ref.ly/Ps19:1); [ISA 40:26](https://ref.ly/Isa40:26); [AMO 4:13](https://ref.ly/Amos4:13)

God renews his creation through redemption
------------------------------------------

**[JHN 3:17](https://ref.ly/John3:17)**; **[2CO 5:17](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:17)** *See also* [JHN 1:12–1:13](https://ref.ly/John1:12-John1:13); [ROM 4:17](https://ref.ly/Rom4:17), [ROM 6:4](https://ref.ly/Rom6:4), [ROM 8:19–8:23](https://ref.ly/Rom8:19-Rom8:23) *The redemption of the physical world must wait until the sons of God are revealed at the end of time*; [GAL 6:15](https://ref.ly/Gal6:15)

God renews his new creation of believing people
-----------------------------------------------

**[2CO 4:16](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:16)** *See also* [COL 3:10](https://ref.ly/Col3:10)

God will reveal a new universe
------------------------------

**[REV 21:1](https://ref.ly/Rev21:1)** *See also* [REV 21:5](https://ref.ly/Rev21:5); [ISA 65:17](https://ref.ly/Isa65:17)

## 1330: God, the provider (id: 1330)

God supplies the needs of all creation, but gives special care to his own people.

God is called \`\`The LORD who provides''
-----------------------------------------

**[GEN 22:13–22:14](https://ref.ly/Gen22:13-Gen22:14)** *The name “Yahweh Yireh” (or “Jehovah Jireh”) is from the verb “to see”, and means “The LORD foresees” or “The LORD will see to it”.* *See also* [GEN 22:8](https://ref.ly/Gen22:8)

God provides for the needs of all creation
------------------------------------------

### He provides for the earth

**[PSA 65:9–65:13](https://ref.ly/Ps65:9-Ps65:13)** *See also* [DEU 11:12](https://ref.ly/Deut11:12), [DEU 11:14–11:15](https://ref.ly/Deut11:14-Deut11:15); [PSA 68:9](https://ref.ly/Ps68:9), [PSA 104:10–104:18](https://ref.ly/Ps104:10-Ps104:18), [PSA 135:7](https://ref.ly/Ps135:7), [PSA 147:8](https://ref.ly/Ps147:8); [EZK 34:26–34:29](https://ref.ly/Ezek34:26-Ezek34:29)

### He provides for the animals

**[PSA 145:16](https://ref.ly/Ps145:16)** *See also* [JOB 38:41](https://ref.ly/Job38:41); [PSA 104:27–104:28](https://ref.ly/Ps104:27-Ps104:28), [PSA 147:9](https://ref.ly/Ps147:9); [MAT 6:26](https://ref.ly/Matt6:26) parallel [LUK 12:24](https://ref.ly/Luke12:24)

### He provides for all people

**[ACT 14:17](https://ref.ly/Acts14:17)** *See also* [1CH 29:12](https://ref.ly/1Chr29:12); [PSA 68:5](https://ref.ly/Ps68:5), [PSA 107:9](https://ref.ly/Ps107:9); [MAT 5:45](https://ref.ly/Matt5:45); [ACT 17:28](https://ref.ly/Acts17:28)

### He provides for the poor and needy

**[PSA 140:12](https://ref.ly/Ps140:12)** *See also* [1SA 2:8](https://ref.ly/1Sam2:8); [PSA 35:10](https://ref.ly/Ps35:10), [PSA 145:13–145:14](https://ref.ly/Ps145:13-Ps145:14), [PSA 146:7–146:9](https://ref.ly/Ps146:7-Ps146:9); [ISA 25:4](https://ref.ly/Isa25:4)

----------------------------------------------

Food and water in the wilderness: [EXO 16:13–16:18](https://ref.ly/Exod16:13-Exod16:18), [EXO 17:3–17:6](https://ref.ly/Exod17:3-Exod17:6); ; [NUM 11:4–11:9](https://ref.ly/Num11:4-Num11:9), [NUM 11:31–11:32](https://ref.ly/Num11:31-Num11:32); [1KI 17:6](https://ref.ly/1Kgs17:6), [1KI 17:16](https://ref.ly/1Kgs17:16), [1KI 19:5–19:8](https://ref.ly/1Kgs19:5-1Kgs19:8); [2KI 4:42–4:44](https://ref.ly/2Kgs4:42-2Kgs4:44) *Elisha feeds 100 men from 20 barley loaves*; ; [MAT 14:15–14:21](https://ref.ly/Matt14:15-Matt14:21) parallels [MRK 6:35–6:44](https://ref.ly/Mark6:35-Mark6:44), [LUK 9:12–9:17](https://ref.ly/Luke9:12-Luke9:17), [JHN 6:5–6:13](https://ref.ly/John6:5-John6:13) *Jesus Christ feeds 5,000*; ; [MAT 15:32–15:38](https://ref.ly/Matt15:32-Matt15:38) parallel [MRK 8:1–8:9](https://ref.ly/Mark8:1-Mark8:9) *Jesus Christ feeds 4,000*

------------------------------------------

## 1335: blessing (id: 1335)

Spiritual and material benefits given by God to be enjoyed. Blessing the name of God is also the appropriate response of believers to all that God has done for them.

God is the source of all blessing
---------------------------------

**[1CH 29:11–29:12](https://ref.ly/1Chr29:11-1Chr29:12)** *See also* [PSA 89:11](https://ref.ly/Ps89:11)

### At creation he blessed humans with fertility and authority over the earth

**[GEN 1:28–1:30](https://ref.ly/Gen1:28-Gen1:30)**

## 1340: consistency (id: 1340)

God's nature, plans and purpose do not change. The same consistent plan of salvation can be seen throughout the OT and NT, culminating in Jesus Christ who is “the same yesterday and today and for ever”. Believers are also called to show the same consistency in their faith and witness.

God's nature is consistent and unchanging
-----------------------------------------

**[MAL 3:6](https://ref.ly/Mal3:6)** *See also* [PSA 102:27](https://ref.ly/Ps102:27); [JAS 1:17](https://ref.ly/Jas1:17)

God's plans and purpose are consistent and unchanging
-----------------------------------------------------

**[PSA 33:11](https://ref.ly/Ps33:11)** *See also* [NUM 23:19](https://ref.ly/Num23:19); [1SA 15:29](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:29); [JOB 36:5](https://ref.ly/Job36:5); [PSA 89:34](https://ref.ly/Ps89:34); [TIT 1:2](https://ref.ly/Titus1:2); [HEB 7:21](https://ref.ly/Heb7:21); [PSA 110:4](https://ref.ly/Ps110:4)

God's plan of salvation is consistent
-------------------------------------

**[GEN 12:2–12:3](https://ref.ly/Gen12:2-Gen12:3)**; **[HEB 6:17–6:18](https://ref.ly/Heb6:17-Heb6:18), [HEB 13:8](https://ref.ly/Heb13:8)** *See also* [GEN 18:18](https://ref.ly/Gen18:18), [GEN 22:17–22:18](https://ref.ly/Gen22:17-Gen22:18), [GEN 26:4](https://ref.ly/Gen26:4), [GEN 28:14](https://ref.ly/Gen28:14); [DEU 18:15](https://ref.ly/Deut18:15), [DEU 18:18](https://ref.ly/Deut18:18); [PSA 72:17](https://ref.ly/Ps72:17); [JER 4:1–4:2](https://ref.ly/Jer4:1-Jer4:2); [ZEC 8:13](https://ref.ly/Zech8:13); [ACT 3:23–3:26](https://ref.ly/Acts3:23-Acts3:26); [GAL 3:8](https://ref.ly/Gal3:8)

Believers are to live lives consistent with their profession of faith
---------------------------------------------------------------------

**[EPH 4:1](https://ref.ly/Eph4:1)**; **[PHP 1:27](https://ref.ly/Phil1:27)** *See also* [MAT 5:37](https://ref.ly/Matt5:37); [1TH 4:12](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:12); [1TI 3:7](https://ref.ly/1Tim3:7); [HEB 13:7](https://ref.ly/Heb13:7); [JAS 5:12](https://ref.ly/Jas5:12); [2PE 3:11](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:11)

## 1345: covenant (id: 1345)

God's commitment to, and requirement of, his people expressed in promise, law, judgment, faithfulness and mercy. Also used of commitment within human relationships based upon agreements.

* **Associated Articles:** 1346: covenants, nature of (ID: `1346@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1347: covenant, God's with Noah (ID: `1347@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1348: covenant, God's with Abraham (ID: `1348@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1349: covenant, God's at Sinai (ID: `1349@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1350: covenant, God's with Israel's priests (ID: `1350@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1351: covenant, God's with David (ID: `1351@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1352: covenant, the new (ID: `1352@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 1346: covenants, nature of (id: 1346)

A solemn agreement or promise, sometimes confirmed by sacrifice or by sharing in a meal, by which two or more parties commit themselves to the rights and responsibilities demanded by their relationship and their agreed course of action, and accept the serious consequences of breaking faith.

Kinds of covenant relationship
------------------------------

### The relationship between king and people

**[2SA 5:3](https://ref.ly/2Sam5:3)** parallel [1CH 11:3](https://ref.ly/1Chr11:3) *See also* [2SA 3:21](https://ref.ly/2Sam3:21); [2KI 11:17](https://ref.ly/2Kgs11:17); [2CH 23:3](https://ref.ly/2Chr23:3)

### Terms for peace granted to a weaker party

**[JOS 9:15](https://ref.ly/Josh9:15)** *See also* [1SA 11:1](https://ref.ly/1Sam11:1); [1KI 15:19–15:20](https://ref.ly/1Kgs15:19-1Kgs15:20), [1KI 20:34](https://ref.ly/1Kgs20:34); [EZK 17:13–17:14](https://ref.ly/Ezek17:13-Ezek17:14)

### A mutual commitment to peaceful relations

**[1KI 5:12](https://ref.ly/1Kgs5:12)** *See also* [GEN 21:27](https://ref.ly/Gen21:27), [GEN 26:28–26:29](https://ref.ly/Gen26:28-Gen26:29), [GEN 31:44](https://ref.ly/Gen31:44); [AMO 1:9](https://ref.ly/Amos1:9)

### An agreement on a common course of action

**[JER 34:8](https://ref.ly/Jer34:8)** *See also* [2KI 11:4](https://ref.ly/2Kgs11:4) parallel [2CH 23:1](https://ref.ly/2Chr23:1); [EZR 10:3](https://ref.ly/Ezra10:3); [NEH 9:38](https://ref.ly/Neh9:38); [PSA 83:5](https://ref.ly/Ps83:5)

### The relationship between husband and wife

[PRO 2:17](https://ref.ly/Prov2:17); ; [MAL 2:14](https://ref.ly/Mal2:14); [JER 2:2](https://ref.ly/Jer2:2); ; [EZK 16:8](https://ref.ly/Ezek16:8)

### An expression of friendship

**[1SA 18:3](https://ref.ly/1Sam18:3)** *See also* [1SA 20:16–20:17](https://ref.ly/1Sam20:16-1Sam20:17)

Sealing a covenant
------------------

### By sharing a meal

[GEN 26:30](https://ref.ly/Gen26:30), [GEN 31:53–31:54](https://ref.ly/Gen31:53-Gen31:54); [MAT 26:26–26:29](https://ref.ly/Matt26:26-Matt26:29) parallels [MRK 14:22–14:25](https://ref.ly/Mark14:22-Mark14:25), [LUK 22:17–22:20](https://ref.ly/Luke22:17-Luke22:20); ; [1CO 11:23–11:25](https://ref.ly/1Cor11:23-1Cor11:25)

### By offering a sacrifice

[JER 34:18–34:19](https://ref.ly/Jer34:18-Jer34:19) *The Hebrew expression for making a covenant means, literally, “to cut a covenant”. This may refer to the solemn practice, described here, of cutting an animal in half and walking between its pieces*; ; [GEN 15:9–15:18](https://ref.ly/Gen15:9-Gen15:18); ; [EXO 24:4–24:8](https://ref.ly/Exod24:4-Exod24:8); ; [PSA 50:5](https://ref.ly/Ps50:5); ; [HEB 12:24](https://ref.ly/Heb12:24) *Sacrifice is an important part in sealing covenants made by God.*

### By making an oath

[GEN 21:31](https://ref.ly/Gen21:31), [GEN 26:31](https://ref.ly/Gen26:31); ; [JOS 9:15](https://ref.ly/Josh9:15); ; [2KI 11:4](https://ref.ly/2Kgs11:4); ; [NEH 10:28–10:29](https://ref.ly/Neh10:28-Neh10:29)

The obligations of a covenant
-----------------------------

### Covenant responsibilities must be honoured

**[NUM 30:2](https://ref.ly/Num30:2)**; **[1SA 20:8](https://ref.ly/1Sam20:8)** *See also* [JOS 9:18](https://ref.ly/Josh9:18); [MAT 5:33–5:37](https://ref.ly/Matt5:33-Matt5:37); [GAL 3:15](https://ref.ly/Gal3:15)

### Covenant obligations are watched over by God

**[1SA 20:42](https://ref.ly/1Sam20:42)** *See also* [GEN 31:48–31:54](https://ref.ly/Gen31:48-Gen31:54); [JOS 9:19](https://ref.ly/Josh9:19); [JER 34:15–34:16](https://ref.ly/Jer34:15-Jer34:16); [MAL 2:14–2:16](https://ref.ly/Mal2:14-Mal2:16)

### The consequences of breaking covenant faith

**[JOS 9:20](https://ref.ly/Josh9:20)** *See also* [JER 34:18–34:22](https://ref.ly/Jer34:18-Jer34:22); [EZK 17:16–17:18](https://ref.ly/Ezek17:16-Ezek17:18); [AMO 1:9](https://ref.ly/Amos1:9)

Covenants with other nations are forbidden
------------------------------------------

[ISA 28:15](https://ref.ly/Isa28:15), [ISA 28:18](https://ref.ly/Isa28:18), [ISA 30:1–30:2](https://ref.ly/Isa30:1-Isa30:2), [ISA 31:1](https://ref.ly/Isa31:1); ; [HOS 12:1](https://ref.ly/Hos12:1)

## 1347: covenant, God's with Noah (id: 1347)

God's confirmation of, and commitment to maintain, his relationship with the natural order\- implicit in the act of creation\- whereby he promised never again to destroy the earth with a flood. This divine pledge, given unconditionally to Noah and to every living creature on earth, was accompanied by the sign of the rainbow.

The occasion of the covenant
----------------------------

### The flood as divine judgment

**[GEN 6:17](https://ref.ly/Gen6:17)** *See also* [GEN 6:5–6:7](https://ref.ly/Gen6:5-Gen6:7), [GEN 6:11–6:13](https://ref.ly/Gen6:11-Gen6:13); [2PE 2:5](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:5)

### God's promise of salvation to Noah and his family

**[GEN 6:18](https://ref.ly/Gen6:18)** *See also* [GEN 7:23](https://ref.ly/Gen7:23), [GEN 8:1](https://ref.ly/Gen8:1), [GEN 8:15–8:17](https://ref.ly/Gen8:15-Gen8:17); [HEB 11:7](https://ref.ly/Heb11:7); [1PE 3:20](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:20)

### God's promise never again to destroy the earth with a flood

**[GEN 9:11](https://ref.ly/Gen9:11)** *See also* [GEN 8:21](https://ref.ly/Gen8:21); [ISA 54:9](https://ref.ly/Isa54:9)

The sign of the covenant
------------------------

**[GEN 9:13](https://ref.ly/Gen9:13)** *See also* [GEN 9:14–9:17](https://ref.ly/Gen9:14-Gen9:17)

A universal covenant
--------------------

### God's relationship with every living creature

**[GEN 9:8–9:10](https://ref.ly/Gen9:8-Gen9:10)** *See also* [GEN 7:1–7:3](https://ref.ly/Gen7:1-Gen7:3); [EZK 34:25](https://ref.ly/Ezek34:25); [HOS 2:18](https://ref.ly/Hos2:18); [ZEC 11:10](https://ref.ly/Zech11:10)

### God's relationship with the natural order

**[GEN 8:22](https://ref.ly/Gen8:22)**; **[JER 33:25–33:26](https://ref.ly/Jer33:25-Jer33:26)** *God's relationship with the created order is here expressed as a covenant. It is probable that this is a reference to the Noahic covenant through which the implicit relationship between Creator and creation was confirmed.* *See also* [GEN 1:14](https://ref.ly/Gen1:14), [GEN 1:31](https://ref.ly/Gen1:31), [GEN 2:1](https://ref.ly/Gen2:1); [PSA 74:16–74:17](https://ref.ly/Ps74:16-Ps74:17); [JER 5:24](https://ref.ly/Jer5:24), [JER 33:20–33:21](https://ref.ly/Jer33:20-Jer33:21)

An everlasting covenant
-----------------------

**[GEN 9:16](https://ref.ly/Gen9:16)** *See also* [GEN 9:12](https://ref.ly/Gen9:12)**[ISA 24:5](https://ref.ly/Isa24:5)** *The reference here is to the Noahic covenant. Though this covenant was unconditional, the prohibition of bloodshed\-\-often described as bringing pollution to the land\-\-was associated with it. There may be, also, a wider reference to the effects of mankind's disregard for the norms laid down at creation.* *See also* [GEN 9:6](https://ref.ly/Gen9:6); [NUM 35:33](https://ref.ly/Num35:33); [ISA 26:21](https://ref.ly/Isa26:21)

* **Associated Passages:** Genesis 6:17; Genesis 6:5-7; Genesis 6:11-13; 2 Peter 2:5; Genesis 6:18; Genesis 7:23; Genesis 8:1; Genesis 8:15-17; Hebrews 11:7; 1 Peter 3:20; Genesis 9:11; Genesis 8:21; Isaiah 54:9; Genesis 9:13; Genesis 9:14-17; Genesis 9:8-10; Genesis 7:1-3; Ezekiel 34:25; Hosea 2:18; Zechariah 11:10; Genesis 8:22; Jeremiah 33:25-26; Genesis 1:14; Genesis 1:31; Genesis 2:1; Psalms 74:16-17; Jeremiah 5:24; Jeremiah 33:20-21; Genesis 9:16; Genesis 9:12; Isaiah 24:5; Genesis 9:6; Numbers 35:33; Isaiah 26:21
* **Associated Articles:** 4005: creation (ID: `4005@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 4845: rainbow (ID: `4845@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5106: Noah (ID: `5106@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5467: promises, divine (ID: `5467@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7203: ark, Noah's (ID: `7203@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7227: flood, the (ID: `7227@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 1348: covenant, God's with Abraham (id: 1348)

God's gracious promise made to Abraham, and repeated to his descendants, to bless both them and, through them, the whole world. In response God calls for faithful obedience, expressed particularly in the outward sign of circumcision.

Features of the Abrahamic covenant
----------------------------------

### The covenant is based upon God's gracious promise

**[GAL 3:18](https://ref.ly/Gal3:18)** *See also* [GEN 15:4–15:7](https://ref.ly/Gen15:4-Gen15:7), [GEN 17:4–17:8](https://ref.ly/Gen17:4-Gen17:8), [GEN 18:10](https://ref.ly/Gen18:10), [GEN 18:14](https://ref.ly/Gen18:14); [HEB 6:13–6:15](https://ref.ly/Heb6:13-Heb6:15)

### The covenant was confirmed by sacrifice

[GEN 15:9–15:18](https://ref.ly/Gen15:9-Gen15:18)

### The covenant was given in perpetuity

**[GEN 17:7](https://ref.ly/Gen17:7)** *See also* [GEN 17:13](https://ref.ly/Gen17:13), [GEN 17:19](https://ref.ly/Gen17:19); [1CH 16:15–16:17](https://ref.ly/1Chr16:15-1Chr16:17) parallel [PSA 105:8–105:10](https://ref.ly/Ps105:8-Ps105:10); [JER 33:23–33:25](https://ref.ly/Jer33:23-Jer33:25)

God's promises to Abraham
-------------------------

--------------------------------

### Obedience

**[GEN 17:9–17:14](https://ref.ly/Gen17:9-Gen17:14)** *Circumcision is the sign of Abraham's commitment to God's covenant with him*; **[GEN 22:18](https://ref.ly/Gen22:18)** *See also* [GEN 26:5](https://ref.ly/Gen26:5); [NUM 32:11](https://ref.ly/Num32:11) *by contrast, the consequences of disobedience*; [HEB 11:8](https://ref.ly/Heb11:8), [HEB 11:17–11:19](https://ref.ly/Heb11:17-Heb11:19)

-------------------------
