## 1349: covenant, God's at Sinai (id: 1349)

God's faithful commitment, made in pursuance of his promises to Abraham, to acknowledge the newly\-redeemed Israel as his own special people. Israel's required response to the grace of God in election was to be holiness and obedience to the law.

The occasion of the covenant
----------------------------

### The covenant fulfilled God's promises to Abraham

**[DEU 29:12–29:13](https://ref.ly/Deut29:12-Deut29:13)** *See also* [EXO 2:24](https://ref.ly/Exod2:24), [EXO 6:4–6:8](https://ref.ly/Exod6:4-Exod6:8); [DEU 7:8](https://ref.ly/Deut7:8)

### The covenant followed Israel's redemption from slavery

**[JER 34:13](https://ref.ly/Jer34:13)** *God's covenant at Sinai was made in the context of his historical acts of deliverance. Covenants (“treaties”) between a supreme (suzerain) overlord and a subordinate ruler (vassal) are well known in ancient Near Eastern writings. They are not “agreements” but “requirements”.* *See also* [EXO 20:2](https://ref.ly/Exod20:2) parallel [DEU 5:6](https://ref.ly/Deut5:6); [LEV 26:45](https://ref.ly/Lev26:45)

### The covenant was mediated through Moses

[EXO 34:27](https://ref.ly/Exod34:27); ; [LEV 26:46](https://ref.ly/Lev26:46); ; [DEU 29:1](https://ref.ly/Deut29:1); ; [JHN 1:17](https://ref.ly/John1:17)

### The covenant was accompanied by signs of God's presence

[EXO 19:18–19:19](https://ref.ly/Exod19:18-Exod19:19), [EXO 20:18–20:19](https://ref.ly/Exod20:18-Exod20:19), [EXO 24:16](https://ref.ly/Exod24:16); ; [PSA 68:8](https://ref.ly/Ps68:8)

Sealing the covenant
--------------------

### Sharing a meal

[EXO 24:11](https://ref.ly/Exod24:11)

### Offering a sacrifice

[EXO 24:5–24:8](https://ref.ly/Exod24:5-Exod24:8); ; [PSA 50:5](https://ref.ly/Ps50:5)

### God's oath

[DEU 28:9](https://ref.ly/Deut28:9), [DEU 29:14](https://ref.ly/Deut29:14); ; [EZK 16:8](https://ref.ly/Ezek16:8)

### Israel's promise

[EXO 19:8](https://ref.ly/Exod19:8), [EXO 24:3](https://ref.ly/Exod24:3), [EXO 24:7](https://ref.ly/Exod24:7)

The covenant relationship
-------------------------

### Israel as God's people

**[DEU 7:6](https://ref.ly/Deut7:6)** *See also* [EXO 19:5–19:6](https://ref.ly/Exod19:5-Exod19:6); [LEV 26:12](https://ref.ly/Lev26:12); [DEU 14:2](https://ref.ly/Deut14:2); [JER 13:11](https://ref.ly/Jer13:11)

### Israel adopted into God's family

**[HOS 11:1](https://ref.ly/Hos11:1)** *See also* [DEU 1:30–1:31](https://ref.ly/Deut1:30-Deut1:31), [DEU 8:5](https://ref.ly/Deut8:5); [ISA 63:16](https://ref.ly/Isa63:16); [MAL 2:10](https://ref.ly/Mal2:10)

### Israel as God's bride

**[JER 2:2](https://ref.ly/Jer2:2)** *See also* [ISA 54:5–54:8](https://ref.ly/Isa54:5-Isa54:8); [JER 31:32](https://ref.ly/Jer31:32); [EZK 16:8](https://ref.ly/Ezek16:8); [HOS 2:14–2:16](https://ref.ly/Hos2:14-Hos2:16)

The blessings of the covenant
-----------------------------

### Inheriting God's promises

[DEU 6:3](https://ref.ly/Deut6:3), [DEU 26:18–26:19](https://ref.ly/Deut26:18-Deut26:19), [DEU 28:9](https://ref.ly/Deut28:9); ; [JOS 23:5](https://ref.ly/Josh23:5)

### Provision and protection

[LEV 26:3–26:13](https://ref.ly/Lev26:3-Lev26:13); ; [DEU 28:1–28:14](https://ref.ly/Deut28:1-Deut28:14) *This pattern of blessings and curses is also a feature of Near Eastern political treaties.*

The requirements of the covenant
--------------------------------

### Obedience to the law

**[EXO 24:7](https://ref.ly/Exod24:7), [EXO 34:27–34:28](https://ref.ly/Exod34:27-Exod34:28)** *See also* [DEU 4:13](https://ref.ly/Deut4:13); [JOS 8:31](https://ref.ly/Josh8:31); [NEH 8:1](https://ref.ly/Neh8:1)

### Holiness

**[DEU 14:2](https://ref.ly/Deut14:2)** *Israel has been made holy through her election as the covenant people of God. The ensuing call for holiness is a call to work out the implications of that relationship and to live in accordance with its demands*; **[LEV 11:45](https://ref.ly/Lev11:45)** *See also* [LEV 20:26](https://ref.ly/Lev20:26)

### Wholehearted devotion

**[EXO 34:14](https://ref.ly/Exod34:14)**; **[DEU 10:12](https://ref.ly/Deut10:12)** *See also* [EXO 23:32](https://ref.ly/Exod23:32); [DEU 4:23](https://ref.ly/Deut4:23), [DEU 6:5](https://ref.ly/Deut6:5), [DEU 10:20](https://ref.ly/Deut10:20); [JOS 24:14–24:15](https://ref.ly/Josh24:14-Josh24:15)

Breaking the covenant
---------------------

### The consequences of breaking the covenant

Disease: [LEV 26:15–26:16](https://ref.ly/Lev26:15-Lev26:16); ; [DEU 28:21–28:22](https://ref.ly/Deut28:21-Deut28:22); [LEV 26:19–26:20](https://ref.ly/Lev26:19-Lev26:20); ; [DEU 28:23–28:24](https://ref.ly/Deut28:23-Deut28:24); [LEV 26:17](https://ref.ly/Lev26:17), [LEV 26:25](https://ref.ly/Lev26:25); ; [DEU 28:25](https://ref.ly/Deut28:25); [LEV 26:32–26:33](https://ref.ly/Lev26:32-Lev26:33); ; [DEU 28:36–28:37](https://ref.ly/Deut28:36-Deut28:37); ; [JOS 23:16](https://ref.ly/Josh23:16); ; [EZK 17:19–17:20](https://ref.ly/Ezek17:19-Ezek17:20)

### Israel's unfaithfulness to the covenant

**[PSA 78:37](https://ref.ly/Ps78:37)** *See also* [2KI 18:12](https://ref.ly/2Kgs18:12); [1CH 5:25](https://ref.ly/1Chr5:25); [JER 3:8](https://ref.ly/Jer3:8), [JER 11:10](https://ref.ly/Jer11:10); [EZK 16:32](https://ref.ly/Ezek16:32); [HOS 6:7](https://ref.ly/Hos6:7)

God's commitment to the covenant
--------------------------------

### God's covenant of love

**[DEU 7:9](https://ref.ly/Deut7:9)** *“love” translates the Hebrew word “hesed”, which here expresses God's loyalty and faithful commitment to his covenant people.* *See also* [NEH 1:5](https://ref.ly/Neh1:5); [DAN 9:4](https://ref.ly/Dan9:4)

### The everlasting covenant

**[EZK 16:60](https://ref.ly/Ezek16:60)** *God's faithfulness to the covenant at Sinai will result in a new covenant that will never come to an end.* *See also* [ISA 61:8](https://ref.ly/Isa61:8); [JER 32:40](https://ref.ly/Jer32:40)

Renewing the covenant
---------------------

## 1350: covenant, God's with Israel's priests (id: 1350)

God's promise to the Levites, and to the family of Phinehas in particular, to maintain those who serve him faithfully in a lasting priesthood.

God's covenant with Phinehas
----------------------------

**[NUM 25:12–25:13](https://ref.ly/Num25:12-Num25:13)** *Phinehas was the grandson of Aaron. God's pledge of “a lasting priesthood”, granted to him as a result of his zeal, probably means that the high priesthood would remain in his family.* *See also* [NUM 25:10–25:11](https://ref.ly/Num25:10-Num25:11); [EZR 7:1–7:5](https://ref.ly/Ezra7:1-Ezra7:5); [PSA 106:30–106:31](https://ref.ly/Ps106:30-Ps106:31)

God's covenant with the Levites
-------------------------------

### An everlasting covenant

**[NUM 18:19](https://ref.ly/Num18:19)** *This covenant confirms the privileges and responsibilities of Aaron and his fellow Levites who have been called to Israel's priesthood. The reference to “salt” may underline the permanent nature of the covenant. God's covenant with David is also described as a “covenant of salt”.* *See also* [2CH 13:5](https://ref.ly/2Chr13:5); [JER 33:18–33:22](https://ref.ly/Jer33:18-Jer33:22)

### Requirements of the covenant

**[MAL 2:5–2:6](https://ref.ly/Mal2:5-Mal2:6)**

### The Levites' portion is the LORD

**[DEU 10:8–10:9](https://ref.ly/Deut10:8-Deut10:9)** *See also* [NUM 3:12](https://ref.ly/Num3:12)

### The covenant violated

**[MAL 2:8](https://ref.ly/Mal2:8)** *By their unfaithfulness, Judah's priests have forfeited the blessings of God's promise to Levi.* *See also* [NEH 13:29](https://ref.ly/Neh13:29)

* **Associated Passages:** Numbers 25:12-13; Numbers 25:10-11; Ezra 7:1-5; Psalms 106:30-31; Numbers 18:19; 2 Chronicles 13:5; Jeremiah 33:18-22; Malachi 2:5-6; Deuteronomy 10:8-9; Numbers 3:12; Malachi 2:8; Nehemiah 13:29
* **Associated Articles:** 5073: Aaron, as model priest (ID: `5073@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7364: fellowship offering (ID: `7364@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7376: high priest (ID: `7376@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7390: Levites (ID: `7390@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7412: priesthood (ID: `7412@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7766: priests (ID: `7766@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 1351: covenant, God's with David (id: 1351)

God's promise to establish David and his descendants on Israel's throne for ever. It provided Israel with a basis for the hope of deliverance and restoration, and became a focus for the Messianic expectation which was fulfilled, ultimately, in Jesus Christ.

God's promise to establish David's line
---------------------------------------

### God's election of David

**[PSA 78:70](https://ref.ly/Ps78:70)** *See also* [2SA 6:21](https://ref.ly/2Sam6:21); [1KI 8:16](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:16) parallel [2CH 6:6](https://ref.ly/2Chr6:6)

### God's covenant is everlasting

**[PSA 89:3–89:4](https://ref.ly/Ps89:3-Ps89:4)** *See also* [2SA 7:11–7:16](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:11-2Sam7:16), [2SA 23:5](https://ref.ly/2Sam23:5); [1KI 2:45](https://ref.ly/1Kgs2:45); [2CH 13:5](https://ref.ly/2Chr13:5); [PSA 18:50](https://ref.ly/Ps18:50), [PSA 89:28–89:29](https://ref.ly/Ps89:28-Ps89:29), [PSA 89:35–89:37](https://ref.ly/Ps89:35-Ps89:37); [JER 33:17](https://ref.ly/Jer33:17)

### God's covenant is inherited through obedience

**[PSA 132:11–132:12](https://ref.ly/Ps132:11-Ps132:12)** *Though God's promise to maintain David's throne is unbreakable, individual descendants must continue to be faithful if they are to inherit the blessings promised to David.* *See also* [1KI 8:25–8:26](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:25-1Kgs8:26) parallel [2CH 6:16–6:17](https://ref.ly/2Chr6:16-2Chr6:17); [1KI 9:4–9:5](https://ref.ly/1Kgs9:4-1Kgs9:5) parallel [2CH 7:17–7:18](https://ref.ly/2Chr7:17-2Chr7:18)

### God's covenant blessings are forfeited through disobedience

**[JER 22:4–22:5](https://ref.ly/Jer22:4-Jer22:5)** *Failure to remain faithful to God brings judgment on the royal house and the people.* *See also* [1KI 9:6–9:9](https://ref.ly/1Kgs9:6-1Kgs9:9) parallel [2CH 7:19–7:22](https://ref.ly/2Chr7:19-2Chr7:22); [1KI 11:11–11:13](https://ref.ly/1Kgs11:11-1Kgs11:13), [1KI 11:31–11:33](https://ref.ly/1Kgs11:31-1Kgs11:33); [JER 7:24–7:26](https://ref.ly/Jer7:24-Jer7:26), [JER 22:6–22:9](https://ref.ly/Jer22:6-Jer22:9), [JER 36:30–36:31](https://ref.ly/Jer36:30-Jer36:31)

### God's promise is fulfilled by grace

**[2CH 21:7](https://ref.ly/2Chr21:7)** parallel [2KI 8:19](https://ref.ly/2Kgs8:19) *Though particular kings may suffer God's anger because of their sin, God's faithfulness to the house of David as a whole, and thus to the nation of Israel, will continue.* *See also* [1KI 11:34–11:36](https://ref.ly/1Kgs11:34-1Kgs11:36), [1KI 11:39](https://ref.ly/1Kgs11:39), [1KI 15:4](https://ref.ly/1Kgs15:4); [PSA 89:30–89:34](https://ref.ly/Ps89:30-Ps89:34)

The Davidic covenant as a basis for hope
----------------------------------------

### God's election of Jerusalem

**[2KI 21:7](https://ref.ly/2Kgs21:7)** parallel [2CH 33:7](https://ref.ly/2Chr33:7) *God's Name signifies his presence. God's choice of David was closely related to his choice of Jerusalem, the city established by David, as the place where the divine presence symbolised in the temple and the ark of the covenant was to be found.* *See also* [1KI 8:20–8:21](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:20-1Kgs8:21) parallel [2CH 6:10–6:11](https://ref.ly/2Chr6:10-2Chr6:11); [1KI 11:32](https://ref.ly/1Kgs11:32), [1KI 11:36](https://ref.ly/1Kgs11:36); [1CH 23:25](https://ref.ly/1Chr23:25); [2CH 6:41–6:42](https://ref.ly/2Chr6:41-2Chr6:42) parallel [PSA 132:8–132:10](https://ref.ly/Ps132:8-Ps132:10)

### God's promise to defend Jerusalem

**[ISA 37:35](https://ref.ly/Isa37:35)** parallel [2KI 19:34](https://ref.ly/2Kgs19:34) *See also* [2KI 19:20](https://ref.ly/2Kgs19:20); [ZEC 12:7–12:9](https://ref.ly/Zech12:7-Zech12:9)

### God's promise to restore David's house

**[AMO 9:11](https://ref.ly/Amos9:11)** *See also* [ACT 15:16](https://ref.ly/Acts15:16); [JER 33:25–33:26](https://ref.ly/Jer33:25-Jer33:26)

Hopes expressed in the Davidic covenant are focused in the Messiah
------------------------------------------------------------------

### The Messiah fulfils the Davidic hope

**[JER 23:5–23:6](https://ref.ly/Jer23:5-Jer23:6)** *See also* [PSA 110:1–110:2](https://ref.ly/Ps110:1-Ps110:2); [ISA 9:7](https://ref.ly/Isa9:7), [ISA 11:1–11:2](https://ref.ly/Isa11:1-Isa11:2), [ISA 16:5](https://ref.ly/Isa16:5), [ISA 55:3](https://ref.ly/Isa55:3); [EZK 34:23–34:25](https://ref.ly/Ezek34:23-Ezek34:25); [ZEC 3:8](https://ref.ly/Zech3:8); [JHN 7:42](https://ref.ly/John7:42)

### God's promise to David fulfilled in Jesus Christ

**[LUK 1:32–1:33](https://ref.ly/Luke1:32-Luke1:33)**; **[REV 22:16](https://ref.ly/Rev22:16)** *See also* [MAT 1:1](https://ref.ly/Matt1:1), [MAT 22:41–22:46](https://ref.ly/Matt22:41-Matt22:46) parallels [MRK 12:35–12:37](https://ref.ly/Mark12:35-Mark12:37), [LUK 20:41–20:44](https://ref.ly/Luke20:41-Luke20:44)MRK [11:10](https://ref.ly/Luke11:10) parallel [MAT 21:9](https://ref.ly/Matt21:9); [LUK 24:21](https://ref.ly/Luke24:21); [ACT 1:6](https://ref.ly/Acts1:6)[ACT 2:29–2:31](https://ref.ly/Acts2:29-Acts2:31), [ACT 13:34](https://ref.ly/Acts13:34); [ROM 1:3](https://ref.ly/Rom1:3); [2TI 2:8](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:8)

## 1352: covenant, the new (id: 1352)

The fulfilment of God's purposes of salvation expressed in the covenants of the OT, mediated by Jesus Christ and sealed in his blood. It is a covenant of grace, the benefits of which include forgiveness, a renewed relationship with God and, through the Holy Spirit, an inward transformation that enables obedience to its demands and so ensures that it will not again be broken. **[JER 31:31](https://ref.ly/Jer31:31)** *The “new” covenant is contrasted with the covenant made at Sinai which is sometimes referred to as the “old” or “first” covenant.*

The new covenant fulfils the OT covenants
-----------------------------------------

### God's covenant with Noah

[ISA 54:9–54:10](https://ref.ly/Isa54:9-Isa54:10); ; [HOS 2:18](https://ref.ly/Hos2:18)

### God's covenant with Abraham

[LUK 1:72–1:73](https://ref.ly/Luke1:72-Luke1:73); ; [ACT 3:25–3:26](https://ref.ly/Acts3:25-Acts3:26); ; [GAL 3:14–3:16](https://ref.ly/Gal3:14-Gal3:16)

### God's covenant at Sinai

[EZK 16:60](https://ref.ly/Ezek16:60), [EZK 16:62](https://ref.ly/Ezek16:62), [EZK 20:37](https://ref.ly/Ezek20:37)

### God's covenant with David

[ISA 55:3](https://ref.ly/Isa55:3); ; [EZK 34:24–34:26](https://ref.ly/Ezek34:24-Ezek34:26), [EZK 37:25–37:26](https://ref.ly/Ezek37:25-Ezek37:26); ; [LUK 1:69](https://ref.ly/Luke1:69)

Jesus Christ, the mediator of the new covenant
----------------------------------------------

### The new covenant fulfilled in the Messiah

**[MAL 3:1](https://ref.ly/Mal3:1)** *See also* [ISA 42:6](https://ref.ly/Isa42:6), [ISA 49:8](https://ref.ly/Isa49:8)

### The new covenant effected through Jesus Christ's death

**[HEB 9:15](https://ref.ly/Heb9:15)** *See also* [HEB 9:16–9:17](https://ref.ly/Heb9:16-Heb9:17)

### The new covenant sealed in Jesus Christ's blood

**[LUK 22:20](https://ref.ly/Luke22:20)** parallels [MAT 26:28](https://ref.ly/Matt26:28), [MRK 14:24](https://ref.ly/Mark14:24) *See also* [EXO 24:8](https://ref.ly/Exod24:8) *Blood was an important element in sealing the Sinaitic covenant*; [JHN 6:54](https://ref.ly/John6:54); [1CO 10:16](https://ref.ly/1Cor10:16), [1CO 11:25](https://ref.ly/1Cor11:25); [HEB 10:29](https://ref.ly/Heb10:29)

The ministry of the Holy Spirit
-------------------------------

**[2CO 3:6](https://ref.ly/2Cor3:6), [2CO 3:18](https://ref.ly/2Cor3:18)** *See also* [ISA 59:21](https://ref.ly/Isa59:21); [EZK 36:26–36:27](https://ref.ly/Ezek36:26-Ezek36:27); [ROM 8:2–8:4](https://ref.ly/Rom8:2-Rom8:4); [2CO 3:8](https://ref.ly/2Cor3:8)

The superior blessings of the new covenant
------------------------------------------

### God's grace and mercy

**[HEB 12:24](https://ref.ly/Heb12:24)** *The blood of Abel cried out to God for justice and retribution; the blood of Jesus Christ, shed to seal the new covenant, cries out for mercy and forgiveness.*

### A complete forgiveness

**[HEB 8:12](https://ref.ly/Heb8:12)** *See also* [JER 31:34](https://ref.ly/Jer31:34); [ROM 11:27](https://ref.ly/Rom11:27); [HEB 10:17](https://ref.ly/Heb10:17)

### Release from the law's condemnation

[2CO 3:9](https://ref.ly/2Cor3:9); ; [GAL 3:13–3:14](https://ref.ly/Gal3:13-Gal3:14)

### An inward enabling to obey God's laws

**[JER 31:32–31:33](https://ref.ly/Jer31:32-Jer31:33)** *The old covenant was broken because its demands were not met. Under the new covenant the requirements of obedience are not abolished, but in writing his laws on human hearts, God gives the ability to meet the covenant demands.* *See also* [JER 32:38–32:40](https://ref.ly/Jer32:38-Jer32:40); [EZK 11:19–11:20](https://ref.ly/Ezek11:19-Ezek11:20); [2CO 3:3](https://ref.ly/2Cor3:3); [HEB 8:9–8:10](https://ref.ly/Heb8:9-Heb8:10), [HEB 9:14](https://ref.ly/Heb9:14), [HEB 10:16](https://ref.ly/Heb10:16)

### A new knowledge of God

**[HEB 8:11](https://ref.ly/Heb8:11)** *See also* [JER 31:34](https://ref.ly/Jer31:34); [2CO 3:15–3:16](https://ref.ly/2Cor3:15-2Cor3:16)

### A renewed relationship with God

**[EZK 37:26–37:27](https://ref.ly/Ezek37:26-Ezek37:27)** *“peace” refers to spiritual and material well\-being; real peace is possible only for those in a right relationship with God. The formula “I will be their God, and they will be my people” is associated also with the Abrahamic and especially the Sinaitic covenants.* *See also* [JER 24:7](https://ref.ly/Jer24:7), [JER 31:1](https://ref.ly/Jer31:1); [EZK 34:30–34:31](https://ref.ly/Ezek34:30-Ezek34:31); [HOS 2:19–2:23](https://ref.ly/Hos2:19-Hos2:23)

### A superior priesthood

**[HEB 8:6](https://ref.ly/Heb8:6)** *See also* [HEB 7:22](https://ref.ly/Heb7:22), [HEB 9:24–9:25](https://ref.ly/Heb9:24-Heb9:25)

### A superior sacrifice

**[HEB 9:14](https://ref.ly/Heb9:14)** *See also* [HEB 9:20–9:23](https://ref.ly/Heb9:20-Heb9:23), [HEB 9:26–9:28](https://ref.ly/Heb9:26-Heb9:28), [HEB 10:4](https://ref.ly/Heb10:4), [HEB 10:8–10:14](https://ref.ly/Heb10:8-Heb10:14)

### A lasting covenant

**[ISA 61:8](https://ref.ly/Isa61:8)**; **[2CO 3:11](https://ref.ly/2Cor3:11)** *See also* [JER 50:5](https://ref.ly/Jer50:5); [HEB 8:7](https://ref.ly/Heb8:7), [HEB 8:13](https://ref.ly/Heb8:13), [HEB 13:20](https://ref.ly/Heb13:20)

## 1355: providence (id: 1355)

The continuing and often unseen activity of God in sustaining his universe, providing for the needs of every creature, and preparing for the completion of his eternal purposes.

God's general providence
------------------------

### God sustains the created order

**[GEN 8:22](https://ref.ly/Gen8:22)** *A promise given by God to all peoples.* *See also* [NEH 9:6](https://ref.ly/Neh9:6); [ISA 40:26](https://ref.ly/Isa40:26); [COL 1:17](https://ref.ly/Col1:17); [HEB 1:3](https://ref.ly/Heb1:3)

### All life is dependent on God

**[1TI 6:13](https://ref.ly/1Tim6:13)** *See also* [1SA 1:27](https://ref.ly/1Sam1:27); [JOB 1:21](https://ref.ly/Job1:21); [PSA 127:3](https://ref.ly/Ps127:3); [ECC 3:2](https://ref.ly/Eccl3:2), [ECC 9:9](https://ref.ly/Eccl9:9); [EZK 24:16](https://ref.ly/Ezek24:16); [DAN 5:26](https://ref.ly/Dan5:26); [MAT 4:4](https://ref.ly/Matt4:4), [MAT 10:29](https://ref.ly/Matt10:29)

### God controls the elements

**[PSA 147:8](https://ref.ly/Ps147:8)** *See also* [JOB 37:1–37:13](https://ref.ly/Job37:1-Job37:13); [PSA 29:3–29:9](https://ref.ly/Ps29:3-Ps29:9), [PSA 135:6–135:7](https://ref.ly/Ps135:6-Ps135:7); [MAT 5:45](https://ref.ly/Matt5:45); [ACT 17:25–17:28](https://ref.ly/Acts17:25-Acts17:28)

### God provides for the created world

**[PSA 145:15–145:16](https://ref.ly/Ps145:15-Ps145:16)** *See also* [JOB 38:39–38:41](https://ref.ly/Job38:39-Job38:41); [PSA 104:27–104:28](https://ref.ly/Ps104:27-Ps104:28), [PSA 136:25](https://ref.ly/Ps136:25), [PSA 147:9](https://ref.ly/Ps147:9); [LUK 12:6–12:7](https://ref.ly/Luke12:6-Luke12:7); [ACT 14:17](https://ref.ly/Acts14:17); [1TI 6:17](https://ref.ly/1Tim6:17)

God's providence through miraculous means
-----------------------------------------

**[JOB 5:9–5:10](https://ref.ly/Job5:9-Job5:10)** *God's regular activity in providing for human beings is regarded as being miraculous in just the same way as special demonstrations of his power.* *See also* [EXO 16:11–16:14](https://ref.ly/Exod16:11-Exod16:14); [NUM 16:28–16:35](https://ref.ly/Num16:28-Num16:35); [JDG 15:18–15:19](https://ref.ly/Judg15:18-Judg15:19); [1KI 17:5–17:6](https://ref.ly/1Kgs17:5-1Kgs17:6); [2KI 4:42–4:44](https://ref.ly/2Kgs4:42-2Kgs4:44)

---------------------------------

### God's control of human intentions

**[HAB 1:12](https://ref.ly/Hab1:12)** *See also* [1KI 22:19–22:20](https://ref.ly/1Kgs22:19-1Kgs22:20); [2KI 19:27–19:28](https://ref.ly/2Kgs19:27-2Kgs19:28) parallel [ISA 37:28–37:29](https://ref.ly/Isa37:28-Isa37:29); [ISA 10:15](https://ref.ly/Isa10:15); [HAB 1:6](https://ref.ly/Hab1:6)

**[ROM 8:28](https://ref.ly/Rom8:28)** *See also* [JOB 1:12](https://ref.ly/Job1:12), [JOB 2:6](https://ref.ly/Job2:6); [PSA 107:12–107:14](https://ref.ly/Ps107:12-Ps107:14), [PSA 107:24–107:29](https://ref.ly/Ps107:24-Ps107:29), [PSA 107:33–107:38](https://ref.ly/Ps107:33-Ps107:38); [ISA 38:17](https://ref.ly/Isa38:17)

### God's saving purposes fulfilled through providence

**[GEN 50:20](https://ref.ly/Gen50:20)** *See also* [GEN 22:13](https://ref.ly/Gen22:13), [GEN 45:5–45:8](https://ref.ly/Gen45:5-Gen45:8); [2CH 36:22–36:23](https://ref.ly/2Chr36:22-2Chr36:23) parallel [EZR 1:1–1:3](https://ref.ly/Ezra1:1-Ezra1:3); [EZR 6:14](https://ref.ly/Ezra6:14); [ISA 44:28–45:1](https://ref.ly/Isa44:28-Isa45:1); [ACT 2:23](https://ref.ly/Acts2:23), [ACT 4:27–4:28](https://ref.ly/Acts4:27-Acts4:28); [GAL 4:4–4:5](https://ref.ly/Gal4:4-Gal4:5)

## 1403: God, revelation of (id: 1403)

God graciously makes himself known to humanity since people cannot discover him on their own. He achieves this in many ways, but supremely through his Son Jesus Christ.

The necessity of revelation
---------------------------

### God is hidden from human view because of sin

**[ISA 59:2](https://ref.ly/Isa59:2)** *See also* [DEU 31:18](https://ref.ly/Deut31:18); [ISA 1:15](https://ref.ly/Isa1:15), [ISA 45:15](https://ref.ly/Isa45:15), [ISA 64:7](https://ref.ly/Isa64:7); [EZK 39:23](https://ref.ly/Ezek39:23); [MIC 3:4](https://ref.ly/Mic3:4)

### People are ignorant of God

**[ACT 17:23](https://ref.ly/Acts17:23)** *See also* [EXO 5:2](https://ref.ly/Exod5:2); [JDG 2:10](https://ref.ly/Judg2:10); [JER 4:22](https://ref.ly/Jer4:22); [JHN 4:22](https://ref.ly/John4:22), [JHN 15:21](https://ref.ly/John15:21); [GAL 4:8](https://ref.ly/Gal4:8); [EPH 4:18](https://ref.ly/Eph4:18); [1TH 4:5](https://ref.ly/1Thess4:5)

### People cannot know God unaided

**[MAT 11:25–11:27](https://ref.ly/Matt11:25-Matt11:27)** parallel [LUK 10:21–10:22](https://ref.ly/Luke10:21-Luke10:22) *See also* [JOB 34:29](https://ref.ly/Job34:29); [1CO 1:21](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:21)

The means by which God reveals himself
--------------------------------------

### In the Scriptures

**[PSA 119:105](https://ref.ly/Ps119:105)** *See also* [PSA 19:7–19:10](https://ref.ly/Ps19:7-Ps19:10), [PSA 119:130](https://ref.ly/Ps119:130), [PSA 147:19](https://ref.ly/Ps147:19); [PRO 6:23](https://ref.ly/Prov6:23); [2TI 3:16](https://ref.ly/2Tim3:16); [2PE 1:19–1:21](https://ref.ly/2Pet1:19-2Pet1:21)

### By the Holy Spirit

**[EPH 1:17](https://ref.ly/Eph1:17)** *See also* [NEH 9:20](https://ref.ly/Neh9:20); [LUK 2:26](https://ref.ly/Luke2:26), [LUK 12:12](https://ref.ly/Luke12:12); [JHN 14:26](https://ref.ly/John14:26); [1CO 2:10](https://ref.ly/1Cor2:10), [1CO 2:12](https://ref.ly/1Cor2:12); [1JN 2:27](https://ref.ly/1John2:27)

### Supremely in Jesus Christ

## 1409: dream (id: 1409)

A series of images or thoughts experienced in one's mind while asleep. A means by which a divine message may be conveyed while the recipient sleeps. God may communicate directly in the dream, or interpretation may be necessary.

Direct communication through dreams
-----------------------------------

**[GEN 31:24](https://ref.ly/Gen31:24)** *See also* [GEN 20:3](https://ref.ly/Gen20:3), [GEN 20:6](https://ref.ly/Gen20:6); [1SA 28:6](https://ref.ly/1Sam28:6), [1SA 28:15](https://ref.ly/1Sam28:15); [1KI 3:5](https://ref.ly/1Kgs3:5), [1KI 3:15](https://ref.ly/1Kgs3:15); [JOB 33:14–33:15](https://ref.ly/Job33:14-Job33:15); [MAT 1:20](https://ref.ly/Matt1:20), [MAT 2:12–2:13](https://ref.ly/Matt2:12-Matt2:13), [MAT 2:19–2:20](https://ref.ly/Matt2:19-Matt2:20), [MAT 2:22](https://ref.ly/Matt2:22)

Dreams involving unusual images
-------------------------------

[GEN 28:12–28:15](https://ref.ly/Gen28:12-Gen28:15), [GEN 31:10–31:13](https://ref.ly/Gen31:10-Gen31:13), [GEN 37:5–37:7](https://ref.ly/Gen37:5-Gen37:7), [GEN 37:9](https://ref.ly/Gen37:9), [GEN 40:9–40:11](https://ref.ly/Gen40:9-Gen40:11), [GEN 40:16–40:17](https://ref.ly/Gen40:16-Gen40:17), [GEN 41:1–41:7](https://ref.ly/Gen41:1-Gen41:7); ; [JDG 7:13](https://ref.ly/Judg7:13); ; [DAN 2:31–2:35](https://ref.ly/Dan2:31-Dan2:35), [DAN 4:10–4:17](https://ref.ly/Dan4:10-Dan4:17)

--------------------------------------------------

## 1412: foreknowledge (id: 1412)

Foreknowledge is an aspect of God's knowledge of everything, and thus nothing can surprise him. Jesus Christ had foreknowledge of his own death, resurrection and coming in glory.

God's foreknowledge
-------------------

### Everything is within God's knowledge

**[ISA 42:9](https://ref.ly/Isa42:9)** *See also* [1KI 22:14](https://ref.ly/1Kgs22:14); [DAN 2:28](https://ref.ly/Dan2:28); [MAT 24:36](https://ref.ly/Matt24:36) parallel [MRK 13:32](https://ref.ly/Mark13:32)

### What God knows he ordains

**[ISA 46:10–46:11](https://ref.ly/Isa46:10-Isa46:11)** *See also* [ACT 2:23](https://ref.ly/Acts2:23); [ROM 8:28–8:30](https://ref.ly/Rom8:28-Rom8:30); [1PE 1:1–1:2](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:1-1Pet1:2)

### God's foreknowledge of the Messiah

**[ACT 3:18](https://ref.ly/Acts3:18)** *See also* [ISA 11:1–11:3](https://ref.ly/Isa11:1-Isa11:3), [ISA 53:7–53:9](https://ref.ly/Isa53:7-Isa53:9); [MIC 5:2](https://ref.ly/Mic5:2); [ACT 2:22–2:23](https://ref.ly/Acts2:22-Acts2:23), [ACT 4:27–4:28](https://ref.ly/Acts4:27-Acts4:28); [1PE 1:20](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:20)

--------------------------------------------------

**[HEB 2:3](https://ref.ly/Heb2:3)** *See also* [JHN 3:18](https://ref.ly/John3:18), [JHN 3:36](https://ref.ly/John3:36); [1CO 15:2](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:2); [2CO 6:1–6:2](https://ref.ly/2Cor6:1-2Cor6:2); [EPH 5:5–5:6](https://ref.ly/Eph5:5-Eph5:6); [HEB 3:12](https://ref.ly/Heb3:12), [HEB 6:4–6:6](https://ref.ly/Heb6:4-Heb6:6); [2PE 2:1](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:1); [HEB 3:15](https://ref.ly/Heb3:15); [PSA 95:7–95:8](https://ref.ly/Ps95:7-Ps95:8)

## 1415: miracles (id: 1415)

Events that are totally out of the ordinary and that cannot be adequately explained on the basis of natural occurrences, such as those associated with the ministry of Jesus Christ. They are seen as evidence of the presence and power of God in the world or as demonstrating authority on the part of one of his servants.

* **Associated Articles:** 1416: miracles, nature of (ID: `1416@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1417: miracles, of Jesus Christ (ID: `1417@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1418: miracles, responses to (ID: `1418@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 1416: miracles, nature of (id: 1416)

Miracles may be performed directly by God or through a human agent. Those recorded in Scripture include healing, raising the dead, miracles of nature and the casting out of demons.

Miracles demonstrate God's greatness and power
----------------------------------------------

**[PSA 77:14](https://ref.ly/Ps77:14)** *See also* [EXO 14:30–14:31](https://ref.ly/Exod14:30-Exod14:31), [EXO 34:10](https://ref.ly/Exod34:10); [DEU 3:24](https://ref.ly/Deut3:24); [1KI 18:37–18:39](https://ref.ly/1Kgs18:37-1Kgs18:39); [JOB 5:9](https://ref.ly/Job5:9); [PSA 78:4](https://ref.ly/Ps78:4); [LUK 9:42–9:43](https://ref.ly/Luke9:42-Luke9:43)

## 1418: miracles, responses to (id: 1418)

Miracles often depend upon faith on the part of those who will benefit from them. Human responses to miracles take various forms. Some respond in faith and obedience, whilst others are confirmed in their unbelief and rebellion.

Faith and obedience required in the working of miracles
-------------------------------------------------------

**[1KI 17:13–17:15](https://ref.ly/1Kgs17:13-1Kgs17:15)** *The widow gave Elijah her last meal before she could be miraculously provided for.* *See also* [EXO 14:16](https://ref.ly/Exod14:16), [EXO 14:21](https://ref.ly/Exod14:21); [NUM 21:8–21:9](https://ref.ly/Num21:8-Num21:9); [JOS 3:13–3:17](https://ref.ly/Josh3:13-Josh3:17); [1KI 17:5](https://ref.ly/1Kgs17:5); [2KI 4:41](https://ref.ly/2Kgs4:41), [2KI 5:10–5:14](https://ref.ly/2Kgs5:10-2Kgs5:14); [MAT 9:6–9:7](https://ref.ly/Matt9:6-Matt9:7) parallels [MRK 2:10–2:12](https://ref.ly/Mark2:10-Mark2:12), [LUK 5:24–5:25](https://ref.ly/Luke5:24-Luke5:25); [MAT 9:22](https://ref.ly/Matt9:22) parallels [MRK 5:34](https://ref.ly/Mark5:34), [LUK 8:48](https://ref.ly/Luke8:48); [LUK 1:38](https://ref.ly/Luke1:38); [HEB 11:29–11:30](https://ref.ly/Heb11:29-Heb11:30)

Miracles limited by lack of faith
---------------------------------

**[MAT 13:58](https://ref.ly/Matt13:58)** parallel [MRK 6:5–6:6](https://ref.ly/Mark6:5-Mark6:6) *See also* [2KI 4:3–4:6](https://ref.ly/2Kgs4:3-2Kgs4:6) *The number of jars limited the miraculous supply of oil*; [MAT 14:28–14:31](https://ref.ly/Matt14:28-Matt14:31), [MAT 17:14–17:20](https://ref.ly/Matt17:14-Matt17:20)

### Hardness of heart

## 1421: oracles (id: 1421)

Divine utterances or messages spoken through human lips. Especially noteworthy are the oracles of Balaam. Several other prophecies are also referred to as oracles.

The oracles of Balaam
---------------------

### Divine inspiration is irresistible

**[NUM 22:38](https://ref.ly/Num22:38)** *See also* [NUM 22:18–22:19](https://ref.ly/Num22:18-Num22:19), [NUM 23:11–23:12](https://ref.ly/Num23:11-Num23:12), [NUM 23:25–23:26](https://ref.ly/Num23:25-Num23:26), [NUM 24:12–24:13](https://ref.ly/Num24:12-Num24:13)

### Balaam's oracles

**[NUM 23:6–23:10](https://ref.ly/Num23:6-Num23:10)** *See also* [NUM 23:18–23:24](https://ref.ly/Num23:18-Num23:24), [NUM 24:2–24:9](https://ref.ly/Num24:2-Num24:9), [NUM 24:15–24:19](https://ref.ly/Num24:15-Num24:19), [NUM 24:20–24:24](https://ref.ly/Num24:20-Num24:24)

## 1424: predictions (id: 1424)

Speaking authoritatively of the future. Since God knows the future he is able to reveal it to people beforehand. Predictions, which are often but not necessarily contained in prophecies, should not be confused with promises or expressions of intention.

God's knowledge of the future
-----------------------------

**[GEN 41:15–41:16](https://ref.ly/Gen41:15-Gen41:16), [GEN 41:28](https://ref.ly/Gen41:28)** *See also* [GEN 18:17](https://ref.ly/Gen18:17); [NUM 24:2–24:4](https://ref.ly/Num24:2-Num24:4); [ISA 44:24–44:26](https://ref.ly/Isa44:24-Isa44:26)

Impossible to predict the future apart from God
-----------------------------------------------

**[ECC 8:7](https://ref.ly/Eccl8:7)** *See also* [ECC 7:14](https://ref.ly/Eccl7:14); [ISA 41:22–41:24](https://ref.ly/Isa41:22-Isa41:24)

---------------------------------

[MAT 24:1–24:2](https://ref.ly/Matt24:1-Matt24:2) parallels [MRK 13:1–13:2](https://ref.ly/Mark13:1-Mark13:2), [LUK 21:5–21:6](https://ref.ly/Luke21:5-Luke21:6); ; [MAT 24:15–24:25](https://ref.ly/Matt24:15-Matt24:25) parallels [MRK 13:14–13:23](https://ref.ly/Mark13:14-Mark13:23), [LUK 21:20–21:24](https://ref.ly/Luke21:20-Luke21:24)

## 1427: prophecy (id: 1427)

The disclosing of the will and purposes of God through inspired or Spirit\-filled human beings. The OT emphasises the importance of prophecy as a means of knowing God. Many OT prophecies find their fulfilment in Jesus Christ. The NT sets out the place of prophecy in the life of the church and gives guidance concerning the use of this gift.

* **Associated Articles:** 1428: prophecy, inspiration of OT (ID: `1428@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1429: prophecy, fulfilment of OT (ID: `1429@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1430: prophecy, concerning Jesus Christ (ID: `1430@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1431: prophecy, methods of OT (ID: `1431@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1432: prophecy, in NT (ID: `1432@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 1428: prophecy, inspiration of OT (id: 1428)

The prophecies of biblical messengers are acknowledged as being of divine origin, inspired through the activity of the Holy Spirit.

God speaks through his prophets
-------------------------------

**[2PE 1:20–1:21](https://ref.ly/2Pet1:20-2Pet1:21)** *See also* [NEH 9:30](https://ref.ly/Neh9:30); [ZEC 7:12](https://ref.ly/Zech7:12); [HEB 1:1](https://ref.ly/Heb1:1)

God is the source of prophecy
-----------------------------

**[EZK 24:20–24:21](https://ref.ly/Ezek24:20-Ezek24:21)** *The phrase “the word of the LORD came to ...” is frequently used of (and by) the prophets to indicate that the message they proclaimed came directly from God.* *See also* [1SA 15:10](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:10); [2SA 7:4](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:4); [1KI 13:20](https://ref.ly/1Kgs13:20), [1KI 16:1](https://ref.ly/1Kgs16:1), [1KI 17:2](https://ref.ly/1Kgs17:2); [2KI 20:4](https://ref.ly/2Kgs20:4); [JER 1:2](https://ref.ly/Jer1:2); [EZK 6:1](https://ref.ly/Ezek6:1); [JON 1:1](https://ref.ly/Jonah1:1); [HAG 2:10](https://ref.ly/Hag2:10); [ZEC 1:1](https://ref.ly/Zech1:1)

Prophets inspired by God speak the truth
----------------------------------------

**[DEU 18:22](https://ref.ly/Deut18:22)** *See also* [JER 28:9](https://ref.ly/Jer28:9)

* **Associated Passages:** 2 Peter 1:20-21; Nehemiah 9:30; Zechariah 7:12; Hebrews 1:1; Ezekiel 24:20-21; 1 Samuel 15:10; 2 Samuel 7:4; 1 Kings 13:20; 1 Kings 16:1; 1 Kings 17:2; 2 Kings 20:4; Jeremiah 1:2; Ezekiel 6:1; Jonah 1:1; Haggai 2:10; Zechariah 1:1; Deuteronomy 18:22; Jeremiah 28:9
* **Associated Articles:** 1150: God, truth of (ID: `1150@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1443: revelation, in OT (ID: `1443@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1610: Scripture (ID: `1610@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1690: word of God (ID: `1690@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 3272: Holy Spirit, in OT (ID: `3272@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 3281: Holy Spirit, inspiration of (ID: `3281@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 4155: divination (ID: `4155@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7772: prophets (ID: `7772@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 7781: seer (ID: `7781@DictionaryBibleThemes`)

All divinely inspired prophecy achieves its purpose. Scripture records the fulfilment of many prophecies.

## 1431: prophecy, methods of OT (id: 1431)

Prophets relayed their messages from God in a variety of ways, choosing methods that would make the meaning clear, attract attention or convince the people of the truth of their words.

God speaks through the prophets
-------------------------------

**[HEB 1:1](https://ref.ly/Heb1:1)**

### Prophecy directly proclaimed

**[JON 3:1–3:4](https://ref.ly/Jonah3:1-Jonah3:4)** *See also* [1KI 13:1–13:3](https://ref.ly/1Kgs13:1-1Kgs13:3), [1KI 14:6–14:16](https://ref.ly/1Kgs14:6-1Kgs14:16), [1KI 20:22](https://ref.ly/1Kgs20:22); [ISA 7:13–7:17](https://ref.ly/Isa7:13-Isa7:17); [JER 26:18](https://ref.ly/Jer26:18); [ACT 11:27–11:28](https://ref.ly/Acts11:27-Acts11:28); [1CO 14:29](https://ref.ly/1Cor14:29)

### Messages presented as coming from God

**[2KI 7:1](https://ref.ly/2Kgs7:1)** *Prophets often used the phrases “hear the word of the LORD” and “says the LORD” to ensure that their audience understood the divine origin of their proclamation.* *See also* [2KI 20:16–20:18](https://ref.ly/2Kgs20:16-2Kgs20:18); [JER 7:2](https://ref.ly/Jer7:2), [JER 30:3](https://ref.ly/Jer30:3), [JER 44:26](https://ref.ly/Jer44:26); [EZK 34:7–34:10](https://ref.ly/Ezek34:7-Ezek34:10); [HOS 4:1](https://ref.ly/Hos4:1); [AMO 1:5](https://ref.ly/Amos1:5), [AMO 7:16–7:17](https://ref.ly/Amos7:16-Amos7:17); [ZEP 3:20](https://ref.ly/Zeph3:20); [HAG 2:9](https://ref.ly/Hag2:9); [ZEC 1:3](https://ref.ly/Zech1:3); [MAL 1:6](https://ref.ly/Mal1:6)

Prophecy enacted
----------------

**[1KI 11:29–11:39](https://ref.ly/1Kgs11:29-1Kgs11:39)** *See also* [1KI 22:11](https://ref.ly/1Kgs22:11); [JER 19:1–19:13](https://ref.ly/Jer19:1-Jer19:13), [JER 27:1–27:7](https://ref.ly/Jer27:1-Jer27:7), [JER 28:10–28:11](https://ref.ly/Jer28:10-Jer28:11), [JER 43:8–43:13](https://ref.ly/Jer43:8-Jer43:13); [EZK 4:1–4:17](https://ref.ly/Ezek4:1-Ezek4:17), [EZK 5:1–5:3](https://ref.ly/Ezek5:1-Ezek5:3), [EZK 12:3–12:11](https://ref.ly/Ezek12:3-Ezek12:11); [ZEC 6:9–6:15](https://ref.ly/Zech6:9-Zech6:15); [ACT 21:10–21:11](https://ref.ly/Acts21:10-Acts21:11)

--------------------------------------------

## 1432: prophecy, in NT (id: 1432)

The NT describes the prophetic aspect of the ministry of Jesus Christ, and also recognises that prophetic gifts are given to believers through the Holy Spirit. It provides guidance on how such prophetic gifts are to be used.

Jesus Christ recognised as a prophet
------------------------------------

[MAT 21:11](https://ref.ly/Matt21:11); ; [MRK 6:4](https://ref.ly/Mark6:4), [MRK 8:27–8:28](https://ref.ly/Mark8:27-Mark8:28); ; [LUK 7:16](https://ref.ly/Luke7:16), [LUK 24:17–24:19](https://ref.ly/Luke24:17-Luke24:19); ; [JHN 4:19](https://ref.ly/John4:19)

Prophecy in the church
----------------------

### Prophecy is one among many spiritual gifts

**[1CO 12:28–12:29](https://ref.ly/1Cor12:28-1Cor12:29)** *See also* [ROM 12:6](https://ref.ly/Rom12:6); [1CO 12:10](https://ref.ly/1Cor12:10); [EPH 4:11](https://ref.ly/Eph4:11)

### Not all are called to be prophets

[1CO 12:29](https://ref.ly/1Cor12:29); ; [EPH 4:11](https://ref.ly/Eph4:11)

### Prophecy is valueless without love

**[1CO 13:1–13:2](https://ref.ly/1Cor13:1-1Cor13:2)**

### Prophecy is for the building up of the church

**[1CO 14:26](https://ref.ly/1Cor14:26)** *See also* [ROM 12:3–12:6](https://ref.ly/Rom12:3-Rom12:6); [1CO 14:3–14:5](https://ref.ly/1Cor14:3-1Cor14:5); [1PE 4:10](https://ref.ly/1Pet4:10)

### Prophecy superior to speaking in tongues

**[1CO 14:5](https://ref.ly/1Cor14:5)**

----------------------------

*See also* [ACT 2:17](https://ref.ly/Acts2:17), [ACT 11:27–11:28](https://ref.ly/Acts11:27-Acts11:28), [ACT 15:32](https://ref.ly/Acts15:32), [ACT 21:9](https://ref.ly/Acts21:9)

## 1436: reality (id: 1436)

Scripture provides an accurate and reliable guide to the realities of the spiritual and material worlds. It affirms the reality of human sin, of the power and purpose of God to deal with sin through Jesus Christ and of the guidance of the Holy Spirit.

The reality of God
------------------

### The reality of the existence of God

**[JOB 42:4–42:5](https://ref.ly/Job42:4-Job42:5)** *See also* [2SA 7:22–7:23](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:22-2Sam7:23); [1KI 8:23](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:23); [JER 10:10](https://ref.ly/Jer10:10)

### The reality of the love of God

**[1JN 4:7–4:9](https://ref.ly/1John4:7-1John4:9)** *See also* [JHN 3:16](https://ref.ly/John3:16); [ROM 5:8](https://ref.ly/Rom5:8); [GAL 2:20–2:21](https://ref.ly/Gal2:20-Gal2:21)

### The reality of God's salvation

**[PSA 68:20](https://ref.ly/Ps68:20)** *See also* [PSA 65:5](https://ref.ly/Ps65:5), [PSA 79:9](https://ref.ly/Ps79:9); [MIC 7:7](https://ref.ly/Mic7:7); [LUK 1:47](https://ref.ly/Luke1:47); [TIT 2:11](https://ref.ly/Titus2:11)

### The reality of the revelation of God

[PSA 19:1–19:4](https://ref.ly/Ps19:1-Ps19:4); ; [JHN 1:1–1:9](https://ref.ly/John1:1-John1:9); ; [ACT 14:15–14:17](https://ref.ly/Acts14:15-Acts14:17); ; [ROM 1:18–1:20](https://ref.ly/Rom1:18-Rom1:20)

## 1439: revelation (id: 1439)

The making known of God's person, nature and deeds, in Scripture, history and supremely the person of Jesus Christ. God is also made known, to a limited yet important extent, through his creation.

* **Associated Articles:** 1440: revelation, through creation (ID: `1440@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1441: revelation, necessity of (ID: `1441@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1442: revelation, of God (ID: `1442@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1443: revelation, in OT (ID: `1443@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1444: revelation, in NT (ID: `1444@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1445: revelation, responses to (ID: `1445@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 1440: revelation, through creation (id: 1440)

The creation bears witness to the wisdom and power of its creator. This natural knowledge of God is limited in its extent, but is sufficient to convince human beings of the existence of God and the need to respond to him.

The creation bears witness to its creator
-----------------------------------------

**[PSA 19:1–19:6](https://ref.ly/Ps19:1-Ps19:6)** *See also* [JOB 36:22–37:18](https://ref.ly/Job36:22-Job37:18); [AMO 4:13](https://ref.ly/Amos4:13); [ACT 14:15–14:17](https://ref.ly/Acts14:15-Acts14:17)

All human beings have a natural awareness of God
------------------------------------------------

**[ROM 2:14–2:15](https://ref.ly/Rom2:14-Rom2:15)** *See also* [ACT 17:22–17:31](https://ref.ly/Acts17:22-Acts17:31)

The limitations of a natural knowledge of God
---------------------------------------------

**[ROM 1:18–1:21](https://ref.ly/Rom1:18-Rom1:21)** *See also* [ROM 1:32](https://ref.ly/Rom1:32); [1CO 1:20–1:21](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:20-1Cor1:21)

* **Associated Passages:** Psalms 19:1-6; Job 36:22-37:18; Amos 4:13; Acts 14:15-17; Romans 2:14-15; Acts 17:22-31; Romans 1:18-21; Romans 1:32; 1 Corinthians 1:20-21
* **Associated Articles:** 1045: God, glory of (ID: `1045@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1325: God, the Creator (ID: `1325@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1403: God, revelation of (ID: `1403@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5008: conscience (ID: `5008@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5548: speech, divine (ID: `5548@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 6183: ignorance, of God (ID: `6183@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 8135: knowing God, nature of (ID: `8135@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 1441: revelation, necessity of (id: 1441)

Finiteness and sin make it impossible to gain adequate knowledge of God through human effort alone. God in mercy makes himself known through the incarnation of the Son and the illumination of human minds to understand him.

The impossibility of fully knowing God without revelation
---------------------------------------------------------

### God is beyond unaided human knowing

**[JHN 1:18](https://ref.ly/John1:18)** *See also* [EXO 33:20](https://ref.ly/Exod33:20); [ISA 55:8–55:9](https://ref.ly/Isa55:8-Isa55:9); [JHN 6:46](https://ref.ly/John6:46); [1JN 4:12](https://ref.ly/1John4:12)

### The human mind is limited

**[JOB 11:7](https://ref.ly/Job11:7)** *See also* [JOB 9:4](https://ref.ly/Job9:4), [JOB 9:10](https://ref.ly/Job9:10), [JOB 23:3–23:9](https://ref.ly/Job23:3-Job23:9), [JOB 26:14](https://ref.ly/Job26:14), [JOB 36:26](https://ref.ly/Job36:26), [JOB 37:5](https://ref.ly/Job37:5), [JOB 37:23](https://ref.ly/Job37:23); [PSA 139:6](https://ref.ly/Ps139:6), [PSA 145:3](https://ref.ly/Ps145:3); [ECC 3:11](https://ref.ly/Eccl3:11); [ISA 40:13–40:14](https://ref.ly/Isa40:13-Isa40:14), [ISA 40:28](https://ref.ly/Isa40:28); [ROM 11:33](https://ref.ly/Rom11:33)

### The human mind cannot discern God of its own accord

**[2CO 4:4](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:4)** *See also* [JHN 1:5](https://ref.ly/John1:5); [ROM 1:18–1:32](https://ref.ly/Rom1:18-Rom1:32); [1CO 1:21](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:21), [1CO 2:14](https://ref.ly/1Cor2:14); [2CO 3:14](https://ref.ly/2Cor3:14); [EPH 4:17–4:18](https://ref.ly/Eph4:17-Eph4:18)

God is known fully only through Jesus Christ
--------------------------------------------

**[HEB 1:1–1:2](https://ref.ly/Heb1:1-Heb1:2)**; **[1JN 5:20](https://ref.ly/1John5:20)** *See also* [JHN 1:14–1:18](https://ref.ly/John1:14-John1:18), [JHN 17:3](https://ref.ly/John17:3); [COL 1:15–1:20](https://ref.ly/Col1:15-Col1:20)

## 1443: revelation, in OT (id: 1443)

The OT bears witness to God's revelation in the history of Israel and in the inspired testimony of the prophets and other writers of the period. This knowledge of God prepares the way for the full disclosure of God in Jesus Christ in the NT.

Revelation in Eden and before the flood
---------------------------------------

**[GEN 1:3](https://ref.ly/Gen1:3), [GEN 2:16–2:18](https://ref.ly/Gen2:16-Gen2:18)** *See also* [GEN 1:29–1:30](https://ref.ly/Gen1:29-Gen1:30), [GEN 3:9–3:19](https://ref.ly/Gen3:9-Gen3:19), [GEN 4:6–4:7](https://ref.ly/Gen4:6-Gen4:7), [GEN 4:9–4:15](https://ref.ly/Gen4:9-Gen4:15), [GEN 6:13–6:22](https://ref.ly/Gen6:13-Gen6:22)

The covenant framework of OT revelation after the flood
-------------------------------------------------------

### God's covenant with Noah

**[GEN 9:8–9:11](https://ref.ly/Gen9:8-Gen9:11)** *This covenant covers all living creatures.* *See also* [GEN 6:18](https://ref.ly/Gen6:18), [GEN 9:12–9:17](https://ref.ly/Gen9:12-Gen9:17)

### God's covenant with Abraham

**[GEN 17:7](https://ref.ly/Gen17:7)** *See also* [GEN 15:9–15:21](https://ref.ly/Gen15:9-Gen15:21), [GEN 17:2](https://ref.ly/Gen17:2), [GEN 17:4](https://ref.ly/Gen17:4), [GEN 17:10–17:14](https://ref.ly/Gen17:10-Gen17:14), [GEN 22:16–22:18](https://ref.ly/Gen22:16-Gen22:18); [EXO 6:2–6:6](https://ref.ly/Exod6:2-Exod6:6); [1CH 16:14–16:18](https://ref.ly/1Chr16:14-1Chr16:18); [PSA 105:8–105:9](https://ref.ly/Ps105:8-Ps105:9)

### God's covenant with Moses at Sinai

**[EXO 34:27](https://ref.ly/Exod34:27)** *See also* [EXO 24:3–24:8](https://ref.ly/Exod24:3-Exod24:8), [EXO 34:10–34:14](https://ref.ly/Exod34:10-Exod34:14); [DEU 5:2–5:4](https://ref.ly/Deut5:2-Deut5:4) *Mount Sinai was also known as Mount Horeb*; [JER 11:2–11:5](https://ref.ly/Jer11:2-Jer11:5)

### God's covenant with David

**[PSA 89:3–89:4](https://ref.ly/Ps89:3-Ps89:4)** *See also* [2SA 7:8–7:16](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:8-2Sam7:16); [PSA 132:11–132:12](https://ref.ly/Ps132:11-Ps132:12)

### The promise of a new covenant

**[JER 31:31–31:34](https://ref.ly/Jer31:31-Jer31:34)** *See also* [ISA 42:6](https://ref.ly/Isa42:6); [MAT 26:27–26:28](https://ref.ly/Matt26:27-Matt26:28) parallels [MRK 14:24](https://ref.ly/Mark14:24), [LUK 22:20](https://ref.ly/Luke22:20), [1CO 11:25](https://ref.ly/1Cor11:25); [HEB 8:8–8:12](https://ref.ly/Heb8:8-Heb8:12), [HEB 9:15](https://ref.ly/Heb9:15), [HEB 10:15–10:18](https://ref.ly/Heb10:15-Heb10:18)

The recipients of OT revelation
-------------------------------

### The people of Israel

**[AMO 3:2](https://ref.ly/Amos3:2)** *See also* [EXO 19:3–19:6](https://ref.ly/Exod19:3-Exod19:6); [DEU 7:6](https://ref.ly/Deut7:6); [ISA 65:1](https://ref.ly/Isa65:1); [EZK 20:5](https://ref.ly/Ezek20:5)

### On occasions God spoke to people outside the covenant community

**[DAN 2:27–2:28](https://ref.ly/Dan2:27-Dan2:28)** *See also* [GEN 41:25](https://ref.ly/Gen41:25), [GEN 41:28–41:32](https://ref.ly/Gen41:28-Gen41:32); [DAN 4:1–4:37](https://ref.ly/Dan4:1-Dan4:37), [DAN 5:17–5:28](https://ref.ly/Dan5:17-Dan5:28)

Methods of OT revelation
------------------------

### Direct communication

**[DEU 18:18](https://ref.ly/Deut18:18)** *See also* [EXO 4:12](https://ref.ly/Exod4:12); [NUM 12:8](https://ref.ly/Num12:8), [NUM 23:5](https://ref.ly/Num23:5); [ISA 50:4](https://ref.ly/Isa50:4), [ISA 51:16](https://ref.ly/Isa51:16); [JER 1:9](https://ref.ly/Jer1:9)

### Visions and dreams

**[NUM 12:6](https://ref.ly/Num12:6)** *See also* [GEN 15:1](https://ref.ly/Gen15:1), [GEN 28:12](https://ref.ly/Gen28:12), [GEN 37:5–37:7](https://ref.ly/Gen37:5-Gen37:7), [GEN 37:9](https://ref.ly/Gen37:9), [GEN 46:2](https://ref.ly/Gen46:2); [NUM 24:4](https://ref.ly/Num24:4); [DEU 13:1](https://ref.ly/Deut13:1); [JDG 7:13–7:14](https://ref.ly/Judg7:13-Judg7:14); [JOB 33:14–33:15](https://ref.ly/Job33:14-Job33:15); [EZK 1:1](https://ref.ly/Ezek1:1), [EZK 1:26–1:28](https://ref.ly/Ezek1:26-Ezek1:28)

### Visible manifestations (theophanies)

**[GEN 18:1](https://ref.ly/Gen18:1)** *See also* [GEN 32:24–32:30](https://ref.ly/Gen32:24-Gen32:30); [EXO 3:1–3:6](https://ref.ly/Exod3:1-Exod3:6), [EXO 34:4–34:7](https://ref.ly/Exod34:4-Exod34:7); [NUM 11:25](https://ref.ly/Num11:25), [NUM 12:5](https://ref.ly/Num12:5), [NUM 14:10–14:12](https://ref.ly/Num14:10-Num14:12); [JOS 5:13–5:15](https://ref.ly/Josh5:13-Josh5:15)

### Scripture

**[DEU 31:9](https://ref.ly/Deut31:9)** *See also* [EXO 17:14](https://ref.ly/Exod17:14); [NUM 33:2](https://ref.ly/Num33:2); [ISA 30:8](https://ref.ly/Isa30:8); [JER 36:2](https://ref.ly/Jer36:2), [JER 51:60](https://ref.ly/Jer51:60)

The content of OT revelation
----------------------------

### Revelation of God's will and purposes

**[GEN 17:1–17:2](https://ref.ly/Gen17:1-Gen17:2)** *See also* [GEN 12:1–12:3](https://ref.ly/Gen12:1-Gen12:3), [GEN 15:1–15:5](https://ref.ly/Gen15:1-Gen15:5); [EXO 19:5–19:6](https://ref.ly/Exod19:5-Exod19:6), [EXO 20:1–20:17](https://ref.ly/Exod20:1-Exod20:17) parallel [DEU 5:6–5:21](https://ref.ly/Deut5:6-Deut5:21); [EXO 22:31](https://ref.ly/Exod22:31); [LEV 11:44–11:45](https://ref.ly/Lev11:44-Lev11:45), [LEV 19:1–19:2](https://ref.ly/Lev19:1-Lev19:2), [LEV 20:7–20:8](https://ref.ly/Lev20:7-Lev20:8)

### Revelation of God's plan

**[GEN 3:15](https://ref.ly/Gen3:15)** *See also* [ISA 9:6–9:7](https://ref.ly/Isa9:6-Isa9:7), [ISA 11:1–11:10](https://ref.ly/Isa11:1-Isa11:10), [ISA 42:1](https://ref.ly/Isa42:1); [MIC 5:1–5:5](https://ref.ly/Mic5:1-Mic5:5); [ZEC 9:9–9:13](https://ref.ly/Zech9:9-Zech9:13)

### Revelation of God's character and being

**[EXO 3:11–3:15](https://ref.ly/Exod3:11-Exod3:15)** [EXO 40:34](https://ref.ly/Exod40:34); ; [1KI 8:11](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:11); ; [EZK 1:28](https://ref.ly/Ezek1:28); [NUM 14:17–14:19](https://ref.ly/Num14:17-Num14:19); ; [PSA 143:1](https://ref.ly/Ps143:1); [DEU 7:7–7:8](https://ref.ly/Deut7:7-Deut7:8); ; [LAM 3:22](https://ref.ly/Lam3:22); [PSA 72:2](https://ref.ly/Ps72:2), [PSA 103:6](https://ref.ly/Ps103:6); ; [ISA 59:17](https://ref.ly/Isa59:17); [PSA 115:3](https://ref.ly/Ps115:3), [PSA 135:5–135:6](https://ref.ly/Ps135:5-Ps135:6)

-----------------------------------

## 1444: revelation, in NT (id: 1444)

The NT fulfils and completes the revelation of God which began in the OT. Jesus Christ is the central focus of this self\-revelation of God.

The unity and progress of revelation
------------------------------------

### The unity of OT and NT

**[MAT 5:17–5:18](https://ref.ly/Matt5:17-Matt5:18)** *See also* [ROM 3:21–3:22](https://ref.ly/Rom3:21-Rom3:22); [2TI 3:14–3:15](https://ref.ly/2Tim3:14-2Tim3:15); [2PE 3:15–3:16](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:15-2Pet3:16) *The writings of Paul are presented as having equal status with the OT Scriptures*; [REV 22:18–22:19](https://ref.ly/Rev22:18-Rev22:19) *These sanctions have the same force as those of [Dt 4:2](https://ref.ly/Deut4:2); [12:32](https://ref.ly/Deut12:32).*

### The progress of NT revelation

**[HEB 1:1–1:2](https://ref.ly/Heb1:1-Heb1:2)** *See also* [HEB 2:1–2:4](https://ref.ly/Heb2:1-Heb2:4), [HEB 12:22–12:27](https://ref.ly/Heb12:22-Heb12:27)

The NT fulfils and completes God's revelation of himself
--------------------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ is the supreme revelation of God

**[COL 1:25–1:27](https://ref.ly/Col1:25-Col1:27)** *See also* [JHN 1:9–1:18](https://ref.ly/John1:9-John1:18), [JHN 14:6](https://ref.ly/John14:6); [ACT 4:12](https://ref.ly/Acts4:12); [GAL 4:4](https://ref.ly/Gal4:4); [PHP 2:6–2:8](https://ref.ly/Phil2:6-Phil2:8); [HEB 2:14](https://ref.ly/Heb2:14)

### Jesus Christ is the image of God

**[2CO 4:4](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:4)**; **[COL 1:15](https://ref.ly/Col1:15)**

### Jesus Christ has the nature of God

**[PHP 2:6](https://ref.ly/Phil2:6)**

### Jesus Christ is the exact representation of God

**[HEB 1:3](https://ref.ly/Heb1:3)**

### Jesus Christ is the incarnate Word of God

**[JHN 1:14](https://ref.ly/John1:14)**

The role of the Holy Spirit in revelation
-----------------------------------------

### He is the divine agent of revelation

**[JHN 16:12–16:15](https://ref.ly/John16:12-John16:15)** *See also* [JHN 14:16–14:17](https://ref.ly/John14:16-John14:17), [JHN 15:26](https://ref.ly/John15:26); [1JN 4:6](https://ref.ly/1John4:6), [1JN 5:6](https://ref.ly/1John5:6); [REV 2:7](https://ref.ly/Rev2:7), [REV 2:11](https://ref.ly/Rev2:11), [REV 2:17](https://ref.ly/Rev2:17), [REV 2:29](https://ref.ly/Rev2:29), [REV 3:6](https://ref.ly/Rev3:6), [REV 3:13](https://ref.ly/Rev3:13), [REV 3:22](https://ref.ly/Rev3:22)

### He is the source of revelatory manifestations

**[1CO 12:7–12:11](https://ref.ly/1Cor12:7-1Cor12:11)** *See also* [ACT 2:1–2:12](https://ref.ly/Acts2:1-Acts2:12); [ROM 12:6](https://ref.ly/Rom12:6); [1CO 12:28–12:30](https://ref.ly/1Cor12:28-1Cor12:30), [1CO 13:8–13:12](https://ref.ly/1Cor13:8-1Cor13:12), [1CO 14:1–14:33](https://ref.ly/1Cor14:1-1Cor14:33); [EPH 4:11](https://ref.ly/Eph4:11)

----------------------------

## 1445: revelation, responses to (id: 1445)

God requires and imparts a frame of mind that receives and responds to what he has made known.

God commands that his word be heeded
------------------------------------

**[MRK 4:3](https://ref.ly/Mark4:3)** *See also* [ISA 1:10](https://ref.ly/Isa1:10); [MRK 4:9](https://ref.ly/Mark4:9); [REV 2:7](https://ref.ly/Rev2:7)

People do not naturally understand what God has revealed
--------------------------------------------------------

### They fail to recognise God's revelation in Jesus Christ

**[MAT 11:25–11:27](https://ref.ly/Matt11:25-Matt11:27)** parallel [LUK 10:21–10:22](https://ref.ly/Luke10:21-Luke10:22) *See also* [JHN 5:37–5:40](https://ref.ly/John5:37-John5:40), [JHN 6:44–6:45](https://ref.ly/John6:44-John6:45), [JHN 10:24–10:26](https://ref.ly/John10:24-John10:26), [JHN 12:37–12:41](https://ref.ly/John12:37-John12:41), [JHN 14:9](https://ref.ly/John14:9); [ROM 9:31–10:4](https://ref.ly/Rom9:31-Rom10:4); [1CO 1:18–1:25](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:18-1Cor1:25), [1CO 2:8](https://ref.ly/1Cor2:8); [2CO 4:4](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:4)

### They fail to understand God's revelation in general

**[1CO 2:14](https://ref.ly/1Cor2:14)** *See also* [MRK 4:11–4:12](https://ref.ly/Mark4:11-Mark4:12) parallels [MAT 13:13–13:15](https://ref.ly/Matt13:13-Matt13:15), [LUK 8:10](https://ref.ly/Luke8:10); [ISA 6:9–6:10](https://ref.ly/Isa6:9-Isa6:10); [JHN 8:43–8:47](https://ref.ly/John8:43-John8:47); [2CO 3:14–3:16](https://ref.ly/2Cor3:14-2Cor3:16); [2TH 2:11–2:13](https://ref.ly/2Thess2:11-2Thess2:13)

God has given his Spirit to illuminate the human mind
-----------------------------------------------------

### He reveals and teaches truth

**[1CO 2:12–2:13](https://ref.ly/1Cor2:12-1Cor2:13)** *See also* [JER 31:31–31:34](https://ref.ly/Jer31:31-Jer31:34); [MAT 16:17](https://ref.ly/Matt16:17); [JHN 3:3–3:10](https://ref.ly/John3:3-John3:10), [JHN 14:16–14:17](https://ref.ly/John14:16-John14:17), [JHN 14:25–14:26](https://ref.ly/John14:25-John14:26), [JHN 16:12–16:15](https://ref.ly/John16:12-John16:15); [PHP 3:15](https://ref.ly/Phil3:15)

### He reveals through prayer for understanding

**[PSA 119:18](https://ref.ly/Ps119:18)** *See also* [PSA 119:12](https://ref.ly/Ps119:12), [PSA 119:27](https://ref.ly/Ps119:27); [EPH 1:17–1:18](https://ref.ly/Eph1:17-Eph1:18)

Understanding God's revelation carries special responsibility
-------------------------------------------------------------

**[LUK 12:47–12:48](https://ref.ly/Luke12:47-Luke12:48)** *See also* [MAT 13:11–13:12](https://ref.ly/Matt13:11-Matt13:12), [MAT 25:14–25:30](https://ref.ly/Matt25:14-Matt25:30) parallel [LUK 19:12–19:27](https://ref.ly/Luke19:12-Luke19:27)

God's revelation of himself will only be fully understood at the second coming of Jesus Christ
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**[1CO 13:12](https://ref.ly/1Cor13:12)** *See also* [1PE 1:13](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:13); [1JN 3:2](https://ref.ly/1John3:2)

--------------------------------------------

### Repentance

**[ACT 2:38](https://ref.ly/Acts2:38)** *See also* [MAT 4:17](https://ref.ly/Matt4:17); [ACT 3:19](https://ref.ly/Acts3:19), [ACT 26:20](https://ref.ly/Acts26:20); [2CO 7:10](https://ref.ly/2Cor7:10)

### Faith

**[ROM 10:17](https://ref.ly/Rom10:17)** *See also* [ROM 10:8–10:10](https://ref.ly/Rom10:8-Rom10:10), [ROM 10:14–10:15](https://ref.ly/Rom10:14-Rom10:15); [1CO 2:4–2:5](https://ref.ly/1Cor2:4-1Cor2:5)

## 1448: signs (id: 1448)

Miraculous or supernatural confirmations of the existence and power of God or the miraculous demonstration of spiritual authority on the part of an individual.

* **Associated Articles:** 1449: signs, purposes of (ID: `1449@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1450: signs, kinds of (ID: `1450@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 1449: signs, purposes of (id: 1449)

Signs are given to confirm God's word. They may warn the rebellious or encourage the faithful. People may seek signs as a result of a genuine desire to serve God.

Signs are given to demonstrate God's power
------------------------------------------

**[DEU 34:10–34:12](https://ref.ly/Deut34:10-Deut34:12)** *See also* [DEU 4:34](https://ref.ly/Deut4:34), [DEU 6:21–6:22](https://ref.ly/Deut6:21-Deut6:22), [DEU 7:19](https://ref.ly/Deut7:19), [DEU 26:8](https://ref.ly/Deut26:8); [1CH 16:11–16:12](https://ref.ly/1Chr16:11-1Chr16:12) parallel [PSA 105:4–105:5](https://ref.ly/Ps105:4-Ps105:5); [JER 32:21](https://ref.ly/Jer32:21)

Signs demonstrate the authority of God's servants
-------------------------------------------------

### Moses and Aaron

**[EXO 4:1–4:9](https://ref.ly/Exod4:1-Exod4:9)** *See also* [EXO 4:30–4:31](https://ref.ly/Exod4:30-Exod4:31), [EXO 7:8–7:12](https://ref.ly/Exod7:8-Exod7:12); [NUM 17:1–17:9](https://ref.ly/Num17:1-Num17:9); [ACT 7:36](https://ref.ly/Acts7:36)

[1KI 18:36–18:38](https://ref.ly/1Kgs18:36-1Kgs18:38)

### Elisha

[2KI 2:13–2:14](https://ref.ly/2Kgs2:13-2Kgs2:14)

**[ACT 2:22](https://ref.ly/Acts2:22)** *See also* [JHN 2:23](https://ref.ly/John2:23), [JHN 3:2](https://ref.ly/John3:2), [JHN 7:21](https://ref.ly/John7:21), [JHN 20:30](https://ref.ly/John20:30)

### The apostles

**[2CO 12:12](https://ref.ly/2Cor12:12)** *See also* [ACT 2:43](https://ref.ly/Acts2:43), [ACT 5:12](https://ref.ly/Acts5:12), [ACT 15:12](https://ref.ly/Acts15:12)

### Signs may accompany the preaching of the gospel

**[HEB 2:3–2:4](https://ref.ly/Heb2:3-Heb2:4)** *See also* [MRK 16:20](https://ref.ly/Mark16:20); [ACT 8:6](https://ref.ly/Acts8:6), [ACT 14:3](https://ref.ly/Acts14:3)

---------------------------------------------

### By encouraging the fearful and doubting

**[ISA 38:7–38:8](https://ref.ly/Isa38:7-Isa38:8)** parallels [2KI 20:8–20:11](https://ref.ly/2Kgs20:8-2Kgs20:11), [2CH 32:24](https://ref.ly/2Chr32:24) *See also* [DEU 7:17–7:19](https://ref.ly/Deut7:17-Deut7:19); [JDG 6:36–6:40](https://ref.ly/Judg6:36-Judg6:40); [2KI 6:15–6:17](https://ref.ly/2Kgs6:15-2Kgs6:17)

## 1450: signs, kinds of (id: 1450)

Signs are miraculous events, supernatural phenomena or everyday things that are given a special significance. The term is used in John's Gospel to describe the miracles of Jesus Christ.

Miraculous signs
----------------

**[2CO 12:12](https://ref.ly/2Cor12:12)** *See also* [EXO 10:1](https://ref.ly/Exod10:1); [PSA 78:43](https://ref.ly/Ps78:43), [PSA 105:27](https://ref.ly/Ps105:27); [MAT 24:24](https://ref.ly/Matt24:24) parallel [MRK 13:22](https://ref.ly/Mark13:22); [MRK 16:17](https://ref.ly/Mark16:17); [ACT 2:43](https://ref.ly/Acts2:43); [ROM 15:19](https://ref.ly/Rom15:19)

The signs of Jesus Christ in John's Gospel
------------------------------------------

**[JHN 2:11](https://ref.ly/John2:11)** *John refers to the miracles of Jesus Christ as “signs” in order to bring out the significance of these deeds.* *See also* [JHN 6:26](https://ref.ly/John6:26) *Jesus Christ, the bread of life*; [JHN 9:16](https://ref.ly/John9:16) *Jesus Christ, the light of the world*; [JHN 11:47](https://ref.ly/John11:47) *Jesus Christ, the resurrection and the life*

Jesus Christ refers to Jonah as a sign
--------------------------------------

[MAT 12:39–12:41](https://ref.ly/Matt12:39-Matt12:41) parallel [LUK 11:29–11:32](https://ref.ly/Luke11:29-Luke11:32)

---------------

## 1454: theophany (id: 1454)

A temporary visible manifestation of the presence and glory of God. This may be in natural phenomena such as cloud or fire, in human form or in prophetic visionary experience.

God is manifested in nature
---------------------------

### God's presence in storms, thunder and lightning

**[PSA 18:7–18:15](https://ref.ly/Ps18:7-Ps18:15)**; **[EXO 19:16](https://ref.ly/Exod19:16)** *See also* [EXO 20:18](https://ref.ly/Exod20:18); [JOB 37:5](https://ref.ly/Job37:5); [PSA 29:3–29:9](https://ref.ly/Ps29:3-Ps29:9), [PSA 77:18](https://ref.ly/Ps77:18), [PSA 97:4](https://ref.ly/Ps97:4); [ISA 30:27–30:33](https://ref.ly/Isa30:27-Isa30:33); [AMO 1:2](https://ref.ly/Amos1:2); [HAB 3:11](https://ref.ly/Hab3:11); [ZEC 9:14](https://ref.ly/Zech9:14); [REV 11:19](https://ref.ly/Rev11:19)

### God's presence in volcanic phenomena

**[EXO 19:18](https://ref.ly/Exod19:18)** *See also* [ISA 30:33](https://ref.ly/Isa30:33)

### God's presence in earthquakes

**[ISA 29:5–29:6](https://ref.ly/Isa29:5-Isa29:6)** *See also* [JDG 5:4–5:5](https://ref.ly/Judg5:4-Judg5:5); [PSA 77:18](https://ref.ly/Ps77:18); [HAB 3:6](https://ref.ly/Hab3:6)

Specific phenomena associated with the presence of God
------------------------------------------------------

### Fire signifies God's presence

**[EXO 3:2](https://ref.ly/Exod3:2)** *Fire in particular represents the purity, holiness and unapproachability of God.* *See also* [EXO 13:21](https://ref.ly/Exod13:21), [EXO 19:18](https://ref.ly/Exod19:18), [EXO 24:17](https://ref.ly/Exod24:17); [LEV 9:24](https://ref.ly/Lev9:24); [NUM 14:14](https://ref.ly/Num14:14); [DEU 4:11–4:12](https://ref.ly/Deut4:11-Deut4:12), [DEU 5:4](https://ref.ly/Deut5:4), [DEU 5:22–5:26](https://ref.ly/Deut5:22-Deut5:26); [JDG 13:20–13:22](https://ref.ly/Judg13:20-Judg13:22); [PSA 97:3](https://ref.ly/Ps97:3); [JOL 2:30](https://ref.ly/Joel2:30)

### Smoke signifies God's presence

**[EXO 19:18](https://ref.ly/Exod19:18)** *See also* [EXO 20:18](https://ref.ly/Exod20:18); [PSA 144:5](https://ref.ly/Ps144:5); [ISA 6:4](https://ref.ly/Isa6:4), [ISA 30:27](https://ref.ly/Isa30:27); [JOL 2:30](https://ref.ly/Joel2:30); [REV 15:8](https://ref.ly/Rev15:8)

### Cloud signifies God's presence

**[EXO 16:10](https://ref.ly/Exod16:10)** *Cloud and smoke convey the mystery and transcendence of God.* *See also* [EXO 13:21](https://ref.ly/Exod13:21)EXO [19:9](https://ref.ly/Exod19:9), [EXO 24:15–24:16](https://ref.ly/Exod24:15-Exod24:16), [EXO 33:9](https://ref.ly/Exod33:9), [EXO 34:5](https://ref.ly/Exod34:5); [DEU 31:15](https://ref.ly/Deut31:15)[LEV 16:2](https://ref.ly/Lev16:2); [NUM 9:15–9:22](https://ref.ly/Num9:15-Num9:22), [NUM 14:14](https://ref.ly/Num14:14); [1KI 8:10–8:11](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:10-1Kgs8:11); [EZK 1:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek1:4), [EZK 10:3–10:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek10:3-Ezek10:4)MAT [17:5](https://ref.ly/Ezek17:5) parallels [MRK 9:7](https://ref.ly/Mark9:7), [LUK 9:34–9:35](https://ref.ly/Luke9:34-Luke9:35)[REV 14:14–14:16](https://ref.ly/Rev14:14-Rev14:16)

God is manifested in human or angelic form
------------------------------------------

**[GEN 16:7–16:13](https://ref.ly/Gen16:7-Gen16:13)** *See also* [GEN 18:1–18:22](https://ref.ly/Gen18:1-Gen18:22), [GEN 32:24–32:30](https://ref.ly/Gen32:24-Gen32:30); [JOS 5:13–5:15](https://ref.ly/Josh5:13-Josh5:15)

God appears in prophetic visions
--------------------------------

### God appears on a throne

## 1457: trance (id: 1457)

An ecstatic state in which people may be aware of God communicating with them; it may cause them to lose control of their actions or to have abnormal strength.

God communicating with people through a trance
----------------------------------------------

### Ezekiel

[EZK 8:1–8:3](https://ref.ly/Ezek8:1-Ezek8:3)

### Peter

[ACT 10:9–10:23](https://ref.ly/Acts10:9-Acts10:23), [ACT 11:4–11:18](https://ref.ly/Acts11:4-Acts11:18)

### Paul

[ACT 22:17–22:21](https://ref.ly/Acts22:17-Acts22:21)

### John

[REV 1:10–1:13](https://ref.ly/Rev1:10-Rev1:13), [REV 4:2](https://ref.ly/Rev4:2), [REV 17:3](https://ref.ly/Rev17:3), [REV 21:10](https://ref.ly/Rev21:10)

## 1460: truth (id: 1460)

Truth in Scripture is more than mere veracity. In the OT it is a moral concept, grounded in the being of God himself, which embodies the ideas of faithfulness and reliability, while in the NT the concept widens to embrace the ideas of reality and completeness.

* **Associated Articles:** 1461: truth, nature of (ID: `1461@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1462: truth, in NT (ID: `1462@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1463: truth, of God (ID: `1463@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 1461: truth, nature of (id: 1461)

God is the essence of truth and this quality should be reflected in the character of his children. Falsehood is condemned in Scripture, particularly in legal contexts, but truth is praised and advocated. God takes pleasure in truth and honesty, which are marks of an upright person.

Truth originates with God
-------------------------

**[PSA 43:3](https://ref.ly/Ps43:3)** *See also* [PSA 25:5](https://ref.ly/Ps25:5), [PSA 26:3](https://ref.ly/Ps26:3), [PSA 86:11](https://ref.ly/Ps86:11); [ISA 65:16](https://ref.ly/Isa65:16); [DAN 9:13](https://ref.ly/Dan9:13)

Truth is an aspect of God's character
-------------------------------------

### It is demonstrated in his faithfulness and reliability

**[NUM 23:19](https://ref.ly/Num23:19)**; **[PSA 33:4](https://ref.ly/Ps33:4)** *See also* [1SA 15:29](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:29); [PSA 31:5](https://ref.ly/Ps31:5), [PSA 40:10–40:11](https://ref.ly/Ps40:10-Ps40:11), [PSA 119:160](https://ref.ly/Ps119:160); [ISA 45:19](https://ref.ly/Isa45:19); [JER 10:10](https://ref.ly/Jer10:10), [JER 42:5](https://ref.ly/Jer42:5); [DAN 10:21](https://ref.ly/Dan10:21); [MIC 7:20](https://ref.ly/Mic7:20)

### It is demonstrated in his justice and mercy

**[PSA 96:13](https://ref.ly/Ps96:13)** *The Hebraic concept of truth embraces the ideas of faithfulness, reliability and justice.* *See also* [PSA 119:30](https://ref.ly/Ps119:30), [PSA 119:43–119:44](https://ref.ly/Ps119:43-Ps119:44), [PSA 119:142](https://ref.ly/Ps119:142), [PSA 119:151](https://ref.ly/Ps119:151)

Amen as a liturgical affirmation of truth
-----------------------------------------

### Of oaths and curses

**[NUM 5:22](https://ref.ly/Num5:22)** *The word “amen” is closely related to the word for “truth” in Hebrew. It constitutes an affirmation of the truth of what has been said and an acceptance of its consequences.* *See also* [DEU 27:15–27:26](https://ref.ly/Deut27:15-Deut27:26); [NEH 5:13](https://ref.ly/Neh5:13); [JER 11:5](https://ref.ly/Jer11:5)

### In general use

**[JER 28:6](https://ref.ly/Jer28:6)** *See also* [1KI 1:32–1:37](https://ref.ly/1Kgs1:32-1Kgs1:37)

## 1462: truth, in NT (id: 1462)

The NT encompasses the Greek idea of truth as reality, as well as the Hebraic concepts of faithfulness and reliability. Jesus Christ is shown as “the Truth” and the apostles present the gospel as “truth”.

Truth as opposed to falsehood and lies
--------------------------------------

**[EPH 4:25](https://ref.ly/Eph4:25)** *See also* [JHN 3:33](https://ref.ly/John3:33), [JHN 4:37](https://ref.ly/John4:37), [JHN 18:23](https://ref.ly/John18:23), [JHN 19:35](https://ref.ly/John19:35); [ACT 7:1](https://ref.ly/Acts7:1), [ACT 21:24](https://ref.ly/Acts21:24), [ACT 24:8](https://ref.ly/Acts24:8), [ACT 26:25](https://ref.ly/Acts26:25); [ROM 1:18](https://ref.ly/Rom1:18), [ROM 9:1](https://ref.ly/Rom9:1); [1CO 15:54](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:54); [2CO 7:14](https://ref.ly/2Cor7:14); [GAL 4:16](https://ref.ly/Gal4:16); [TIT 1:13](https://ref.ly/Titus1:13); [2PE 2:22](https://ref.ly/2Pet2:22); [1JN 2:4](https://ref.ly/1John2:4); [2JN 1:1–1:2](https://ref.ly/2John1:1-2John1:2)

----------------

### The quality of truth

## 1466: vision (id: 1466)

Scripture uses the term to refer to both the physical act of seeing, and also the gift of spiritual insight. All things, physical and spiritual, are seen by God.

God's vision
------------

### God views all life on earth

**[2CH 16:9](https://ref.ly/2Chr16:9)**; **[PSA 11:4](https://ref.ly/Ps11:4)** *See also* [GEN 6:11](https://ref.ly/Gen6:11); [EXO 3:9](https://ref.ly/Exod3:9); [PSA 31:22](https://ref.ly/Ps31:22), [PSA 34:15](https://ref.ly/Ps34:15), [PSA 139:16](https://ref.ly/Ps139:16); [ZEC 4:10](https://ref.ly/Zech4:10)

### God sees the hearts and thoughts of people

**[GEN 6:5](https://ref.ly/Gen6:5)** *See also* [1SA 2:3](https://ref.ly/1Sam2:3); [PSA 139:1–139:4](https://ref.ly/Ps139:1-Ps139:4), [PSA 139:23–139:24](https://ref.ly/Ps139:23-Ps139:24); [PRO 15:11](https://ref.ly/Prov15:11); [JER 20:12](https://ref.ly/Jer20:12); [MAT 6:8](https://ref.ly/Matt6:8), [MAT 6:18](https://ref.ly/Matt6:18); [LUK 16:15](https://ref.ly/Luke16:15); [HEB 4:13](https://ref.ly/Heb4:13); [1JN 3:20](https://ref.ly/1John3:20)

The physical vision of human beings
-----------------------------------

### It is given and can be taken by God

**[EXO 4:11](https://ref.ly/Exod4:11)**; **[PSA 146:8](https://ref.ly/Ps146:8)** *See also* [LEV 26:16](https://ref.ly/Lev26:16); [PRO 29:13](https://ref.ly/Prov29:13); [ACT 9:8–9:9](https://ref.ly/Acts9:8-Acts9:9) parallel [ACT 22:11](https://ref.ly/Acts22:11)

### Jesus Christ restores the sight of the blind

**[LUK 4:18](https://ref.ly/Luke4:18)** *See also* [MAT 9:30](https://ref.ly/Matt9:30); [JHN 9:7](https://ref.ly/John9:7); [ACT 9:17–9:18](https://ref.ly/Acts9:17-Acts9:18) parallel [ACT 22:13](https://ref.ly/Acts22:13)

### Physical sight diminishes with age

[GEN 27:1](https://ref.ly/Gen27:1), [GEN 48:10](https://ref.ly/Gen48:10); ; [1SA 3:2](https://ref.ly/1Sam3:2), [1SA 4:15](https://ref.ly/1Sam4:15); ; [1KI 14:4](https://ref.ly/1Kgs14:4); ; [ECC 12:3](https://ref.ly/Eccl12:3) *[Ecc 12:2–5](https://ref.ly/Eccl12:2-Eccl12:5) is an allegory on ageing. It gives a graphic description of a person's progressive deterioration.*

Physical vision has its dangers
-------------------------------

### It can create fear

[JOB 41:9](https://ref.ly/Job41:9); ; [JOL 2:6](https://ref.ly/Joel2:6); ; [MAT 28:3–28:4](https://ref.ly/Matt28:3-Matt28:4) parallels [MRK 16:5](https://ref.ly/Mark16:5), [LUK 24:4–24:5](https://ref.ly/Luke24:4-Luke24:5); ; [REV 1:17](https://ref.ly/Rev1:17)

### It gives rise to temptation

**[1JN 2:16](https://ref.ly/1John2:16)** *See also* [GEN 3:6](https://ref.ly/Gen3:6); [JOS 7:21](https://ref.ly/Josh7:21); [2SA 11:2–11:4](https://ref.ly/2Sam11:2-2Sam11:4); [JOB 31:1](https://ref.ly/Job31:1); [PSA 119:37](https://ref.ly/Ps119:37); [MAT 5:28–5:29](https://ref.ly/Matt5:28-Matt5:29)

Christians are to live by faith rather than by sight
----------------------------------------------------

**[HEB 11:1](https://ref.ly/Heb11:1)** *See also* [ROM 8:24](https://ref.ly/Rom8:24); [2CO 4:18](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:18), [2CO 5:7](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:7); [HEB 11:27](https://ref.ly/Heb11:27)

Visions of God
--------------

### Examples of those who saw God

## 1469: visions (id: 1469)

Mental pictures used by God to convey messages or reveal future events. They are normally received in private by individuals who are often prophets.

God speaks to individuals in visions
------------------------------------

**[GEN 46:2–46:4](https://ref.ly/Gen46:2-Gen46:4)** *See also* [GEN 15:1](https://ref.ly/Gen15:1); [1SA 3:10–3:15](https://ref.ly/1Sam3:10-1Sam3:15); [ACT 9:10–9:12](https://ref.ly/Acts9:10-Acts9:12), [ACT 10:3–10:6](https://ref.ly/Acts10:3-Acts10:6), [ACT 11:5–11:12](https://ref.ly/Acts11:5-Acts11:12), [ACT 16:9–16:10](https://ref.ly/Acts16:9-Acts16:10), [ACT 18:9–18:10](https://ref.ly/Acts18:9-Acts18:10), [ACT 26:12–26:19](https://ref.ly/Acts26:12-Acts26:19)

Visions may reveal future events
--------------------------------

**[DAN 8:17–8:19](https://ref.ly/Dan8:17-Dan8:19)** *See also* [DAN 7:15–7:18](https://ref.ly/Dan7:15-Dan7:18), [DAN 7:23–7:27](https://ref.ly/Dan7:23-Dan7:27); [AMO 7:7–7:9](https://ref.ly/Amos7:7-Amos7:9); [LUK 1:11–1:22](https://ref.ly/Luke1:11-Luke1:22); [REV 22:6](https://ref.ly/Rev22:6)

-----------------------------------------------

## 1500: God, the Trinity (id: 1500)

* 1510: Trinity, the
* **Associated Articles:** 1510: Trinity, the (ID: `1510@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 1510: Trinity, the (id: 1510)

The characteristically Christian doctrine about God. It declares that there is only one true God; that this God is three persons, the Father, the Son and the Holy Spirit, each of whom is distinct from, yet interrelated with, the others; and that all three persons are fully, equally and eternally divine.

* **Associated Articles:** 1511: Trinity, relationships between the persons (ID: `1511@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1512: Trinity, equality of the persons (ID: `1512@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1513: Trinity, mission of the persons (ID: `1513@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 1511: Trinity, relationships between the persons (id: 1511)

The actual term “the Trinity” is not found in Scripture, but the truths implied in a trinitarian understanding of God are clearly set out. The OT hints at a plurality of persons in the Godhead. The NT affirms that the Son and the Holy Spirit are divine.

There is only one God
---------------------

**[DEU 6:4](https://ref.ly/Deut6:4)** *See also* [ISA 43:10–43:11](https://ref.ly/Isa43:10-Isa43:11), [ISA 44:8](https://ref.ly/Isa44:8); [1TI 1:17](https://ref.ly/1Tim1:17), [1TI 2:5](https://ref.ly/1Tim2:5); [JAS 2:19](https://ref.ly/Jas2:19)

OT indications of plurality in the Godhead
------------------------------------------

### God refers to himself in the plural

**[GEN 1:26](https://ref.ly/Gen1:26)** *See also* [GEN 3:22](https://ref.ly/Gen3:22), [GEN 11:7](https://ref.ly/Gen11:7); [ISA 6:8](https://ref.ly/Isa6:8)

### The angel of the LORD

**[GEN 16:11–16:13](https://ref.ly/Gen16:11-Gen16:13)** *The “angel of the LORD” is identified with, yet distinct from, God.* *See also* [GEN 18:1–18:33](https://ref.ly/Gen18:1-Gen18:33); [EXO 3:2–3:6](https://ref.ly/Exod3:2-Exod3:6); [JDG 13:3–13:22](https://ref.ly/Judg13:3-Judg13:22)

### The word of God

The `word of the LORD'' or`wisdom of God'' is personified and identified with, yet distinct from, God: [PSA 33:4](https://ref.ly/Ps33:4); ; [PRO 8:22–8:31](https://ref.ly/Prov8:22-Prov8:31)

### The Spirit of God

The Spirit of God is God's personal agent: [GEN 1:2](https://ref.ly/Gen1:2); ; [NEH 9:20](https://ref.ly/Neh9:20); ; [JOB 33:4](https://ref.ly/Job33:4); ; [ISA 40:13](https://ref.ly/Isa40:13)

### The Messiah

The Messiah's divine nature is emphasised: [PSA 110:1](https://ref.ly/Ps110:1); ; [ISA 9:6](https://ref.ly/Isa9:6); ; [JER 23:5–23:6](https://ref.ly/Jer23:5-Jer23:6)

### Interchangeable expressions

Word, Spirit (or breath) and LORD are used interchangeably for God: [PSA 33:6](https://ref.ly/Ps33:6); ; [ISA 48:16](https://ref.ly/Isa48:16), [ISA 61:1](https://ref.ly/Isa61:1)

NT trinitarian references
-------------------------

**[MAT 28:19](https://ref.ly/Matt28:19)** *The unity of the three persons is reflected in the singular name.* *See also* [2CO 13:14](https://ref.ly/2Cor13:14); [EPH 4:4–4:6](https://ref.ly/Eph4:4-Eph4:6); [REV 1:4–1:5](https://ref.ly/Rev1:4-Rev1:5)

The unity of the three persons
------------------------------

### The Son is fully united with the Father

**[JHN 10:30](https://ref.ly/John10:30)** *See also* [MRK 9:37](https://ref.ly/Mark9:37) parallel [LUK 9:48](https://ref.ly/Luke9:48); [LUK 10:16](https://ref.ly/Luke10:16); [JHN 10:38](https://ref.ly/John10:38), [JHN 12:44–12:45](https://ref.ly/John12:44-John12:45), [JHN 13:20](https://ref.ly/John13:20), [JHN 14:7](https://ref.ly/John14:7), [JHN 14:9–14:11](https://ref.ly/John14:9-John14:11), [JHN 15:23](https://ref.ly/John15:23)

### The Spirit is identified with God

**[2SA 23:2–23:3](https://ref.ly/2Sam23:2-2Sam23:3)** *See also* [PSA 51:11](https://ref.ly/Ps51:11); [MAT 28:19](https://ref.ly/Matt28:19); [1CO 3:16](https://ref.ly/1Cor3:16)

The three persons are distinct from one another
-----------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ addresses the Father directly

[MAT 11:25–11:26](https://ref.ly/Matt11:25-Matt11:26) parallel [LUK 10:21](https://ref.ly/Luke10:21); ; [MAT 26:39](https://ref.ly/Matt26:39) parallels [MRK 14:36](https://ref.ly/Mark14:36), [LUK 22:42](https://ref.ly/Luke22:42); ; [MAT 26:42](https://ref.ly/Matt26:42), [MAT 27:46](https://ref.ly/Matt27:46) parallel [MRK 15:34](https://ref.ly/Mark15:34); ; [LUK 23:46](https://ref.ly/Luke23:46); ; [JHN 11:41–11:42](https://ref.ly/John11:41-John11:42), [JHN 17:1](https://ref.ly/John17:1)

### The Father speaks to the Son from heaven

[MAT 3:17](https://ref.ly/Matt3:17) parallels [MRK 1:11](https://ref.ly/Mark1:11), [LUK 3:22](https://ref.ly/Luke3:22); ; [MAT 17:5](https://ref.ly/Matt17:5) parallels [MRK 9:7](https://ref.ly/Mark9:7), [LUK 9:35](https://ref.ly/Luke9:35); ; [JHN 12:27–12:28](https://ref.ly/John12:27-John12:28)

### The Spirit speaks to the Father on behalf of believers

[ROM 8:26–8:27](https://ref.ly/Rom8:26-Rom8:27)

### Other examples of the difference between the persons

The relationship between the Father and the Son
-----------------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ is God's unique Son

**[JHN 1:14](https://ref.ly/John1:14)** *The Greek word for “One and Only”, traditionally rendered “only begotten”, is actually used to signify “the only one of its kind”; “unique”.* *See also* [JHN 1:18](https://ref.ly/John1:18), [JHN 3:16](https://ref.ly/John3:16), [JHN 3:18](https://ref.ly/John3:18); [ACT 13:33](https://ref.ly/Acts13:33); [HEB 1:5](https://ref.ly/Heb1:5); [PSA 2:7](https://ref.ly/Ps2:7); [1JN 4:9](https://ref.ly/1John4:9)

### The relationship of Father and Son is unique

**[MAT 11:27](https://ref.ly/Matt11:27)** parallel [LUK 10:22](https://ref.ly/Luke10:22) *See also* [JHN 6:46](https://ref.ly/John6:46), [JHN 7:28–7:29](https://ref.ly/John7:28-John7:29), [JHN 8:55](https://ref.ly/John8:55), [JHN 10:15](https://ref.ly/John10:15), [JHN 17:25](https://ref.ly/John17:25)

### The Father loves the Son

**[JHN 3:35](https://ref.ly/John3:35)** *See also* [JHN 5:20](https://ref.ly/John5:20), [JHN 10:17](https://ref.ly/John10:17), [JHN 15:9](https://ref.ly/John15:9), [JHN 17:24](https://ref.ly/John17:24)

### The Father shares his divine life with the Son

**[COL 2:9](https://ref.ly/Col2:9)** *See also* [JHN 5:26](https://ref.ly/John5:26), [JHN 6:57](https://ref.ly/John6:57); [COL 1:19](https://ref.ly/Col1:19)

### The Father delegates his authority to the Son

**[JHN 5:27](https://ref.ly/John5:27)** *See also* [MAT 28:18](https://ref.ly/Matt28:18); [JHN 3:35](https://ref.ly/John3:35), [JHN 5:21–5:22](https://ref.ly/John5:21-John5:22), [JHN 16:15](https://ref.ly/John16:15); [REV 2:26–2:27](https://ref.ly/Rev2:26-Rev2:27)

**[JHN 14:10–14:11](https://ref.ly/John14:10-John14:11)** *See also* [JHN 10:38](https://ref.ly/John10:38), [JHN 14:20](https://ref.ly/John14:20), [JHN 17:21–17:23](https://ref.ly/John17:21-John17:23)
