## 1512: Trinity, equality of the persons (id: 1512)

The Son and the Holy Spirit are equal to God the Father in eternity, nature and status. Within the Trinity the Father is head, first among equals; the Son and the Holy Spirit do the Father's will, glorifying him and making him known; and the Holy Spirit glorifies and makes known the Son.

The Son is equal with the Father
--------------------------------

**[JHN 5:18](https://ref.ly/John5:18)** *See also* [JHN 5:23](https://ref.ly/John5:23), [JHN 8:16](https://ref.ly/John8:16), [JHN 14:9](https://ref.ly/John14:9), [JHN 17:10](https://ref.ly/John17:10); [PHP 2:6](https://ref.ly/Phil2:6); [COL 2:9](https://ref.ly/Col2:9)**[ROM 1:7](https://ref.ly/Rom1:7)** *The equality of the Son and the Father is often implied in the opening greetings of the NT letters.* *See also* [1CO 1:3](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:3); [GAL 1:3](https://ref.ly/Gal1:3); [EPH 1:2](https://ref.ly/Eph1:2); [1TH 1:1](https://ref.ly/1Thess1:1); [1TI 1:2](https://ref.ly/1Tim1:2); [PHM 1:3](https://ref.ly/Phlm1:3); [2PE 1:2](https://ref.ly/2Pet1:2)**[REV 5:13](https://ref.ly/Rev5:13)** *Doxologies are addressed to the Father and the Son equally or just to the Son.* *See also* [ROM 9:5](https://ref.ly/Rom9:5); [HEB 13:21](https://ref.ly/Heb13:21); [2PE 3:18](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:18); [REV 7:10](https://ref.ly/Rev7:10)

The Holy Spirit is equal with the Father and the Son
----------------------------------------------------

**[2CO 13:14](https://ref.ly/2Cor13:14)** *See also* [MAT 28:19](https://ref.ly/Matt28:19); [1PE 1:2](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:2); [REV 1:4–1:5](https://ref.ly/Rev1:4-Rev1:5)

## 1513: Trinity, mission of the persons (id: 1513)

All three persons of the Trinity co\-operate in God's work of salvation. For this purpose, the Father sends the Son and the Holy Spirit to redeem his people on earth and to live in and among them.

The Son and the Holy Spirit do God's work on earth
--------------------------------------------------

### In the OT, the LORD alone is Saviour

**[ISA 43:11](https://ref.ly/Isa43:11)** *See also* [PSA 19:14](https://ref.ly/Ps19:14), [PSA 78:35](https://ref.ly/Ps78:35); [ISA 43:3](https://ref.ly/Isa43:3), [ISA 49:26](https://ref.ly/Isa49:26), [ISA 60:16](https://ref.ly/Isa60:16); [JER 14:8](https://ref.ly/Jer14:8); [HOS 13:4](https://ref.ly/Hos13:4)

### In the NT, the Son is the Saviour

**[MAT 1:21](https://ref.ly/Matt1:21)** *See also* [LUK 2:11](https://ref.ly/Luke2:11); [JHN 4:42](https://ref.ly/John4:42); [GAL 3:13](https://ref.ly/Gal3:13), [GAL 4:5](https://ref.ly/Gal4:5); [TIT 2:13](https://ref.ly/Titus2:13), [TIT 3:6](https://ref.ly/Titus3:6)

### In the OT, the LORD lives among his people

**[EXO 29:45](https://ref.ly/Exod29:45)** *See also* [PSA 135:21](https://ref.ly/Ps135:21); [ISA 57:15](https://ref.ly/Isa57:15); [EZK 43:7](https://ref.ly/Ezek43:7); [JOL 3:17](https://ref.ly/Joel3:17); [ZEC 2:10–2:11](https://ref.ly/Zech2:10-Zech2:11)

### In the NT, the Spirit lives in the church

**[1CO 3:16](https://ref.ly/1Cor3:16)** *See also* [JHN 14:17](https://ref.ly/John14:17); [ROM 8:9](https://ref.ly/Rom8:9), [ROM 8:11](https://ref.ly/Rom8:11); [2TI 1:14](https://ref.ly/2Tim1:14)

---------------------------------------------

### The Father sends the Son

------------------------------

## 1610: Scripture (id: 1610)

The biblical writings, inspired by the Holy Spirit, have been entrusted to the church to remind it of the central teachings of the gospel, to guard it from error and to enable it to grow into holiness. The church is required to be obedient to Scripture and revere it as the Word of God.

* **Associated Articles:** 1611: Scripture, inspiration and authority of (ID: `1611@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1612: Scripture, and Holy Spirit (ID: `1612@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1613: Scripture, purpose of (ID: `1613@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1614: Scripture, understanding (ID: `1614@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1615: Scripture, sufficiency of (ID: `1615@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 1611: Scripture, inspiration and authority of (id: 1611)

Those writings that are acknowledged to be the word of God to be revered as issuing from him and as having his authority.

Recognition of a body of sacred writings
----------------------------------------

## 1613: Scripture, purpose of (id: 1613)

Scripture has been given by God to lead people to faith and salvation. Through Scripture believers are nurtured in faith and led to spiritual maturity.

Scripture is intended to lead people to salvation
-------------------------------------------------

**[2TI 3:14–3:15](https://ref.ly/2Tim3:14-2Tim3:15)** *See also* [PSA 19:7–19:11](https://ref.ly/Ps19:7-Ps19:11); [JHN 20:30–20:31](https://ref.ly/John20:30-John20:31); [ROM 10:8](https://ref.ly/Rom10:8)

Scripture is intended to lead believers to maturity in faith
------------------------------------------------------------

### By its teaching

**[2TI 3:16](https://ref.ly/2Tim3:16)** *See also* [DEU 6:6–6:9](https://ref.ly/Deut6:6-Deut6:9); [PSA 19:7–19:8](https://ref.ly/Ps19:7-Ps19:8), [PSA 119:9](https://ref.ly/Ps119:9), [PSA 119:130](https://ref.ly/Ps119:130); [COL 3:16](https://ref.ly/Col3:16)

### By its rebuke and correction

**[2TI 3:16](https://ref.ly/2Tim3:16)** *See also* [PSA 19:11–19:13](https://ref.ly/Ps19:11-Ps19:13); [1CO 10:11–10:12](https://ref.ly/1Cor10:11-1Cor10:12); [HEB 4:12–4:13](https://ref.ly/Heb4:12-Heb4:13)

### By training in righteousness

**[2TI 3:16](https://ref.ly/2Tim3:16)** *See also* [DEU 29:29](https://ref.ly/Deut29:29)

### By its illumination

**[PSA 119:105](https://ref.ly/Ps119:105), [PSA 119:130](https://ref.ly/Ps119:130)** *See also* [2PE 1:19](https://ref.ly/2Pet1:19); [1JN 2:8](https://ref.ly/1John2:8)

**[1KI 8:56](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:56)**; **[PSA 119:140](https://ref.ly/Ps119:140)** *See also* [EZK 12:25](https://ref.ly/Ezek12:25); [LUK 24:44](https://ref.ly/Luke24:44); [2CO 1:19–1:22](https://ref.ly/2Cor1:19-2Cor1:22)

Scripture is essential for spiritual growth and maturity
--------------------------------------------------------

**[PSA 1:1–1:3](https://ref.ly/Ps1:1-Ps1:3)** *See also* [MAT 4:4](https://ref.ly/Matt4:4); [JHN 15:5–15:8](https://ref.ly/John15:5-John15:8), [JHN 17:17](https://ref.ly/John17:17); [EPH 6:10–6:17](https://ref.ly/Eph6:10-Eph6:17); [2TI 3:14–3:17](https://ref.ly/2Tim3:14-2Tim3:17)

## 1614: Scripture, understanding (id: 1614)

God intends his word to be understood and has provided the directions and means for understanding it.

Scripture is intended to be clearly understood
----------------------------------------------

### It is accessible to ordinary people

**[PSA 119:130](https://ref.ly/Ps119:130)** *See also* [PSA 19:7](https://ref.ly/Ps19:7)

### Some sections are difficult to understand

**[2PE 3:15–3:16](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:15-2Pet3:16)** *See also* [HEB 5:11](https://ref.ly/Heb5:11)

God has prescribed the way to understand Scripture
--------------------------------------------------

### Through public reading

**[1TI 4:13](https://ref.ly/1Tim4:13)** *See also* [NEH 8:2–8:8](https://ref.ly/Neh8:2-Neh8:8), [NEH 13:1–13:3](https://ref.ly/Neh13:1-Neh13:3)

### Through diligent study

**[2TI 2:15](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:15)** *See also* [DEU 17:18–17:20](https://ref.ly/Deut17:18-Deut17:20); [ACT 17:11](https://ref.ly/Acts17:11)

### Through thoughtful meditation

**[PSA 1:1–1:3](https://ref.ly/Ps1:1-Ps1:3)** *See also* [JOS 1:8](https://ref.ly/Josh1:8); [JOB 23:12](https://ref.ly/Job23:12); [PSA 119:15](https://ref.ly/Ps119:15), [PSA 119:27](https://ref.ly/Ps119:27), [PSA 119:48](https://ref.ly/Ps119:48), [PSA 119:97](https://ref.ly/Ps119:97), [PSA 119:148](https://ref.ly/Ps119:148)

Assistance in understanding through the Holy Spirit
---------------------------------------------------

**[1CO 2:9–2:12](https://ref.ly/1Cor2:9-1Cor2:12)** *See also* [ISA 64:4](https://ref.ly/Isa64:4); [LUK 24:45](https://ref.ly/Luke24:45); [JHN 14:26](https://ref.ly/John14:26), [JHN 16:13](https://ref.ly/John16:13); [1JN 2:27](https://ref.ly/1John2:27)

---------------------------------------------------------

**[NEH 8:2–8:8](https://ref.ly/Neh8:2-Neh8:8)** *See also* [EPH 4:11–4:14](https://ref.ly/Eph4:11-Eph4:14); [1TI 4:11–4:16](https://ref.ly/1Tim4:11-1Tim4:16); [2TI 4:1–4:5](https://ref.ly/2Tim4:1-2Tim4:5)

## 1615: Scripture, sufficiency of (id: 1615)

Scripture is presented as being of itself sufficient for faith and for life.

God's written revelation is sufficient
--------------------------------------

**[DEU 4:1–4:2](https://ref.ly/Deut4:1-Deut4:2)** *See also* [DEU 12:32](https://ref.ly/Deut12:32); [JOS 1:7–1:8](https://ref.ly/Josh1:7-Josh1:8); [PRO 30:5–30:6](https://ref.ly/Prov30:5-Prov30:6); [JER 26:2](https://ref.ly/Jer26:2)

------------------------------------------------------

**[HEB 1:1–1:2](https://ref.ly/Heb1:1-Heb1:2)** *See also* [JHN 12:47–12:50](https://ref.ly/John12:47-John12:50); [EPH 2:20](https://ref.ly/Eph2:20)

## 1620: beatitudes, the (id: 1620)

The blessings pronounced by Jesus Christ in the Sermon on the Mount on those whose lives exhibit particular characteristics or qualities. These contrast sharply with popular values and outlooks.

The poor in spirit
------------------

**[MAT 5:3](https://ref.ly/Matt5:3)** parallel [LUK 6:20](https://ref.ly/Luke6:20) *See also* [PSA 69:32–69:33](https://ref.ly/Ps69:32-Ps69:33); [ISA 61:1](https://ref.ly/Isa61:1); [MAT 23:12](https://ref.ly/Matt23:12); [LUK 18:9–18:14](https://ref.ly/Luke18:9-Luke18:14)

Those who mourn
---------------

**[MAT 5:4](https://ref.ly/Matt5:4)** parallel [LUK 6:21](https://ref.ly/Luke6:21) *See also* [PSA 51:17](https://ref.ly/Ps51:17); [ISA 57:18–57:21](https://ref.ly/Isa57:18-Isa57:21), [ISA 61:1–61:3](https://ref.ly/Isa61:1-Isa61:3); [JER 31:13](https://ref.ly/Jer31:13); [REV 7:17](https://ref.ly/Rev7:17), [REV 21:4](https://ref.ly/Rev21:4)

The meek
--------

**[MAT 5:5](https://ref.ly/Matt5:5)** *See also* [PSA 37:11](https://ref.ly/Ps37:11); [ZEP 3:11–3:12](https://ref.ly/Zeph3:11-Zeph3:12); [MAT 11:29](https://ref.ly/Matt11:29)

------------------------------------

## 1630: Book of the Covenant (id: 1630)

The customary designation given to the code of law in [Ex 20:22–23:33](https://ref.ly/Exod20:22-Exod23:33), but it may also have included the Ten Commandments ([Ex 20:2–17](https://ref.ly/Exod20:2-Exod20:17)).

Moses reads the Book of the Covenant to the Israelites
------------------------------------------------------

**[EXO 24:7](https://ref.ly/Exod24:7)** *See also* [EXO 20:22–23:33](https://ref.ly/Exod20:22-Exod23:33) *The Book of the Covenant is the oldest, extant codification of Israelite law, where human values are constantly elevated over material ones. It can be argued that each section of the code is a further exposition of one of the Ten Commandments, giving specific case laws.*

Josiah reads the rediscovered Book of the Covenant to the people of Judah
-------------------------------------------------------------------------

**[2KI 23:2–23:3](https://ref.ly/2Kgs23:2-2Kgs23:3)** parallel [2CH 34:30–34:31](https://ref.ly/2Chr34:30-2Chr34:31) *See also* [2KI 23:21](https://ref.ly/2Kgs23:21) *This reference to the Book of the Covenant applies either to all or part of the book of Deuteronomy, or to the entire Mosaic Law.*

* **Associated Passages:** Exodus 20:22-23:33; Exodus 20:2-17; Exodus 24:7; 2 Kings 23:2-3; 2 Chronicles 34:30-31; 2 Kings 23:21
* **Associated Articles:** 1345: covenant (ID: `1345@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1640: Book of the Law (ID: `1640@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5375: law (ID: `5375@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 5377: law, Ten Commandments (ID: `5377@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 8466: reformation (ID: `8466@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 1640: Book of the Law (id: 1640)

A documentary form of the Law placed beside the ark of the covenant as a reminder to Israel of her covenant obligation. It was rediscovered and applied during the reign of King Josiah of Judah and read publicly by Ezra after the rebuilding of the walls of Jerusalem.

The Book of the Law was written by Moses
----------------------------------------

**[DEU 31:24–31:26](https://ref.ly/Deut31:24-Deut31:26)** *The book in question could be the material now included as chapters 1–30, although some scholars suggest it might refer to the material now included as chapters 12–26\.* *See also* [DEU 28:58–28:61](https://ref.ly/Deut28:58-Deut28:61), [DEU 29:18–29:21](https://ref.ly/Deut29:18-Deut29:21), [DEU 30:10](https://ref.ly/Deut30:10)

The Book of the Law was passed from Moses to Joshua
---------------------------------------------------

**[JOS 1:7–1:8](https://ref.ly/Josh1:7-Josh1:8)** *See also* [JOS 8:30–8:31](https://ref.ly/Josh8:30-Josh8:31), [JOS 8:34–8:35](https://ref.ly/Josh8:34-Josh8:35), [JOS 23:6](https://ref.ly/Josh23:6), [JOS 24:26](https://ref.ly/Josh24:26)

The Book of the Law during the monarchy
---------------------------------------

[2KI 14:6](https://ref.ly/2Kgs14:6) parallel [2CH 25:4](https://ref.ly/2Chr25:4); ; [2CH 17:9](https://ref.ly/2Chr17:9)

The Book of the Law was rediscovered and applied in Josiah's reign
------------------------------------------------------------------

**[2KI 22:8–22:16](https://ref.ly/2Kgs22:8-2Kgs22:16)** parallel [2CH 34:15–34:24](https://ref.ly/2Chr34:15-2Chr34:24) *A reference to part or all of Deuteronomy or possibly the entire Pentateuch (Genesis to Deuteronomy).*

The Book of the Law was read publicly by Ezra
---------------------------------------------

**[NEH 8:1–8:18](https://ref.ly/Neh8:1-Neh8:18)** *See also* [NEH 9:3](https://ref.ly/Neh9:3)

Paul refers to the Book of the Law
----------------------------------

## 1650: numbers, significance of (id: 1650)

Numbers appear frequently in Scripture and in a variety of contexts. Occasionally they have a special theological significance.

* **Associated Articles:** 1651: numbers, 1-2 (ID: `1651@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1652: numbers, 3-5 (ID: `1652@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1653: numbers, 6-10 (ID: `1653@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1654: numbers, 11-99 (ID: `1654@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1655: numbers, hundreds and thousands (ID: `1655@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1656: numbers, combinations (ID: `1656@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 1657: numbers, fractions (ID: `1657@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 1651: numbers, 1–2 (id: 1651)

The number one is often associated with the uniqueness of God and also with the unity between God and his people. The number two is used in a variety of contexts.

---

## 1652: numbers, 3–5 (id: 1652)

The number three, primarily associated with the doctrine of the Trinity, is also associated with periods of specially significant divine activity (e.g., “on the third day”). Four and five have a variety of associations.

Three
-----

### The Trinity

**[MAT 28:19](https://ref.ly/Matt28:19)** *See also* [JHN 14:26](https://ref.ly/John14:26), [JHN 15:26](https://ref.ly/John15:26); [1CO 12:4–12:6](https://ref.ly/1Cor12:4-1Cor12:6); [1PE 1:2](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:2)

### The triad of faith, hope and love

**[1CO 13:13](https://ref.ly/1Cor13:13)** *See also* [1TH 1:3](https://ref.ly/1Thess1:3)

### Three days

**[GEN 30:36](https://ref.ly/Gen30:36)** *Three days is a common period, often indicating the length of a journey or a period leading to a critical point.* *See also* [GEN 40:12–40:22](https://ref.ly/Gen40:12-Gen40:22); [EXO 3:18](https://ref.ly/Exod3:18), [EXO 10:22](https://ref.ly/Exod10:22); [NUM 10:33](https://ref.ly/Num10:33); [JDG 14:14](https://ref.ly/Judg14:14); [1KI 12:5](https://ref.ly/1Kgs12:5) parallel [2CH 10:5](https://ref.ly/2Chr10:5)

### Jesus Christ was raised after three days

**[LUK 24:46](https://ref.ly/Luke24:46)** *See also* [MAT 16:21](https://ref.ly/Matt16:21) parallels [MRK 8:31](https://ref.ly/Mark8:31), [LUK 9:22](https://ref.ly/Luke9:22); [MAT 17:23](https://ref.ly/Matt17:23) parallel [MRK 9:31](https://ref.ly/Mark9:31); [MAT 20:19](https://ref.ly/Matt20:19) parallels [MRK 10:34](https://ref.ly/Mark10:34), [LUK 18:33](https://ref.ly/Luke18:33); [MAT 27:63–27:64](https://ref.ly/Matt27:63-Matt27:64); [LUK 24:7](https://ref.ly/Luke24:7), [LUK 24:21](https://ref.ly/Luke24:21); [ACT 10:40](https://ref.ly/Acts10:40); [1CO 15:3–15:4](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:3-1Cor15:4)JON [1:17](https://ref.ly/1Cor1:17); [MAT 12:39–12:40](https://ref.ly/Matt12:39-Matt12:40) parallel [LUK 11:29–11:30](https://ref.ly/Luke11:29-Luke11:30); [MAT 16:4](https://ref.ly/Matt16:4)

Job's friends: [JOB 2:11](https://ref.ly/Job2:11), [JOB 32:3](https://ref.ly/Job32:3), [JOB 32:5](https://ref.ly/Job32:5); [MAT 17:1](https://ref.ly/Matt17:1) parallels [MRK 9:2](https://ref.ly/Mark9:2), [LUK 9:28](https://ref.ly/Luke9:28); ; [MAT 26:37](https://ref.ly/Matt26:37) parallel [MRK 14:33](https://ref.ly/Mark14:33); ; [GEN 18:2](https://ref.ly/Gen18:2); ; [EZK 14:14–14:18](https://ref.ly/Ezek14:14-Ezek14:18); ; [DAN 3:23–3:24](https://ref.ly/Dan3:23-Dan3:24); ; [ZEC 11:8](https://ref.ly/Zech11:8); ; [2SA 23:8–23:12](https://ref.ly/2Sam23:8-2Sam23:12) *the Three in David's army*; ; [2SA 23:13–23:23](https://ref.ly/2Sam23:13-2Sam23:23) parallel [1CH 11:15–11:25](https://ref.ly/1Chr11:15-1Chr11:25) *the three mighty men among David's chiefs*

### Three annual festivals

[EXO 23:14](https://ref.ly/Exod23:14), [EXO 23:17](https://ref.ly/Exod23:17), [EXO 34:23–34:24](https://ref.ly/Exod34:23-Exod34:24); ; [DEU 16:16](https://ref.ly/Deut16:16); ; [1KI 9:25](https://ref.ly/1Kgs9:25); ; [2CH 8:13](https://ref.ly/2Chr8:13)

Three and a half
----------------

**[DAN 7:25](https://ref.ly/Dan7:25)** *NIV footnote.* *See also* [DAN 12:7](https://ref.ly/Dan12:7); [REV 11:2](https://ref.ly/Rev11:2), [REV 12:6](https://ref.ly/Rev12:6), [REV 13:5](https://ref.ly/Rev13:5)

Four
----

### Four representing the complete created order

**[REV 7:1](https://ref.ly/Rev7:1)** *This symbol is probably based on the four points of the compass.* *See also* [JER 49:36](https://ref.ly/Jer49:36); [EZK 37:9](https://ref.ly/Ezek37:9); [DAN 7:2](https://ref.ly/Dan7:2); [MAT 24:31](https://ref.ly/Matt24:31) parallel [MRK 13:27](https://ref.ly/Mark13:27)

### Four living creatures

The four living creatures in Ezekiel and Revelation represent the whole animate creation glorifying God: [EZK 1:5–1:10](https://ref.ly/Ezek1:5-Ezek1:10); ; [REV 4:6–4:7](https://ref.ly/Rev4:6-Rev4:7), [REV 5:6](https://ref.ly/Rev5:6), [REV 5:8](https://ref.ly/Rev5:8), [REV 14:3](https://ref.ly/Rev14:3)

### Four kingdoms

Human history before the coming of God's kingdom is spanned by four great human kingdoms, often understood to refer to the empires of Babylon, Persia, Greece and Rome: [DAN 2:39–2:40](https://ref.ly/Dan2:39-Dan2:40), [DAN 7:17](https://ref.ly/Dan7:17)

Five
----

### Fives in Jesus Christ's teaching

[MAT 25:2](https://ref.ly/Matt25:2), [MAT 25:15–25:20](https://ref.ly/Matt25:15-Matt25:20); ; [LUK 12:6](https://ref.ly/Luke12:6), [LUK 12:52](https://ref.ly/Luke12:52), [LUK 14:19](https://ref.ly/Luke14:19), [LUK 16:28](https://ref.ly/Luke16:28), [LUK 19:18–19:19](https://ref.ly/Luke19:18-Luke19:19); ; [JHN 4:18](https://ref.ly/John4:18)

### Five loaves

[1SA 21:3](https://ref.ly/1Sam21:3); ; [MAT 14:17–14:19](https://ref.ly/Matt14:17-Matt14:19) parallels [MRK 6:38–6:41](https://ref.ly/Mark6:38-Mark6:41), [LUK 9:13–9:16](https://ref.ly/Luke9:13-Luke9:16), [JHN 6:8–6:13](https://ref.ly/John6:8-John6:13); ; [MAT 16:9](https://ref.ly/Matt16:9) parallel [MRK 8:19](https://ref.ly/Mark8:19)

* **Associated Passages:** Matthew 28:19; John 14:26; John 15:26; 1 Corinthians 12:4-6; 1 Peter 1:2; 1 Corinthians 13:13; 1 Thessalonians 1:3; Genesis 30:36; Genesis 40:12-22; Exodus 3:18; Exodus 10:22; Numbers 10:33; Judges 14:14; 1 Kings 12:5; 2 Chronicles 10:5; Luke 24:46; Matthew 16:21; Mark 8:31; Luke 9:22; Matthew 17:23; Mark 9:31; Matthew 20:19; Mark 10:34; Luke 18:33; Matthew 27:63-64; Luke 24:7; Luke 24:21; Acts 10:40; 1 Corinthians 15:3-4; 1 Corinthians 1:17; Matthew 12:39-40; Luke 11:29-30; Matthew 16:4; Genesis 6:10; Genesis 7:13; Genesis 9:19; 1 Samuel 2:21; 1 Samuel 31:6; 1 Chronicles 10:6; 2 Samuel 2:18; Job 2:11; Job 32:3; Job 32:5; Matthew 17:1; Mark 9:2; Luke 9:28; Matthew 26:37; Mark 14:33; Genesis 18:2; Ezekiel 14:14-18; Daniel 3:23-24; Zechariah 11:8; 2 Samuel 23:8-12; 2 Samuel 23:13-23; 1 Chronicles 11:15-25; Exodus 23:14; Exodus 23:17; Exodus 34:23-24; Deuteronomy 16:16; 1 Kings 9:25; 2 Chronicles 8:13; Daniel 7:25; Daniel 12:7; Revelation 11:2; Revelation 12:6; Revelation 13:5; Revelation 7:1; Jeremiah 49:36; Ezekiel 37:9; Daniel 7:2; Matthew 24:31; Mark 13:27; Ezekiel 1:5-10; Revelation 4:6-7; Revelation 5:6; Revelation 5:8; Revelation 14:3; Daniel 2:39-40; Daniel 7:17; Matthew 25:2; Matthew 25:15-20; Luke 12:6; Luke 12:52; Luke 14:19; Luke 16:28; Luke 19:18-19; John 4:18; 1 Samuel 21:3; Matthew 14:17-19; Mark 6:38-41; Luke 9:13-16; John 6:8-13; Matthew 16:9; Mark 8:19
* **Associated Articles:** 1510: Trinity, the (ID: `1510@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2351: Jesus Christ, miracles of (ID: `2351@DictionaryBibleThemes`); 2560: Jesus Christ, resurrection of (ID: `2560@DictionaryBibleThemes`)


## 1653: numbers, 6–10 (id: 1653)

The number seven is especially associated with completeness and perfection. The number ten is occasionally used as a symbol of completeness. Other numbers have a variety of associations.

Six
---

### The world was created in six days

**[EXO 20:11](https://ref.ly/Exod20:11)** *See also* [GEN 1:1–1:31](https://ref.ly/Gen1:1-Gen1:31); [EXO 31:17](https://ref.ly/Exod31:17)

### Human work is to be limited to six days a week

[EXO 16:26](https://ref.ly/Exod16:26), [EXO 20:9](https://ref.ly/Exod20:9) parallel [DEU 5:13](https://ref.ly/Deut5:13); ; [EXO 23:12](https://ref.ly/Exod23:12), [EXO 31:15](https://ref.ly/Exod31:15), [EXO 34:21](https://ref.ly/Exod34:21), [EXO 35:2](https://ref.ly/Exod35:2); ; [LEV 23:3](https://ref.ly/Lev23:3); ; [LUK 13:14](https://ref.ly/Luke13:14)

### Other important six\-day periods

[DEU 16:8](https://ref.ly/Deut16:8); ; [JOS 6:3–6:14](https://ref.ly/Josh6:3-Josh6:14); ; [MAT 17:1](https://ref.ly/Matt17:1) parallel [MRK 9:2](https://ref.ly/Mark9:2); ; [JHN 12:1](https://ref.ly/John12:1)

### Human work restricted to six\-year periods

[EXO 21:2](https://ref.ly/Exod21:2), [EXO 23:10](https://ref.ly/Exod23:10); ; [LEV 25:3](https://ref.ly/Lev25:3); ; [DEU 15:12](https://ref.ly/Deut15:12), [DEU 15:18](https://ref.ly/Deut15:18); ; [JER 34:14](https://ref.ly/Jer34:14)

Seven
-----

### The seventh day is a day of rest

**[GEN 2:2–2:3](https://ref.ly/Gen2:2-Gen2:3)** *See also* [EXO 20:10](https://ref.ly/Exod20:10) parallel [DEU 5:14](https://ref.ly/Deut5:14); [EXO 31:15–31:17](https://ref.ly/Exod31:15-Exod31:17), [EXO 35:2–35:3](https://ref.ly/Exod35:2-Exod35:3); [HEB 4:4](https://ref.ly/Heb4:4)

### The seventh year symbolises rest and freedom

**[LEV 25:4](https://ref.ly/Lev25:4)** *See also* [EXO 23:10–23:11](https://ref.ly/Exod23:10-Exod23:11); [LEV 25:2–25:6](https://ref.ly/Lev25:2-Lev25:6); [DEU 15:1](https://ref.ly/Deut15:1), [DEU 15:12](https://ref.ly/Deut15:12); [NEH 10:31](https://ref.ly/Neh10:31)

### Major festivals lasted seven days

Unleavened Bread: [EXO 12:15](https://ref.ly/Exod12:15), [EXO 23:15](https://ref.ly/Exod23:15); ; [LEV 23:6](https://ref.ly/Lev23:6); ; [NUM 28:17](https://ref.ly/Num28:17); ; [DEU 16:8](https://ref.ly/Deut16:8); ; [2CH 30:21](https://ref.ly/2Chr30:21), [2CH 35:17](https://ref.ly/2Chr35:17); ; [EZK 45:21](https://ref.ly/Ezek45:21); [LEV 23:34](https://ref.ly/Lev23:34); ; [NUM 29:12](https://ref.ly/Num29:12); ; [DEU 16:13](https://ref.ly/Deut16:13); [EXO 29:30](https://ref.ly/Exod29:30), [EXO 29:35](https://ref.ly/Exod29:35); ; [LEV 8:33](https://ref.ly/Lev8:33)

### Festivals in the seventh month

## 1654: numbers, 11–99 (id: 1654)

Significant numbers include twelve, often associated with the full number of God's people, and multiples of ten, especially forty and seventy.

Eleven
------

### Eleven sons of Jacob

[GEN 32:22](https://ref.ly/Gen32:22), [GEN 37:9](https://ref.ly/Gen37:9)

### Jesus Christ's eleven disciples

[MAT 28:16](https://ref.ly/Matt28:16); ; [MRK 16:14](https://ref.ly/Mark16:14); ; [LUK 24:9](https://ref.ly/Luke24:9), [LUK 24:33](https://ref.ly/Luke24:33); ; [ACT 1:26](https://ref.ly/Acts1:26), [ACT 2:14](https://ref.ly/Acts2:14)

Twelve
------

### Twelve tribes of Israel

**[GEN 49:28](https://ref.ly/Gen49:28)** *See also* [GEN 35:22–35:26](https://ref.ly/Gen35:22-Gen35:26); [EXO 24:4](https://ref.ly/Exod24:4), [EXO 28:21](https://ref.ly/Exod28:21), [EXO 39:14](https://ref.ly/Exod39:14); [JDG 19:29](https://ref.ly/Judg19:29); [EZR 8:35](https://ref.ly/Ezra8:35); [ACT 26:7](https://ref.ly/Acts26:7)

**[MRK 3:14](https://ref.ly/Mark3:14)** *See also* [MAT 10:1–10:4](https://ref.ly/Matt10:1-Matt10:4), [MAT 19:28](https://ref.ly/Matt19:28); [LUK 9:1](https://ref.ly/Luke9:1), [LUK 22:30](https://ref.ly/Luke22:30); [JHN 6:70–6:71](https://ref.ly/John6:70-John6:71); [ACT 6:2](https://ref.ly/Acts6:2); [1CO 15:5](https://ref.ly/1Cor15:5) *The term “the Twelve” is used here even though only eleven disciples remained at the time referred to.*

Forty
-----

Fifty
-----

### The fiftieth year as the Year of Jubilee

**[LEV 25:10–25:11](https://ref.ly/Lev25:10-Lev25:11)** *The word “jubilee” refers to the liberation of slaves, rather than to a fixed period of time. The number 50 represents the year following seven periods of seven years, i.e., 49 years \+ 1\.*

## 1655: numbers, hundreds and thousands (id: 1655)

The words “hundreds” and, especially, “thousands”, often refer to large quantities in general; they are also used simply in a superlative sense.

Hundreds
--------

### A hundred in Jesus Christ's teaching

**[MAT 13:23](https://ref.ly/Matt13:23)** parallel [MRK 4:20](https://ref.ly/Mark4:20) *See also* [MAT 13:8](https://ref.ly/Matt13:8) parallels [MRK 4:8](https://ref.ly/Mark4:8), [LUK 8:8](https://ref.ly/Luke8:8); [MAT 18:12](https://ref.ly/Matt18:12) parallel [LUK 15:4](https://ref.ly/Luke15:4); [MAT 18:28](https://ref.ly/Matt18:28); [MRK 10:30](https://ref.ly/Mark10:30)

### Abraham becomes a father at 100

[GEN 17:17](https://ref.ly/Gen17:17), [GEN 21:5](https://ref.ly/Gen21:5); ; [ROM 4:19](https://ref.ly/Rom4:19)

### People who lived to over 100

## 1656: numbers, combinations (id: 1656)

Numbers may be combined for making a comparison. When they are combined in such a pattern as “two or three” the emphasis usually falls on the second figure.

Two and three
-------------

### Two or three witnesses

**[DEU 19:15](https://ref.ly/Deut19:15)** *See also* [NUM 35:30](https://ref.ly/Num35:30); [DEU 17:6](https://ref.ly/Deut17:6); [MAT 18:16](https://ref.ly/Matt18:16); [2CO 13:1](https://ref.ly/2Cor13:1); [1TI 5:19](https://ref.ly/1Tim5:19); [HEB 10:28](https://ref.ly/Heb10:28)

**[MAT 18:20](https://ref.ly/Matt18:20)** *See also* [2KI 9:32](https://ref.ly/2Kgs9:32); [ISA 17:6](https://ref.ly/Isa17:6); [HOS 6:2](https://ref.ly/Hos6:2); [1CO 14:27](https://ref.ly/1Cor14:27), [1CO 14:29](https://ref.ly/1Cor14:29)

### Two and three in a climactic pattern

**[ECC 4:12](https://ref.ly/Eccl4:12)** *See also* [PRO 30:15](https://ref.ly/Prov30:15)

---------

### Instructions about God's tithe

**[LEV 27:30–27:32](https://ref.ly/Lev27:30-Lev27:32)** *The term “tithe” is the Old English word for “one tenth”.* *See also* [NUM 18:21](https://ref.ly/Num18:21), [NUM 18:26](https://ref.ly/Num18:26); [DEU 12:6](https://ref.ly/Deut12:6), [DEU 12:11](https://ref.ly/Deut12:11), [DEU 14:22](https://ref.ly/Deut14:22); [NEH 10:38](https://ref.ly/Neh10:38); [AMO 4:4](https://ref.ly/Amos4:4); [MAL 3:8–3:10](https://ref.ly/Mal3:8-Mal3:10)

### The royal tithe

[1SA 8:15](https://ref.ly/1Sam8:15), [1SA 8:17](https://ref.ly/1Sam8:17)

### Examples of the tithe

Abraham: [GEN 14:20](https://ref.ly/Gen14:20); ; [HEB 7:1–7:10](https://ref.ly/Heb7:1-Heb7:10); [GEN 28:22](https://ref.ly/Gen28:22) *Jacob*; [2CH 31:5–31:6](https://ref.ly/2Chr31:5-2Chr31:6), [2CH 31:12](https://ref.ly/2Chr31:12); ; [NEH 10:37](https://ref.ly/Neh10:37); [MAT 23:23](https://ref.ly/Matt23:23) *teachers of the law and Pharisees*

## 1660: Sermon on the Mount (id: 1660)

A collection of Jesus Christ's teaching on the theme of discipleship. It deals with the righteousness required of disciples, the way they are to perform their religious duties, and the blessing and persecution they will know as followers of Christ. It can be seen as a manifesto setting out the nature of life in the kingdom of God.

The setting of the Sermon on the Mount
--------------------------------------

**[MAT 5:1](https://ref.ly/Matt5:1)**; **[LUK 6:17](https://ref.ly/Luke6:17)** *Either Jesus Christ taught similar material in two different locations, as is common in preaching, or else Luke more specifically identifies that he taught on a level place or plateau on the mountainside.*

The teaching of the Sermon on the Mount
---------------------------------------

### The blessings of being in the kingdom

*See also* [MAT 5:3–5:12](https://ref.ly/Matt5:3-Matt5:12) parallel [LUK 6:20–6:23](https://ref.ly/Luke6:20-Luke6:23)

### Jesus Christ's disciples are to have a positive influence on the world

[MAT 5:13–5:16](https://ref.ly/Matt5:13-Matt5:16)

### The relationship between Jesus Christ's message and the law

[MAT 5:17–5:21](https://ref.ly/Matt5:17-Matt5:21)

### Jesus Christ's disciples are to exhibit a new depth of righteousness

**[MAT 5:20](https://ref.ly/Matt5:20)** *See also* [MAT 5:48](https://ref.ly/Matt5:48)

### The righteousness required of Jesus Christ disciples

Not only murder but also anger and broken relationships are wrong: [MAT 5:21–5:24](https://ref.ly/Matt5:21-Matt5:24); ; [EXO 20:13](https://ref.ly/Exod20:13); ; [MAT 5:25–5:26](https://ref.ly/Matt5:25-Matt5:26) parallel [LUK 12:58–12:59](https://ref.ly/Luke12:58-Luke12:59); [MAT 5:27–5:30](https://ref.ly/Matt5:27-Matt5:30); ; [EXO 20:14](https://ref.ly/Exod20:14); [MAT 5:31–5:32](https://ref.ly/Matt5:31-Matt5:32) *faithfulness in marriage is called for*; ; [MAT 5:33–5:37](https://ref.ly/Matt5:33-Matt5:37) *faithfulness in speech is called for*; ; [MAT 5:38–5:48](https://ref.ly/Matt5:38-Matt5:48) *Retaliation must be abandoned, and enemies as well as neighbours must be loved.*

### Jesus Christ's disciples are to seek only God's approval in their religious duties

**[MAT 6:1](https://ref.ly/Matt6:1)**

### How religious duties are to be performed

*See also* [MAT 6:2–6:4](https://ref.ly/Matt6:2-Matt6:4) *Giving to the poor is to be done secretly*; [MAT 6:5–6:8](https://ref.ly/Matt6:5-Matt6:8) *Prayer is not to become a public display*; [MAT 6:16–6:18](https://ref.ly/Matt6:16-Matt6:18) *Fasting is to be done without show.*

### The kingdom is to be valued above material possessions

**[MAT 6:19–6:21](https://ref.ly/Matt6:19-Matt6:21)** *See also* [MAT 6:24–6:34](https://ref.ly/Matt6:24-Matt6:34) parallel [LUK 12:22–12:31](https://ref.ly/Luke12:22-Luke12:31)

### Jesus Christ's disciples are to avoid being judgmental

**[MAT 7:1–7:2](https://ref.ly/Matt7:1-Matt7:2)** *See also* [MAT 7:3–7:5](https://ref.ly/Matt7:3-Matt7:5) parallel [LUK 6:41–6:42](https://ref.ly/Luke6:41-Luke6:42)

### Jesus Christ's disciples should pray, confident of an answer

**[MAT 7:7–7:8](https://ref.ly/Matt7:7-Matt7:8)** parallel [LUK 11:9–11:10](https://ref.ly/Luke11:9-Luke11:10) *See also* [MAT 7:9–7:12](https://ref.ly/Matt7:9-Matt7:12) parallel [LUK 11:11–11:13](https://ref.ly/Luke11:11-Luke11:13)

### A pattern for prayer

[MAT 6:9–6:15](https://ref.ly/Matt6:9-Matt6:15) parallel [LUK 11:2–11:4](https://ref.ly/Luke11:2-Luke11:4)

### True disciples will obey Jesus Christ teaching

**[MAT 7:21](https://ref.ly/Matt7:21)** *See also* [MAT 7:15–7:20](https://ref.ly/Matt7:15-Matt7:20), [MAT 7:24–7:27](https://ref.ly/Matt7:24-Matt7:27) parallel [LUK 6:47–6:49](https://ref.ly/Luke6:47-Luke6:49)

Characteristics of Jesus Christ's teaching in the Sermon on the Mount
---------------------------------------------------------------------

**[MAT 7:28–7:29](https://ref.ly/Matt7:28-Matt7:29)**

## 1670: symbols (id: 1670)

Objects, actions or creatures that have a deeper significance and are so understood by those who see them or use them.

Symbolic objects
----------------

### The rainbow: a symbol of God's covenant

*See also* [GEN 9:13](https://ref.ly/Gen9:13); [EZK 1:28](https://ref.ly/Ezek1:28); [REV 4:3](https://ref.ly/Rev4:3)

### A stairway: a symbol of the way to God

[GEN 28:11–28:13](https://ref.ly/Gen28:11-Gen28:13); ; [JHN 1:51](https://ref.ly/John1:51)

### Thunder, lightning, cloud and smoke: symbols of God's majesty

[EXO 19:16–19:18](https://ref.ly/Exod19:16-Exod19:18), [EXO 24:17](https://ref.ly/Exod24:17); ; [PSA 97:2](https://ref.ly/Ps97:2), [PSA 97:4](https://ref.ly/Ps97:4); ; [REV 4:5](https://ref.ly/Rev4:5), [REV 8:5](https://ref.ly/Rev8:5), [REV 11:19](https://ref.ly/Rev11:19)

### Thunder: a symbol of God's voice

[PSA 29:3](https://ref.ly/Ps29:3), [PSA 68:33](https://ref.ly/Ps68:33)

### Trumpets: a symbol of God speaking

[EXO 19:19](https://ref.ly/Exod19:19); ; [REV 8:6](https://ref.ly/Rev8:6)

### The pillar of cloud and fire: a symbol of guidance

[EXO 13:21](https://ref.ly/Exod13:21)

### A throne: a symbol of God's glory

[ISA 6:1](https://ref.ly/Isa6:1); ; [EZK 1:26](https://ref.ly/Ezek1:26); ; [REV 4:2](https://ref.ly/Rev4:2), [REV 22:3](https://ref.ly/Rev22:3)

[EZK 37:1–37:2](https://ref.ly/Ezek37:1-Ezek37:2), [EZK 37:11](https://ref.ly/Ezek37:11)

[DAN 7:9](https://ref.ly/Dan7:9); ; [REV 1:14](https://ref.ly/Rev1:14)

### The wind: a symbol of the Holy Spirit

[JHN 3:8](https://ref.ly/John3:8); ; [ACT 2:2](https://ref.ly/Acts2:2)

[ACT 2:3](https://ref.ly/Acts2:3)

### Stars and lampstands: symbols of God's ministers

[REV 1:20](https://ref.ly/Rev1:20)

[PSA 38:2](https://ref.ly/Ps38:2), [PSA 120:4](https://ref.ly/Ps120:4)

[PSA 2:9](https://ref.ly/Ps2:9); ; [REV 2:27](https://ref.ly/Rev2:27), [REV 19:15](https://ref.ly/Rev19:15)

### The capstone: a symbol of pre\-eminence

[MAT 21:42](https://ref.ly/Matt21:42) parallels [MRK 12:10–12:11](https://ref.ly/Mark12:10-Mark12:11), [LUK 20:17](https://ref.ly/Luke20:17); ; [PSA 118:22](https://ref.ly/Ps118:22)

### A rock: a symbol of stability

[PSA 18:2](https://ref.ly/Ps18:2), [PSA 40:2](https://ref.ly/Ps40:2)

### The human body: a symbol of interdependence

[1CO 12:27](https://ref.ly/1Cor12:27)

### Grass: a symbol of human frailty

[PSA 90:5–90:6](https://ref.ly/Ps90:5-Ps90:6); ; [1PE 1:24](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:24)

## 1680: types (id: 1680)

An OT institution, person, place or event regarded as anticipating the person of Jesus Christ or some aspect of the Christian faith or life.

OT foreshadowings of Jesus Christ
---------------------------------

**[LUK 24:25–24:27](https://ref.ly/Luke24:25-Luke24:27)** *See also* [LUK 24:44](https://ref.ly/Luke24:44); [1PE 1:10–1:12](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:10-1Pet1:12)

OT institutions as types
------------------------

### The Sabbath: Jesus Christ's finished work

**[HEB 4:3–4:6](https://ref.ly/Heb4:3-Heb4:6)** *See also* [GEN 2:2–2:3](https://ref.ly/Gen2:2-Gen2:3); [HEB 4:9–4:10](https://ref.ly/Heb4:9-Heb4:10)

### Marriage: Jesus Christ's union with his people

**[EPH 5:30–5:32](https://ref.ly/Eph5:30-Eph5:32)** *See also* [GEN 2:22–2:24](https://ref.ly/Gen2:22-Gen2:24) *Adam may be viewed as a figure of Jesus Christ, and Eve, of the church, formed in Christ, loved and united with him*; [PSA 45:10–45:11](https://ref.ly/Ps45:10-Ps45:11); [MAT 9:15](https://ref.ly/Matt9:15), [MAT 25:1](https://ref.ly/Matt25:1); [JHN 3:29](https://ref.ly/John3:29); [EPH 5:25–5:27](https://ref.ly/Eph5:25-Eph5:27); [REV 19:7](https://ref.ly/Rev19:7), [REV 21:2](https://ref.ly/Rev21:2)

### Circumcision: believers' union with Christ

**[COL 2:11](https://ref.ly/Col2:11)** *See also* [GEN 17:9–17:14](https://ref.ly/Gen17:9-Gen17:14); [ROM 2:29](https://ref.ly/Rom2:29); [PHP 3:3](https://ref.ly/Phil3:3)

### The tabernacle: Jesus Christ's coming among his people

**[JHN 1:14](https://ref.ly/John1:14)** *The context shows that “The Word” is Jesus Christ; “made his dwelling” involves the idea of pitching a tent and reflects the tabernacle which was pitched among the Israelites and filled with God's glory; so Christ has pitched his tent among his people and revealed his glory.* *See also* [EXO 25:8](https://ref.ly/Exod25:8), [EXO 40:34–40:35](https://ref.ly/Exod40:34-Exod40:35)

### The tabernacle: the way to God

**[HEB 9:11–9:12](https://ref.ly/Heb9:11-Heb9:12)** *See also* [EXO 25:22](https://ref.ly/Exod25:22), [EXO 30:6](https://ref.ly/Exod30:6), [EXO 30:36](https://ref.ly/Exod30:36); [NUM 17:4](https://ref.ly/Num17:4); [HEB 9:8](https://ref.ly/Heb9:8), [HEB 10:19–10:22](https://ref.ly/Heb10:19-Heb10:22)

### The high priesthood: Jesus Christ as intercessor

**[HEB 7:23–7:28](https://ref.ly/Heb7:23-Heb7:28)** *See also* [EXO 29:1–29:7](https://ref.ly/Exod29:1-Exod29:7); [LEV 16:11–16:17](https://ref.ly/Lev16:11-Lev16:17); [HEB 4:14–4:16](https://ref.ly/Heb4:14-Heb4:16), [HEB 5:1–5:5](https://ref.ly/Heb5:1-Heb5:5) *Jesus Christ, the great high priest, is both human and divine*; [HEB 9:11–9:12](https://ref.ly/Heb9:11-Heb9:12), [HEB 10:11–10:12](https://ref.ly/Heb10:11-Heb10:12) *Note the contrast between the many OT sacrifices and Jesus Christ's once\-for\-all offering of himself.*

### The priesthood: Christian worship and service

**[HEB 13:15–13:16](https://ref.ly/Heb13:15-Heb13:16)** *See also* [EXO 19:6](https://ref.ly/Exod19:6), [EXO 29:8–29:9](https://ref.ly/Exod29:8-Exod29:9); [1PE 2:5](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:5); [REV 1:6](https://ref.ly/Rev1:6)

### Sacrifices: Jesus Christ as substitute

**[ROM 3:25](https://ref.ly/Rom3:25)** *See also* [LEV 4:13–4:15](https://ref.ly/Lev4:13-Lev4:15), [LEV 4:25–4:35](https://ref.ly/Lev4:25-Lev4:35) *Hands laid on the head of the sacrifice symbolised the transfer of guilt and its consequences to another. A perfect animal was required*; [ISA 53:4–53:12](https://ref.ly/Isa53:4-Isa53:12); [MRK 15:25–15:37](https://ref.ly/Mark15:25-Mark15:37); [2CO 5:15](https://ref.ly/2Cor5:15); [GAL 2:20](https://ref.ly/Gal2:20); [1PE 3:18](https://ref.ly/1Pet3:18)

### Sacrifice: believers' consecration

**[ROM 12:1](https://ref.ly/Rom12:1)** *See also* [LEV 1:1–1:9](https://ref.ly/Lev1:1-Lev1:9); [NUM 15:1–15:12](https://ref.ly/Num15:1-Num15:12); [PHP 2:17](https://ref.ly/Phil2:17); [2TI 4:6](https://ref.ly/2Tim4:6)

### The day of atonement: Jesus Christ as sin\-bearer

**[HEB 9:28](https://ref.ly/Heb9:28)** *See also* [LEV 16:1–16:34](https://ref.ly/Lev16:1-Lev16:34); [HEB 9:7](https://ref.ly/Heb9:7)

### Passover: deliverance from judgment

**[1CO 5:7](https://ref.ly/1Cor5:7)** *See also* [EXO 12:1–12:16](https://ref.ly/Exod12:1-Exod12:16); [MAT 26:17](https://ref.ly/Matt26:17) parallels [MRK 14:12](https://ref.ly/Mark14:12), [LUK 22:7](https://ref.ly/Luke22:7); [MAT 26:26–26:29](https://ref.ly/Matt26:26-Matt26:29) parallels [MRK 14:22–14:25](https://ref.ly/Mark14:22-Mark14:25), [LUK 22:14–22:20](https://ref.ly/Luke22:14-Luke22:20); [JHN 1:29](https://ref.ly/John1:29); [1PE 1:18–1:19](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:18-1Pet1:19)

### Redemption: release from sin

**[MAT 20:28](https://ref.ly/Matt20:28)** parallel [MRK 10:45](https://ref.ly/Mark10:45) *“Redemption” and “ransom” both involve buying back that which has been lost.* *See also* [EXO 13:11–13:13](https://ref.ly/Exod13:11-Exod13:13), [EXO 21:28–21:32](https://ref.ly/Exod21:28-Exod21:32); [JOB 19:25](https://ref.ly/Job19:25); [PSA 78:35](https://ref.ly/Ps78:35); [ISA 41:14](https://ref.ly/Isa41:14); [ROM 3:24](https://ref.ly/Rom3:24); [1CO 6:20](https://ref.ly/1Cor6:20)GAL [3:13](https://ref.ly/1Cor3:13), [GAL 4:5](https://ref.ly/Gal4:5)[EPH 1:7](https://ref.ly/Eph1:7) *Blood is the ransom price for the forgiveness of sin*; [1TI 2:6](https://ref.ly/1Tim2:6); [TIT 2:14](https://ref.ly/Titus2:14); [HEB 9:15](https://ref.ly/Heb9:15)

### The temple: the church

**[2CO 6:16](https://ref.ly/2Cor6:16)** *See also* [1KI 6:1](https://ref.ly/1Kgs6:1), [1KI 8:10–8:13](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:10-1Kgs8:13); [1CO 3:16](https://ref.ly/1Cor3:16); [EPH 2:21–2:22](https://ref.ly/Eph2:21-Eph2:22); [1PE 2:5](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:5)

## 1690: word of God (id: 1690)

The utterances of God, especially as revealed in Scripture. This may take the form of commands or promises. The term can also refer to Jesus Christ as the incarnate Word of God.

The word of God revealed as law
-------------------------------

### God has made his commands and requirements known

**[PSA 147:19](https://ref.ly/Ps147:19)** *See also* [EXO 20:1–20:17](https://ref.ly/Exod20:1-Exod20:17), [EXO 24:3](https://ref.ly/Exod24:3), [EXO 34:27–34:28](https://ref.ly/Exod34:27-Exod34:28); [DEU 5:5](https://ref.ly/Deut5:5); [ISA 2:3](https://ref.ly/Isa2:3) parallel [MIC 4:2](https://ref.ly/Mic4:2); [MAT 15:6](https://ref.ly/Matt15:6) parallel [MRK 7:13](https://ref.ly/Mark7:13)

### God's law is to be obeyed

**[DEU 30:14](https://ref.ly/Deut30:14)** *See also* [JOS 23:6](https://ref.ly/Josh23:6); [PSA 119:4](https://ref.ly/Ps119:4); [LUK 8:21](https://ref.ly/Luke8:21), [LUK 11:28](https://ref.ly/Luke11:28); [JAS 1:22–1:23](https://ref.ly/Jas1:22-Jas1:23)

### Examples of disobedience and its consequences

[NUM 15:31](https://ref.ly/Num15:31); ; [1SA 15:23–15:26](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:23-1Sam15:26); ; [2SA 12:9](https://ref.ly/2Sam12:9); ; [1CH 10:13](https://ref.ly/1Chr10:13); ; [2CH 34:21](https://ref.ly/2Chr34:21); ; [ISA 5:24](https://ref.ly/Isa5:24); ; [JER 8:9](https://ref.ly/Jer8:9)

The word of God as prophecy
---------------------------

### The prophets spoke the words of God

**[JER 1:9](https://ref.ly/Jer1:9)**; **[1SA 3:1](https://ref.ly/1Sam3:1)**; **[JER 25:3](https://ref.ly/Jer25:3)** *God's prophetic word came to Israel with varying frequency.* *See also* [1KI 17:24](https://ref.ly/1Kgs17:24); [2KI 24:2](https://ref.ly/2Kgs24:2); [2CH 36:12](https://ref.ly/2Chr36:12), [2CH 36:15](https://ref.ly/2Chr36:15); [ISA 16:13](https://ref.ly/Isa16:13), [ISA 24:3](https://ref.ly/Isa24:3); [JER 7:1](https://ref.ly/Jer7:1), [JER 14:1](https://ref.ly/Jer14:1); [AMO 8:11–8:12](https://ref.ly/Amos8:11-Amos8:12); [MAL 1:1](https://ref.ly/Mal1:1)

### Prophetic introductory formulae

\`\`The word of the LORD came to ...'': [GEN 15:1](https://ref.ly/Gen15:1); ; [1SA 15:10](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:10); ; [2SA 24:11](https://ref.ly/2Sam24:11); ; [1KI 6:11](https://ref.ly/1Kgs6:11); ; [2KI 20:4](https://ref.ly/2Kgs20:4) parallel [ISA 38:4](https://ref.ly/Isa38:4); ; [JER 16:1](https://ref.ly/Jer16:1); ; [EZK 6:1](https://ref.ly/Ezek6:1); ; [JON 1:1](https://ref.ly/Jonah1:1); ; [ZEC 1:1](https://ref.ly/Zech1:1); [1KI 22:19](https://ref.ly/1Kgs22:19); ; [2KI 20:16](https://ref.ly/2Kgs20:16) parallel [ISA 39:5](https://ref.ly/Isa39:5); ; [ISA 1:10](https://ref.ly/Isa1:10); ; [JER 2:4](https://ref.ly/Jer2:4); ; [HOS 4:1](https://ref.ly/Hos4:1); [2SA 7:5](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:5) parallel [1CH 17:4](https://ref.ly/1Chr17:4); ; [2KI 1:6](https://ref.ly/2Kgs1:6); ; [ISA 37:6](https://ref.ly/Isa37:6); ; [JER 2:5](https://ref.ly/Jer2:5); ; [EZK 2:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek2:4); ; [AMO 1:3](https://ref.ly/Amos1:3); ; [HAG 2:11](https://ref.ly/Hag2:11)

### Prophetic predictions fulfilled

**[1KI 12:15](https://ref.ly/1Kgs12:15)** *See also* [1KI 15:29](https://ref.ly/1Kgs15:29), [1KI 16:12](https://ref.ly/1Kgs16:12), [1KI 16:34](https://ref.ly/1Kgs16:34), [1KI 22:38](https://ref.ly/1Kgs22:38); [2KI 1:17](https://ref.ly/2Kgs1:17), [2KI 9:36](https://ref.ly/2Kgs9:36), [2KI 10:17](https://ref.ly/2Kgs10:17), [2KI 14:25](https://ref.ly/2Kgs14:25), [2KI 15:12](https://ref.ly/2Kgs15:12), [2KI 23:16](https://ref.ly/2Kgs23:16); [2CH 36:21–36:22](https://ref.ly/2Chr36:21-2Chr36:22)

### The word \`\`against'' a people, indicating judgment

[ISA 9:8](https://ref.ly/Isa9:8), [ISA 37:22](https://ref.ly/Isa37:22); ; [JER 25:30](https://ref.ly/Jer25:30); ; [AMO 3:1](https://ref.ly/Amos3:1); ; [ZEP 2:5](https://ref.ly/Zeph2:5); ; [ZEC 9:1](https://ref.ly/Zech9:1)

### True prophecy is inspired by God

**[2PE 1:20–1:21](https://ref.ly/2Pet1:20-2Pet1:21)** *See also* [NEH 9:30](https://ref.ly/Neh9:30); [JER 23:16](https://ref.ly/Jer23:16), [JER 23:25–23:26](https://ref.ly/Jer23:25-Jer23:26), [JER 23:30](https://ref.ly/Jer23:30); [EZK 13:1–13:3](https://ref.ly/Ezek13:1-Ezek13:3); [MIC 3:8](https://ref.ly/Mic3:8)

### A true prophet hears from God

[2KI 3:12](https://ref.ly/2Kgs3:12); ; [JER 5:13](https://ref.ly/Jer5:13), [JER 23:18](https://ref.ly/Jer23:18), [JER 27:18](https://ref.ly/Jer27:18)

### The prophetic word is to be heeded

[EXO 9:20–9:21](https://ref.ly/Exod9:20-Exod9:21); ; [JER 6:10](https://ref.ly/Jer6:10), [JER 25:3](https://ref.ly/Jer25:3); ; [ZEC 7:12](https://ref.ly/Zech7:12)

The word of God as Scripture
----------------------------

### Scripture is the written word of God

**[DAN 9:2](https://ref.ly/Dan9:2)** *See also* [ROM 3:2](https://ref.ly/Rom3:2), [ROM 15:4](https://ref.ly/Rom15:4)

### NT writings are classified as Scripture

[1TI 5:18](https://ref.ly/1Tim5:18); ; [2PE 3:16](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:16)

### Scripture is inspired and true

[JHN 10:35](https://ref.ly/John10:35); ; [2TI 3:15](https://ref.ly/2Tim3:15)

### The foundational importance of Scripture

It must not be distorted or changed: [DEU 4:2](https://ref.ly/Deut4:2), [DEU 12:32](https://ref.ly/Deut12:32); ; [PRO 30:6](https://ref.ly/Prov30:6); ; [2CO 2:17](https://ref.ly/2Cor2:17), [2CO 4:2](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:2); ; [2TI 2:15](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:15); ; [REV 22:19](https://ref.ly/Rev22:19); [NEH 8:1–8:8](https://ref.ly/Neh8:1-Neh8:8); ; [1TI 4:13](https://ref.ly/1Tim4:13); [PSA 1:2](https://ref.ly/Ps1:2), [PSA 119:15](https://ref.ly/Ps119:15), [PSA 119:97](https://ref.ly/Ps119:97); [ISA 8:20](https://ref.ly/Isa8:20); ; [ACT 17:11](https://ref.ly/Acts17:11); [MAT 22:29](https://ref.ly/Matt22:29) parallel [MRK 12:24](https://ref.ly/Mark12:24); [ACT 17:2](https://ref.ly/Acts17:2), [ACT 18:28](https://ref.ly/Acts18:28); [1CO 4:6](https://ref.ly/1Cor4:6) *It sets the limit of authoritative doctrine.*

Jesus Christ as the incarnate Word of God
-----------------------------------------

### Jesus Christ is God in the flesh

**[JHN 1:1](https://ref.ly/John1:1)** *See also* [JHN 1:14](https://ref.ly/John1:14), [JHN 12:45](https://ref.ly/John12:45); [COL 1:15](https://ref.ly/Col1:15); [HEB 1:2](https://ref.ly/Heb1:2); [1JN 1:1](https://ref.ly/1John1:1); [REV 19:13](https://ref.ly/Rev19:13)

**[JHN 8:40](https://ref.ly/John8:40)** *See also* [MAT 22:16](https://ref.ly/Matt22:16) parallels [MRK 12:14](https://ref.ly/Mark12:14), [LUK 20:21](https://ref.ly/Luke20:21); [JHN 7:18](https://ref.ly/John7:18)

### Jesus Christ's words have sovereign power

[MAT 8:8](https://ref.ly/Matt8:8) parallel [LUK 7:7](https://ref.ly/Luke7:7); ; [MAT 8:16](https://ref.ly/Matt8:16); ; [HEB 1:3](https://ref.ly/Heb1:3)

The gospel as the word of God
-----------------------------

### It was preached by Jesus Christ

**[MRK 2:2](https://ref.ly/Mark2:2)** *See also* [MAT 13:19–13:23](https://ref.ly/Matt13:19-Matt13:23) parallels [MRK 4:14–4:20](https://ref.ly/Mark4:14-Mark4:20), [LUK 8:11–8:15](https://ref.ly/Luke8:11-Luke8:15); [MRK 4:33](https://ref.ly/Mark4:33); [LUK 4:43](https://ref.ly/Luke4:43) parallel [MRK 1:38](https://ref.ly/Mark1:38); [LUK 5:1](https://ref.ly/Luke5:1)

### It was preached by the first Christians

**[1TH 2:13](https://ref.ly/1Thess2:13)** *See also* [MRK 16:20](https://ref.ly/Mark16:20); [ACT 6:2](https://ref.ly/Acts6:2), [ACT 8:4](https://ref.ly/Acts8:4), [ACT 11:1](https://ref.ly/Acts11:1) *to the Gentiles*; [ACT 13:5](https://ref.ly/Acts13:5) *to the Jews*; [ACT 15:35–15:36](https://ref.ly/Acts15:35-Acts15:36), [ACT 17:13](https://ref.ly/Acts17:13); [1CO 14:36](https://ref.ly/1Cor14:36); [2CO 2:17](https://ref.ly/2Cor2:17), [2CO 4:2](https://ref.ly/2Cor4:2); [PHP 1:14](https://ref.ly/Phil1:14); [COL 1:25](https://ref.ly/Col1:25); [2TI 4:2](https://ref.ly/2Tim4:2)

### It leads to numerical and spiritual growth within the church

[ACT 6:7](https://ref.ly/Acts6:7), [ACT 12:24](https://ref.ly/Acts12:24), [ACT 13:49](https://ref.ly/Acts13:49), [ACT 19:20](https://ref.ly/Acts19:20); ; [COL 1:5–1:6](https://ref.ly/Col1:5-Col1:6); ; [1TH 2:13](https://ref.ly/1Thess2:13) *Paul stresses that the preached word is not merely a verbal message but a dynamic power which achieves things.*

### It must be preached

[ROM 10:14](https://ref.ly/Rom10:14); ; [2TI 4:2](https://ref.ly/2Tim4:2)

Descriptions of God's word
--------------------------

It is true: [PSA 33:4](https://ref.ly/Ps33:4); ; [JHN 17:17](https://ref.ly/John17:17); [2SA 22:31](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:31) parallel [PSA 18:30](https://ref.ly/Ps18:30); ; [PRO 30:5](https://ref.ly/Prov30:5); [1KI 8:56](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:56); ; [2KI 10:10](https://ref.ly/2Kgs10:10); [PSA 103:20](https://ref.ly/Ps103:20) *It is obeyed by angels.*; [PSA 119:89](https://ref.ly/Ps119:89), [PSA 119:152](https://ref.ly/Ps119:152); ; [ISA 40:8](https://ref.ly/Isa40:8); ; [1PE 1:25](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:25); [PSA 119:103](https://ref.ly/Ps119:103) *It is sweet and delightful*; ; [PSA 138:2](https://ref.ly/Ps138:2) *It is exalted above all things*; ; [ISA 45:23](https://ref.ly/Isa45:23) *It is irrevocable*; ; [EPH 6:17](https://ref.ly/Eph6:17) *It is the sword of the Spirit*; ; [2TI 2:9](https://ref.ly/2Tim2:9) *It is not chained*; ; [HEB 4:12](https://ref.ly/Heb4:12) *It is living and active*; ; [1PE 1:23](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:23) *It is living and enduring.*

Comparisons of the word of God with everyday things
---------------------------------------------------

Food: [DEU 8:3](https://ref.ly/Deut8:3); ; [JOB 23:12](https://ref.ly/Job23:12); ; [PSA 119:103](https://ref.ly/Ps119:103); ; [JER 15:16](https://ref.ly/Jer15:16); ; [EZK 2:8](https://ref.ly/Ezek2:8), [EZK 3:1](https://ref.ly/Ezek3:1); ; [1PE 2:2](https://ref.ly/1Pet2:2); [PSA 119:105](https://ref.ly/Ps119:105) *light*; [JER 5:14](https://ref.ly/Jer5:14), [JER 20:9](https://ref.ly/Jer20:9), [JER 23:29](https://ref.ly/Jer23:29); [JER 23:29](https://ref.ly/Jer23:29) *a hammer*; ; [HEB 4:12](https://ref.ly/Heb4:12) *a two\-edged sword*

The word of God has power
-------------------------

### It is active

**[ISA 55:11](https://ref.ly/Isa55:11)** *The Hebrew for “word” can also mean “action” or “deed”. This indicates that God's word is active.*

### It brings about creation

**[PSA 33:6](https://ref.ly/Ps33:6)** *See also* [2PE 3:5](https://ref.ly/2Pet3:5)

### It governs and maintains the created order

**[HEB 1:3](https://ref.ly/Heb1:3)** *See also* [PSA 147:18](https://ref.ly/Ps147:18)

### It gives life

**[DEU 8:3](https://ref.ly/Deut8:3)** *See also* [ISA 55:2–55:3](https://ref.ly/Isa55:2-Isa55:3); [MAT 4:4](https://ref.ly/Matt4:4) parallel [LUK 4:4](https://ref.ly/Luke4:4)

### It consecrates secular things

[1TI 4:5](https://ref.ly/1Tim4:5) *“the word of God and prayer” probably means “scriptural prayer”; i.e., on the basis of scriptural teaching the believer offers thanksgiving and prayer.*

### It restrains from evil

[PSA 17:4](https://ref.ly/Ps17:4), [PSA 119:11](https://ref.ly/Ps119:11)

### It heals and rescues

[PSA 107:20](https://ref.ly/Ps107:20)

### It has power to save

**[JAS 1:21](https://ref.ly/Jas1:21)** *See also* [2TI 3:15](https://ref.ly/2Tim3:15); [1PE 1:23](https://ref.ly/1Pet1:23)

### It brings about the growth of the kingdom of God

[MAT 13:23](https://ref.ly/Matt13:23) parallels [MRK 4:20](https://ref.ly/Mark4:20), [LUK 8:15](https://ref.ly/Luke8:15)

### It builds up the saints

[ACT 20:32](https://ref.ly/Acts20:32)
